# Context Mode Index

Index local project content for later search.

## Instructions

1. Prefer the `ctx_index` MCP tool when it is available.
2. Ask for a path only if the user did not provide one and the current project root is ambiguous.
3. Use `path`, not large inline `content`, so file bytes do not enter the conversation.
4. For repository indexing, pass conservative bounds and a clear source label:

```javascript
ctx_index({
  path: ".",
  source: "project:<name>",
  maxDepth: 5,
  maxFiles: 200
})
```

5. If MCP tools are unavailable, fall back to the CLI:

```bash
context-mode index . --source project:<name>
```

6. Report the indexed source label, file count or section count, and the matching search command:

```javascript
ctx_search({ source: "project:<name>", queries: ["..."] })
```

## Safety

- Do not index dependency directories, build outputs, secrets, or generated artifacts.
- Prefer `--exclude` or `exclude` for project-specific noisy paths.
- For broad repos, ask the user before raising `maxFiles` above 500.

# Test-Harness Recon: `pantheon-sitehealth-emails` at `/workspace`

## 1. Existing test infrastructure — NONE

Confirmed by exhaustive search. There is **zero** test tooling in the repo:

- No `test_*.py`, `*_test.py`, or `conftest.py` anywhere (excluding `.venv`).
- No `tests/` or `test/` directory.
- No `tox.ini`, `noxfile.py`, `Makefile`, `pytest.ini`.
- No `.github/` directory at all → **no CI**.
- `pytest` / any test framework does **not** appear in `pyproject.toml` or `uv.lock`.
- `CLAUDE.md` states outright: "There is no build step and no test suite."
- `README.md` "TO DO" list (lines 177-178) has `* test harness` and `* test suite` as the top two open items — this task is that work, greenfield.

You are building from scratch; nothing to conflict with or reuse.

## 2. Python packaging &amp; dependencies

`/workspace/pyproject.toml` (name `pantheon-sitehealth-emails`, version `0.2.0`):
- `requires-python = "&gt;=3.11"` (README says tested on 3.13 and 3.12; 3.11 untested; 3.10 unsupported. Dev container and README setup both target **3.13**).
- Core deps (exact): `rich`, `SQLAlchemy`, `matplotlib`, `Jinja2`, `dnspython`, `html2text`, `semver`.
- Optional-dependency extras (exact):
  - `mysql = ["mysqlclient"]`
  - `aws = ["boto3", "botocore"]`
  - `cloudflare = ["cloudflare"]`
- Build backend: `setuptools` (`py-modules = []` — nothing is actually packaged as a module; the deliverable is the standalone script).
- **No pytest or any test/dev dependency declared. No `[dependency-groups]`, no `[tool.pytest]`, no dev extra.**
- No `setup.py`, `setup.cfg`, `requirements.txt`, or `requirements-dev.txt` (all absent).
- Lockfile: `uv.lock` present (version 1, revision 3, `requires-python = "&gt;=3.11"`). Dependency management is **uv**. Locked `boto3`/`botocore` = `1.43.39`. Install line used everywhere: `uv pip install .[mysql,aws,cloudflare]` inside an activated `.venv` (managed Python via `uv venv --managed-python --python 3.13`).
- An `egg-info` exists on disk (`pantheon_sitehealth_emails.egg-info/`) but is gitignored.

Note: if you add pytest, the natural spot is a new `[project.optional-dependencies]` `dev`/`test` extra or a uv dependency-group, installed via `uv pip install .[test]` / `uv sync`.

## 3. PHP side

- `/workspace/composer.json`: single require — `"pelago/emogrifier": "^7.2"`.
- `composer.lock` (present on disk but **gitignored** — see §9): resolves `pelago/emogrifier v7.3.0`, plus transitive `sabberworm/php-css-parser v8.7.0` and `symfony/css-selector v7.2.0`.
- `/workspace/inline-styles.php` is tiny and self-contained:
  ```php
  require __DIR__ . '/vendor/autoload.php';
  use Pelago\Emogrifier\CssInliner;
  $infile = $argv[1]; $outfile = $argv[2];
  $html = file_get_contents($infile);
  $visualHtml = CssInliner::fromHtml($html)-&gt;inlineCss()-&gt;render();
  file_put_contents($outfile, $visualHtml);
  ```
  It takes two CLI args (input HTML path, output HTML path), needs `vendor/autoload.php` (so `composer install` must have run — `vendor/` is gitignored), and `php` on PATH. Invoked from the main script as a subprocess during the render step (per CLAUDE.md: the per-site `build/&lt;site&gt;.html` is piped through `inline-styles.php` to inline CSS for email clients). For tests this is an easily isolatable unit: pure stdin-file → stdout-file transform, no network.

## 4. Dev container (`.devcontainer/`)

`Dockerfile` base `node:24-trixie` (Debian trixie). Pre-installed:
- **Node 24.18.0 + npm** (confirmed live: `/usr/local/bin/node`).
- **uv + Python** — uv copied from `ghcr.io/astral-sh/uv:latest`; `UV_CACHE_DIR` and `UV_PYTHON_INSTALL_DIR` point under `/workspace/.venv`. `.venv` is a named Docker volume (`python-venv-...`), and `.bashrc` auto-sources it.
- **PHP + Composer** — apt `php-cli php-zip php-mysql php-curl php-mbstring php-xml php-dev` (distro PHP, i.e. trixie's PHP, likely 8.3/8.4 — note the PHP 8.4/Terminus caveat in §7); Composer copied from `composer/composer:latest-bin`.
- **Terminus** — latest `.phar` from pantheon-systems/terminus into `/usr/local/bin/terminus`.
- **AWS CLI v2** — official installer.
- **mise** — installed via `curl https://mise.run`; `devcontainer.json` runs `mise install` as `postCreateCommand`. BUT there is **no committed mise config** (`.mise.toml`/`mise.toml`/`.config/mise` — none in repo), so `mise install` is effectively a no-op currently.
- Other: `gh`, `git-delta` 0.18.2, Starship, RTK (rtk-ai), CodeGraph (`@colbymchenry/codegraph`), `tui-use`, and **Claude Code** (`@anthropic-ai/claude-code@latest`).
- `default-mysql-client`, `build-essential`, `python3-dev` present (so `mysqlclient` can compile).
- `devcontainer.json`: `remoteUser: node`, caps `NET_ADMIN`/`NET_RAW`, mounts volumes for bash history, `~/.claude`, and `.venv`; passes `CLOUDFLARE_EMAIL`/`CLOUDFLARE_API_KEY` from host env; `postStartCommand: sudo /usr/local/bin/container-start.sh`.
- `container-start.sh` just fixes ownership of `.venv`, `/commandhistory`, `~/.claude` (chown to node). It does **not** run the firewall.

### Firewall / network restrictions (critical for test design)
`init-firewall.sh` sets iptables default policy to **DROP** and only allows an explicit allowlist. Reachable hosts: internal Docker DNS, GitHub (meta IP ranges), `registry.npmjs.org`, `api.anthropic.com`, `sentry.io`, `statsig.com`, `api.toolkit.umgpt.umich.edu`, `toolkit.umgpt.umich.edu`, `developers.cloudflare.com`, `api.cloudflare.com`, and the Anthropic net `160.79.104.0/21`. All other outbound is **REJECTed**.

**Implication for tests:** external services the app actually talks to are NOT on the allowlist — Pantheon/Terminus endpoints, `*.drush.in` (SSH port 2222), `smtp.mail.umich.edu:465`, AWS APIs, PyPI proxy (`pypi.org` is not listed — only npm registry is). So any test reaching real Pantheon/SMTP/AWS/PyPI will be blocked when the firewall is active. **Tests must mock/stub all network I/O** (Terminus subprocess, SMTP, boto3, Cloudflare, DNS). Note the firewall is not auto-run by `container-start.sh`, so it may or may not be active in a given session — do not rely on network either way.

### SSH keys (`.devcontainer/ssh/`)
`ssh/config` defines: `github.com` → `github-ed25519`; `*.drush.in` (Pantheon, port 2222) and Pantheon env hosts → `pantheon-ecdsa256` with `StrictHostKeyChecking no`. Private keys live under `.devcontainer/ssh/keys/` and are **gitignored** (`/.devcontainer/ssh/keys/**`). `terminus/config.yml` sets non-interactive mode (`http_max_retries: 10`, `interactive: false`, `no-interaction: true`); its token cache is gitignored too. `.envrc` sets `AWS_CONFIG_FILE=./aws-config` (direnv).

## 5. `development/` archive convention

`/workspace/development/README.md` + `finalize-session.py` + the `/archive-session` skill (`.claude/skills/archive-session/SKILL.md`) define a committed, per-feature record. One folder per feature: `YYYY-MM-DD-slug/`.

Fixed filenames inside a feature folder:
- `NN-*.prompt.md` — numbered input prompts (`01-design.prompt.md`, `02-implement.prompt.md`, …).
- `SPEC.md` — generated then hand-edited spec/plan (written into the same folder as the initial prompt, per `prompts/new-feature-design.prompt-template.md`).
- `transcript.md` — rendered + **secret-scrubbed** transcript (committed).
- `statistics.md` — auto-generated by `finalize-session.py`; **do not hand-edit**.
- `analytics.md` — optional hand-written narrative.
- Multi-session features suffix files: `transcript-01.md`, `statistics-01.md`, etc.

Two safety rules: (a) transcripts must be scrubbed of secrets (regex redaction in `finalize-session.py`, backed by a manual grep) before commit; (b) raw session JSONL is **never committed** — gitignored. A feature's `development/` folder is committed in the **same commit** as the code it documents.

`finalize-session.py`: renders `transcript.md` from session JSONL, does best-effort labeled-regex secret scrubbing, builds `statistics.md` from token counts in the JSONL. Dollar cost is intentionally NOT computed (no price source; `/usage` output is pasted in via `--usage-capture` and embedded verbatim).

**This task lives in `/workspace/development/2026-07-04-test-harness/`** — it currently contains only `PROMPT.md`. Its output `SPEC.md` must follow this convention (written into that same folder). Existing example to mirror: `development/2026-07-03-archive-session/` (has `transcript.md`, `statistics.md`, `analytics.md`, plus pasted context files).

## 6. Node/JS tooling (headless-browser testing potential)

- **Node 24.18.0 and npm are installed** in the container.
- **No `package.json`** anywhere in the project (excluding `.venv`/`node_modules`).
- **No existing browser automation** — no Playwright or Puppeteer references anywhere in the repo.
- So Playwright/Puppeteer for email-HTML rendering tests is feasible tooling-wise (Node present), but would be net-new, would need `package.json` + install, and browser binary downloads would be **blocked by the firewall** if active (Playwright fetches from `playwright.azureedge.net`/`cdn.playwright.dev`, not on the allowlist). Consider whether HTML-rendering assertions can be done without a real browser.

## 7. `README.md` (currently NOT modified — see note)

Purpose: emails Pantheon site owners traffic/plan reports; a temporary standalone script meant to eventually fold into the ITS Web Hosting portal. GPLv3, © 2025 Regents of the University of Michigan.

First-time setup (lines 40-56): clone → `uv self update` → `uv python install/upgrade --managed-python 3.13` → `uv venv --managed-python --python 3.13` → activate → `uv pip install .[mysql,aws,cloudflare]` → `composer install`. Config is a per-institution `pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml` (symlinked from a private config repo).

**PHP 8.4 warning (line 17):** As of Jan 2025 Pantheon's Terminus does not work with PHP 8.4 — use **PHP 8.3 or earlier**, because the sitehealth script also runs Terminus. (Relevant because the dev container installs distro PHP + Terminus `.phar`; if a test exercises Terminus it inherits this constraint.)

Runtime credentials the app expects (from CLAUDE.md): authenticated `terminus` (Pantheon machine token), ssh-agent holding the Pantheon key, `SMTP_PASSWORD` (U-M Kerberos, `smtp.mail.umich.edu:465`, hardcoded in `smtp_login()`), optional `AWS_*` and `CLOUDFLARE_EMAIL`/`CLOUDFLARE_API_KEY`, and `php`+`composer` on PATH.

Full "TO DO" list (lines 175-221) — top items are `test harness` and `test suite`; also: refactor the ~3,700-line script into plugins/packages, document plugin+config system, SendGrid support, `fqdns.json` from Cloudflare, cache-status/cache-control checks, better secrets handling (Terminus token, SSH key, Kerberos→SendGrid API key in AWS Secrets Manager, Cloudflare read-only token, AWS creds), Pantheon API migration, terraform-infra, `terminus()` → `(output, errors, fatal)` tuple, check Live vs Dev env, env-lock report, daily traffic alerts, move nightly capture to portal, accessibility-score notice, PHP memory in plan recs, Cloudflare cache %, SiteLens security/Cloudflare scores, CSV attach, AI-based recommendations. **No testing guidance beyond the two TODO bullets.**

Note: the task brief said README.md is "modified in git status," but current `git status --short` shows only `.claude/settings.local.json` modified — README.md is clean at time of investigation.

## 8. `docs/` directory

Two end-user docs, both about AWS setup:
- `/workspace/docs/aws-credentials.md` — "Setting up AWS credentials for pantheon-sitehealth-email": set shell variables, create a restricted IAM policy, log in to AWS.
- `/workspace/docs/awscli-login.md` — AWS CLI login.

No testing docs.

## 9. `.gitignore` (`/workspace/.gitignore`)

Ignored (load-bearing for tests — these are working data, not fixtures to commit):
- App data/output: `/pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml`, `/pantheon-sitehealth-emails-config`, `/local.toml`, `/database.db`, `/site_results.json`, `/fqdns.json`, `/news/*.toml`, `/build/`, `/tmp/`, `*.csv`, `*-results.json`.
- Secrets: `/.devcontainer/ssh/keys/**`, `/.devcontainer/terminus/cache/tokens/**`, `.env*`.
- Claude archive: `/development/**/*.raw.txt`, `*.raw.md`, `*.jsonl` (raw JSONL never committed).
- Editor/OS: `.*.swp`, `*~`, `.DS_Store`, `/.idea/`.
- Logs: `logs/`, `*.log`.
- Python: `/venv/`, `/.venv/`, `/pantheon_sitehealth_emails.egg-info/`, `**/__pycache__/`, `*.pyc`.
- PHP: `/vendor/`, and **`composer.lock` is gitignored** (comment: different people run different PHP versions → different resolved deps). This matters: a test that pins PHP-package versions can't rely on a committed lock.

## Key takeaways for the harness design
- Greenfield: add pytest via a new extra/uv group; no config to reconcile.
- The app is one ~3,700-line script (`/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails`, `#!/usr/bin/env python`) plus `script_context.py` (shared globals) and `plugin/` + `check/` packages — the plugin/check hook system and pure helpers (`add_notice`, `add_news_item`, html2text config, plan-recommendation math, config substitution) are the testable seams. Network wrappers (`run_terminus`/`terminus`, `wp`/`drush`, SMTP, boto3, Cloudflare) must be mocked — the firewall blocks their real endpoints.
- `inline-styles.php` is an isolable subprocess unit (PHP + `vendor/` required).
- Output `SPEC.md` goes in `/workspace/development/2026-07-04-test-harness/` following the archive convention; commit it with the code; keep raw JSONL out; scrub transcripts.</result>

## Top-level architecture note
The program is not self-contained: it dynamically imports **plugins** (`plugin/*/__init__.py`) and **checks** (`check/*/__init__.py`) at runtime via `importlib.import_module` (main lines 769-772, 778-781). Several external seams (Cloudflare API, AWS Secrets Manager) live in those plugin modules, not the main script. Shared mutable state lives in `script_context.py` (imported as `sc`): `sc.config`, `sc.options`, `sc.console`, `sc.plugin_context`, `sc.hooks`. That module is the natural place to inject test doubles.

---

## 1. Terminus / WP / Drush wrappers (the #1 subprocess seam)

All Pantheon data flows through **one** subprocess primitive: `run_terminus`. Every higher-level wrapper calls it. Mock `run_terminus` (or `subprocess.Popen`) and you control every Pantheon interaction.

- **`run_terminus(command: list, input_data=None) -&gt; (str, str, bool)`** — line 226. Uses `subprocess.Popen` (line 239), NOT `subprocess.run`, and **no `shell=True`** (argument list form, safe). Pipes: `stdin=PIPE if input_data else None`, `stdout=PIPE`, `stderr=PIPE`, `close_fds=True`. Executes via `p.communicate(input=data, timeout=300)` (line 248) — the 5-minute timeout; `subprocess.TimeoutExpired` handled at 249 (kills process, returns `(out, err, True)`). Prepends `["terminus", "--no-ansi", "--no-interaction", *command]` (line 228). Returns `(output, errors, fatal)`. Wraps the call in a `sc.console.status(...)` spinner (line 238) — that is a `rich` object on `sc`, mockable.
- **`terminus(*args) -&gt; Any`** — line 316. JSON wrapper: appends `--format=json`, calls `run_terminus`, `json.loads(output)` (327). Session-expiry retry at 333-337: on `"Invalid or expired session header: X-Pantheon-Session"` it `time.sleep(5)` and recurses once (guarded by the `pshe-no-retry` sentinel). Note there are latent bugs here (`del args["pshe-no-retry"]` / `args.push(...)` on a tuple) — relevant if you test the retry path. Returns only `result` (the tuple return is TODO-commented at 338).
- **`wp(siteenv, *args) -&gt; (Any, str)`** — line 342. Builds `["wp", siteenv, "--", *args, "--format=json"]` → `run_terminus` → JSON.
- **`wp_eval(siteenv, *args) -&gt; (str, str)`** — line 356. Builds `["wp", siteenv, "--", "eval", *args]`, returns raw stripped string.
- **`drush(siteenv, *args) -&gt; (Any, str)`** — line 413. `["drush", siteenv, "--", *args, "--format=json"]`, post-processed by `fix_drush_output` (line 391) then JSON.
- **`drush_php_script(siteenv, script) -&gt; (Any, str)`** — line 428. `["drush", siteenv, "--", "php:script", "--format=json", "-"]`; passes `script` as `input_data` (stdin) to `run_terminus`.
- **`wp_error(...)`** line 365 / **`drush_error(...)`** line 443 — pure formatters (build notice dicts from error strings), no external call. No mocking needed.

Injectability: excellent. One patch point (`run_terminus`) fakes all of Terminus/WP/Drush. `terminus` also independently patchable for JSON-level fakes.

---

## 2. Pantheon HTTP API — NOT called directly

No `requests` / `httpx` / `urllib.request` / `http.client` anywhere in the main script or plugins. `import urllib.parse` (line 31) is used only for URL *encoding* (`escape_url`, line 222). All Pantheon access is via the `terminus` CLI subprocess. There is **no machine-token→session-token auth flow in code** — auth is delegated entirely to the Terminus binary's own session (the only auth-related logic is the session-expiry *retry* at 333-337). So for tests, Pantheon = the `run_terminus` seam; there is no HTTP client to intercept.

---

## 3. Email sending (SMTP) — currently DISABLED

- **`smtp_login() -&gt; SMTP_SSL`** — line 755. `SMTP_SSL("smtp.mail.umich.edu", port=465)` (757) then `.login(sc.options.smtp_username, os.environ["SMTP_PASSWORD"])` (758). `SMTP_PASSWORD` read from env here — the only hard env read for a credential. Hardcoded host/port (TODO to move to config, line 756).
- Message assembly (lines 3579-3625, inside the per-site loop):
  - `msg = EmailMessage()` (3579); headers From/To/Bcc/Reply-to/Date/Subject (3580-3591). `sc.options.for_real` toggles real recipients vs. dev recipient (3581-3588).
  - `msg.set_content(text_body, subtype="plain")` (3593) + `msg.add_alternative(html_body, subtype="html")` (3594).
  - Inline images via `msg.get_payload()[1].add_related(...)`: banner/wordmark (3596), matplotlib chart (3605), plus a loop over `site_context["attachments"]` (3614-3622). CIDs from `make_msgid(domain="webservices.umich.edu")` at 3505-3506; passed to template as `banner_cid[1:-1]` / `chart_cid[1:-1]` (3535-3536).
  - **Always writes `build/&lt;site&gt;.eml`**: `f.write(msg.as_bytes(policy=SMTP))` (3624-3625) — a filesystem side effect that happens even in tests.
- **DISABLED send block — lines 3627-3631** (verbatim):
  ```
  # TODO: uncomment and also add SendGrid support
  # smtp_connection = smtp_login()
  # smtp_connection.send_message(msg)
  # emails_sent += 1
  # smtp_connection.quit()
  ```
  So no mail is actually transmitted today; the `.eml` on disk is the only output. A matching TODO comment sits at line 845. **SendGrid would plug in exactly here (3627-3631)** as an alternative to `smtp_login()/send_message()`, and/or inside a refactored `smtp_login()`. `smtp_login` is fully injectable (patch it or `SMTP_SSL`), but note tests must still tolerate the unconditional `.eml` write at 3624.

---

## 4. Rendering pipeline (Jinja2 → PHP/Emogrifier → matplotlib)

Per-site, lines ~3505-3625:
- **Jinja2**: `from jinja2 import Template` (line 46). HTML: reads `email_template.html` (3539), `Template(f.read())`, `render(**template_dict)` (3541); writes `build/&lt;site&gt;.html` (3545). Text: reads `email_template.txt` (3548), renders, writes `build/&lt;site&gt;.txt` (3551). Uses the low-level `Template` directly — no `Environment`/loader (so no FS loader to stub; patch `open` or the `Template` class).
- **Emogrifier PHP subprocess**: `subprocess.run(["php", "inline-styles.php", "build/&lt;site&gt;.html", "build/&lt;site&gt;-inline.html"], stdout=sys.stdout, stderr=sys.stderr, check=True)` — lines 3554-3564. This is `subprocess.run` with `check=True` (raises `CalledProcessError`), no shell. `inline-styles.php` (repo root) requires `vendor/autoload.php` and calls `Pelago\Emogrifier\CssInliner::fromHtml(...)-&gt;inlineCss()-&gt;render()` (vendor: `pelago/`, `symfony/`, `sabberworm/`). Reads inlined result back at 3565, post-processes `&lt;style&gt;` blocks to add `!important` (3568-3574), writes `build/&lt;site&gt;-inline2.html` (3576). This is a **second subprocess seam** — separate patch point from `run_terminus`.
- **matplotlib charts** — `matplotlib` imports 39-48; charts built in the per-site loop. Traffic-surge chart uses `GridSpec(2,1,...)` with `ax_surge`/`ax_plan` subplots (lines 2641-2652, surge threshold logic 2626-2636, cap-shape/bars 2752-2811). Rendered to an in-memory PNG: `buf = io.BytesIO(); fig.savefig(buf, format="png"); chart_image = buf.read()` (2946-2949), then `plt.close(fig)` (2951, also 3638). `chart_image` is attached inline (3605). **SiteLens gauge images** live in `check/umich/sitelens.py`: `create_gauge_image(value, color, title) -&gt; bytes` (line 122) uses `plt` pie wedges and returns PNG bytes; produced in `check_sitelens_scores` (line 149, call at 206) and attached via the `site_context["attachments"]` loop. No file writes for charts (in-memory BytesIO) — easily testable with a non-interactive matplotlib backend.
- Also reads **`header-image.png`** (repo root) into memory at 842-843 (`wordmark_image`), attached at 3596.

---

## 5. Database (SQLAlchemy)

- Imports: `import sqlalchemy as db` (45); `from sqlalchemy.dialects.sqlite import insert as sqlite_insert` (60); `DeclarativeBase, Mapped, mapped_column` (61); `CHAR` (62); a bulk import block 51-59.
- Models: `class Base(DeclarativeBase)` (93); **`PantheonTraffic`** (97); **`PantheonOverageProtection`** (120).
- **Engine/session creation — lines 818-836** inside `main()`. Config-driven from `sc.config["Database"]["type"]`:
  - sqlite: `f"sqlite:///{sc.config['Database']['name']}"` (819).
  - mysql: `f"mysql+mysqldb://{user}:{password}@{host}:{port}/{name}"` (822-825) with pool kwargs.
  - `db_engine = db.create_engine(conn_str, echo=&lt;verbose&gt;=2&gt;, **kwargs)` (830); `db_session_factory = db.orm.sessionmaker(bind=db_engine)` (835); `db_session = db_session_factory()` (836). Torn down at 3643-3644 (`db_session.close()`, `db_engine.dispose()`).
- Table creation: `Base.metadata.create_all(db_engine)` under `--create-tables` (838-839, then `sys.exit`).
- Upsert: no helper function — done inline. Traffic uses `db_session.merge(traffic)` (1096) plus dialect-specific bulk inserts: `sqlite_insert(PantheonTraffic).on_conflict_do_nothing(...)` for sqlite (1108-1114, 1124-1130) vs. `insert(PantheonTraffic).prefix_with("IGNORE")` for mysql (1115-1117, 1131-1133), executed via `db_session.execute(...)` + `commit()`. Overage rows use `db_session.get(PantheonOverageProtection, {...})` (2975, 3040, 3114) + `db_session.add(op)` (3050) + `commit()` (3077).
- **Test injection**: the engine URL is built purely from `sc.config["Database"]`. Set config `type="sqlite"`, `name=":memory:"` (or a temp file) before `main()` runs — no code change needed. For finer control, patch `db.create_engine` at 830. Real default DB is `database.db` (repo root, ~5 MB; sample config `name = "database.db"`). Note: sqlite in-memory + a fresh session works, but the code calls `create_all` only under `--create-tables`, so tests must create tables themselves or run that path. Additional model setup exists in `plugin/umich/portal.py:setup_portal_db` (13) and `check/umich/sitelens.py:setup_sitelens` (35).

---

## 6. Config loading

- CLI parsed at import time: `argparse.ArgumentParser` (142), `sc.options = args_parser.parse_args()` (219). Options: positional `sites`; `--all/-a` (dest `all`), `--date/-d`, `--update`, `--for-real` (dest `for_real`), `--config/-c` (default `"pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml"`), `--only-warn`, `--smtp-username/-u` (default `os.environ.get("USER","")`, line 196), `--create-tables`, `--import-older-metrics`, `--verbose/-v` (count).
- TOML: `import tomllib` (30). Main config loaded in `main()`: `with open(sc.options.config, "rb") as f: sc.config = tomllib.load(f)` (765-766). Two config-substitution passes: `process_config(sc.config)` at 775 and 806. News TOMLs also loaded via `glob.glob(f"{sc.config['News']['folder']}/*.toml")` + `tomllib.load` (857-859).
- The active `pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml` is a **symlink** → `pantheon-sitehealth-emails-config/pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml` (a private repo); `local.toml` → `sample-pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml`. Template sections: `[Pantheon]`, `[Pantheon.plan_info.*]`, `[Pantheon.plan_sku_to_name]`, `[Database]` (default `type="sqlite"`, `name="database.db"`), `[Cloudflare]`, `[AWS]` (`profile="webhosting"`), `[News]` (`folder="./news"`). Tests can just point `--config` / `sc.options.config` at a fixture TOML.
- **Environment variables** are read in scattered places, mostly in plugins:
  - `SMTP_PASSWORD` — `os.environ["SMTP_PASSWORD"]`, main line 758 (in `smtp_login`, currently only called from the disabled block).
  - `USER` — `os.environ.get("USER","")`, line 196 (argparse default).
  - `CLOUDFLARE_EMAIL`, `CLOUDFLARE_API_KEY` — `plugin/cloudflare/__init__.py` lines 9-12 (override `sc.config['Cloudflare']['member_email'/'member_api_key']`).
  - `AWS_PROFILE`, `AWS_DEFAULT_REGION` — `plugin/aws/__init__.py` lines 10-13 (set into env from config for boto).
  There are **no `AWS_*` secret-value reads** in code — AWS creds come from the boto profile / SDK chain (see §7). No `CLOUDFLARE_*` beyond the two above.

---

## 7. Other network calls, credential reads, filesystem writes

**Network (beyond Terminus subprocess):**
- **DNS resolution** — `import dns.resolver` (38); live `dns.resolver.resolve(hostname, "A")` (1218) and `"AAAA"` (1248) inside the FQDN/Cloudflare check loop, with handlers for NoAnswer/NXDOMAIN/NoNameservers/Timeout (1238-1274). This is a real network seam in the main script; patch `dns.resolver.resolve`.
- **Cloudflare API** — `plugin/cloudflare/ips.py`: `from cloudflare import Cloudflare` (5); constructs client with `api_email`/`api_key` from config (15-18) and calls `cloudflare.ips.list()` (22) in a `setup` hook to fetch CF IP CIDR ranges. Only active when `[Cloudflare].enabled` is true. Patch the `Cloudflare` client or disable the plugin in test config.
- **AWS Secrets Manager** — `plugin/aws/get_secret.py`: `import boto3` (5); `get_secret(secret_name, ...)` (16) builds `boto3.session.Session(...)` (25/27/29), `session.client("secretsmanager")` (32/34), `client.get_secret_value(SecretId=...)` (38). Registered as a `get_secret` hook (`plugin/aws/__init__.py` 15-18). Network + credential seam; patch boto3 or the `get_secret` hook. `aws-config` file exists at repo root.
- No other HTTP clients. `plugin/umich/portal.py` and `check/umich/sitelens.py` are DB/matplotlib only (their `https://...umich.edu` strings are just link text in email bodies, not requests).

**Credential reads:** `SMTP_PASSWORD` (env, 758); Cloudflare `member_api_key` (config/env, cloudflare plugin); AWS via boto profile chain (no literal secret in code); mysql `password` from `sc.config['Database']['password']` (823).

**Filesystem writes/reads (side effects to stub or sandbox in tests):**
- Creates `build/` dir: `os.makedirs("build")` if missing (800-801).
- Writes per site: `build/&lt;site&gt;.html` (3545), `.txt` (3551), `-inline.html` (produced by PHP, 3559), `-inline2.html` (3576), **`.eml`** (3624). The `build/` dir already holds ~1580 entries.
- Reads: `sc.options.config` TOML (765), news `*.toml` (858), `email_template.html`/`.txt` (3539/3548), `header-image.png` (842), and **`fqdns.json`** — resolved through a symlink and staleness-checked: `os.path.islink`/`os.readlink` (1174-1175), `os.path.getmtime` &gt;86400s aborts under `--all` (1176-1184), then `json.load` (1184-1185). `fqdns.json` (~148 KB) lives at repo root.
- DB file `database.db` (sqlite, repo root) via the engine (§5).

| Seam | Best mock target | File:line |
|---|---|---|

| Unconditional FS writes | `build/*.{html,txt,eml}`, needs temp cwd | main:3545-3624 |

Two independent subprocess seams (`run_terminus` via `Popen`, and the Emogrifier `php` via `subprocess.run`), no direct HTTP to Pantheon, and three genuinely external network dependencies outside Terminus: DNS, Cloudflare SDK, and boto3/Secrets Manager (the latter two only when their plugins are enabled in config).</result>

# Structural Map: `pantheon-sitehealth-emails`

**Files:** main script `/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails` (3674 lines, no `.py` extension, shebang `#!/usr/bin/env python`), shared-state module `/workspace/script_context.py` (93 lines, imported everywhere as `sc`), plus `plugin/` and `check/` packages.

## Module-load order (import-time execution) — testing seam #1

The script executes top-to-bottom at import. Nothing is lazy:

1. **Lines 1–90** – imports (`argparse`, `subprocess`, `smtplib.SMTP_SSL`, `email.*`, `matplotlib`, `numpy`, SQLAlchemy as `db`, `tomllib`, `rich`, `import script_context as sc`, etc.). `matplotlib` is imported at module scope.
2. **Lines 93–135** – SQLAlchemy ORM model classes (run at import): `class Base` (93), `class PantheonTraffic(Base)` (97), `class PantheonOverageProtection(Base)` (120), each with a `__repr__` (113, 133).
3. **Lines 141–219** – **argparse at module scope**, exactly as CLAUDE.md claims. Verbatim confirmation:
   - `142  args_parser = argparse.ArgumentParser(`
   - `147  args_parser.add_argument("sites", ...)` … through line 218
   - `219  sc.options = args_parser.parse_args()`
   
   The comment on line 141 states the intent: *"Parse command line arguments. This is outside main() so the arguments are available to all functions."* **Consequence for tests:** any `import` of this script immediately calls `parse_args()` against the live `sys.argv` and populates the global `sc.options`. You cannot import the module without argv side effects, and because the file has no `.py` extension you must load it via `importlib.util.spec_from_file_location` / SourceFileLoader anyway.
4. **Lines 222–760** – all free function `def`s are defined (not run).
5. **Lines 3672–3673** – `if __name__ == "__main__": main()`.

**There is no `argparse` mutually-exclusive group.** Mutual exclusivity is enforced *imperatively inside `main()`* (see below), not by argparse.

## 1. Command-line options (all defined lines 147–218)

| Flag | Line | action / type | Default | Effect |
|---|---|---|---|---|
| `sites` (positional `SITE`, `nargs="*"`) | 147 | list | `[]` | Explicit site names to process |
| `--all` / `-a` | 153 | store_true | False | Process all org sites |
| `--date` / `-d` | 160 | `datetime.date.fromisoformat` | today | Report "as of" date (should be last day of month) |
| `--update` | 167 | store_true | False | Only refresh visitor counts in DB; skip reports |
| `--for-real` | 173 | store_true | False | Send to owners; **without it all mail is redirected to the logged-in user** (primary safety mechanism) |
| `--config` / `-c` | 179 | store | `pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml` | TOML config path |
| `--only-warn` | 186 | store_true | False | Only check for warnings; no reports/email |
| `--smtp-username` / `-u` | 192 | store | `$USER` | SMTP login user |
| `--create-tables` | 199 | store_true | False | Create DB tables and exit, ignoring other options |
| `--import-older-metrics` | 205 | store_true | False | Backfill weekly/monthly Pantheon aggregates and exit |
| `--verbose` / `-v` | 212 | count | 0 | `-v`/`-vv`/`-vvv` verbosity |

**Mutual-exclusivity / validation logic (in `main()`, lines 784–793):**
- `--create-tables` + `--import-older-metrics` → `sys.exit(...)` "mutually exclusive" (line 786).
- `--create-tables` forces `sc.options.verbose = 3` (line 789).
- **`--all` vs `SITE` list:** `sys.exit("You must specify either at least one site or the --all option.")` when `(--all AND sites non-empty) OR (not --all AND sites empty)` (lines 790–793). Note this XOR check is *skipped* when `--create-tables` is set (it's the `elif` branch).

## 2. `main()` control flow (762 → 3669)

**Setup phase (762–917):**
- 765–766: `open(config)` → `tomllib.load` into `sc.config` (filesystem read).
- 769–772: load `plugin.*` modules via `find_modules("plugin")` + `importlib.import_module` → `sc.plugin[...]`.
- 775: **`process_config(sc.config)` — first pass** (pre-setup substitutions).
- 778–781: load `check.*` modules → `sc.check[...]`.
- 784–793: option validation / mutual-exclusivity (above).
- 797: `pprint(terminus("self:info"))` if verbose (network).
- 800–801: `os.makedirs("build")` if missing (filesystem write).
- 803: **`sc.invoke_hooks("setup")`** — runs all registered setup hooks (DB connect, Cloudflare IP fetch, portal DB).
- 806: **`process_config(sc.config)` — second pass** (post-setup; so hooks can populate data later substitutions consume). Confirms the CLAUDE.md "run twice" claim.
- 818–836: build SQLAlchemy engine (`sqlite:///` or `mysql+mysqldb://`) and session. Unsupported type → `sys.exit` (828).
- **`--create-tables` terminal branch (838–840):** `Base.metadata.create_all(db_engine)` then `sys.exit("Tables created.")`.
- 842–843: read `header-image.png` bytes.
- 849–868: load news items from `[News]` config section and from `*.toml` in `[News].folder` → `sc.add_news_item(...)`.
- 870–882: normalize `[Pantheon].plan_info` (`"-"`→`None` for upgrade/downgrade), alias `plan_info`, `plan_names`.
- 884–902: compute `start_date`/`end_date`, `end_of_contract_year`, and matplotlib "cap" polygon geometry.
- 904: `sites = terminus("org:site:list", org_id)` (network). Build `site_name_to_id` (916).

**Per-site loop (919 → 3641)** — iterates `sorted(site_name_to_id)`:
- 927–939: skip filters (e.g. `if not --all and name not in options.sites: continue`).
- 956–1015: plan-based early handling (Elite/Sandbox/frozen/unknown plan).
- 1032–1038: skip if no initialized `live` env.
- 1070–1098: preload + `db_session.merge(traffic)` + `commit` (current-period traffic upsert).
- **`--import-older-metrics` branch (1100–1137):** calls `get_old_metrics(..., "week"/"month", ...)`, bulk `db_session.execute(insert … on_conflict_do_nothing / IGNORE)`, commit, then `continue` (skips report).
- **`--update` branch (1139–1141):** prints "skipping report", `continue`.
- 1144–1151: `db_session.query(PantheonTraffic)` for the reporting window.
- **1161–1166: `site_context` built** — dict with keys `site`, `notices` (seeded from `site_notices`), `sections` (empty list), `attachments` (empty list).
- **1167: `sc.invoke_hooks("check", site_context)`** — the only per-site check-hook invocation.
- 1174–1494: Cloudflare/DNS FQDN checks (reads `fqdns.json`, may fetch DNS), builds notices.
- **1494–2139: WordPress branch** (`framework.startswith("wordpress")`): `wp()`/`wp_eval()` calls, `check_wordpress_plugin(...)` (1539, 1547, 1556, …) accumulate into `site_notices`.
- **1805–2139: Drupal branch** (`elif framework.startswith("drupal")`): `drush`/`drush_php_script`, `check_drupal_module(...)` (1843, 1875–1909).
- 2140/2308: else/unknown-framework and update-count handling.
- 2461–2523: PHP-version checks; `--only-warn` short-circuit at 2523.
- 2532–2604: traffic aggregation by day/month.
- 2628–2947: matplotlib chart building (traffic surge bars, gauges); `fig.savefig(buf, ...)` at 2947 → PNG bytes.
- 3050–3077: `PantheonOverageProtection` rows — `db_session.add(op)` (3050), `commit` (3077).
- **3095–3211: plan-recommendation computation** — cost model over `plan_info`; `site_recommended_plan = min(costs_best, key=...)` (3161); upgrade/downgrade adjustments; ends with `recommended_plan` in results (3219, 3255).
- 3395–3474: assemble `sorted_notices`, contract-year banner.
- **3505–3537: template_dict** assembled; `banner_cid`/`chart_cid` via `make_msgid`.
- **3539–3552: Jinja2 render** — `Template(open("email_template.html").read()).render(**template_dict)` → `build/&lt;site&gt;.html`; same for `.txt`.
- **3554–3564: `subprocess.run(["php","inline-styles.php", …], check=True)`** — CSS inliner (external PHP process).
- 3568–3577: post-process styles, write `build/&lt;site&gt;-inline2.html`.
- **3579–3625: MIME assembly** — `EmailMessage`; To/Bcc depend on `--for-real` (3581–3588; without it, mail is addressed to `januside@…` + `{smtp_username}@umich.edu`); `set_content`/`add_alternative`; `add_related` for banner, chart, and `site_context["attachments"]`; write `build/&lt;site&gt;.eml`.
- **3627–3631: SMTP send is COMMENTED OUT** — `smtp_login()` / `send_message` / `emails_sent += 1` are all disabled. **The program currently never sends email**; it only writes `.eml` files. `smtp_login()` (755) and the `SMTP_SSL` import are effectively dead code at present.
- 3633–3636: append notices to `all_warnings` CSV rows. 3638: `plt.close(fig)`.

**Teardown (3643–3669):** `db_session.close()`, `db_engine.dispose()`; if `--all`, write `&lt;YYYYMMDD&gt;-notices.csv` and `-results.json` (filesystem write), else print to console; print savings summary.

## 3. Per-site pipeline summary (for seams)

`site_context` (1161) is the single mutable object threaded through checks. `check` hooks run once at 1167 right after it's built (before framework-specific data gathering). Notices accumulate via the local `site_notices` list and `sc.add_notice`. Recommendation is computed late (3095–3211) purely from `plan_info` config + aggregated visitor data. Rendering (Jinja2) → PHP inliner (subprocess) → MIME → `.eml` file.

## 4. `script_context.py` — shared global state (`/workspace/script_context.py`)

**Module-level mutable globals (initialized at import):**
- `options = {}` (9) — replaced by `args_parser.parse_args()` in the main script.
- `config = {}` (10) — parsed TOML.
- `plugin = {}` (11), `check = {}` (12) — loaded modules.
- `news = []` (13) — org-wide news items.
- `console = Console()` (16) — rich console (stdout).
- `substitutions = []` (18) — config-substitution registry.
- `hooks = {'setup': [], 'check': []}` (20–23).
- `plugin_context = {}` (25) — per-plugin scratch space (e.g. Cloudflare).
- `icon = {...}` (27–31) — type→emoji map (`info`/`warning`/`alert`).
- `text_maker = html2text.HTML2Text()` (54–63) — configured HTML→text converter.

**Helper functions:**
- `debug(*args, level=1) -&gt; None` (34) — prints via `console.log` when `options.verbose &gt;= level`. **Impure (stdout); depends on global `options`.**
- `add_hook(hook_name, target: dict) -&gt; None` (39) — appends to `hooks[name]`.
- `invoke_hooks(hook_name, *args, **kwargs) -&gt; None` (46) — calls each `hook['func'](*args, **kwargs)`. **Effects depend on registered hooks.**
- `add_notice(notice: dict, site_context: dict) -&gt; None` (65) — validates `message`, defaults `icon` from `icon[type]`, auto-generates `text` via `text_maker.handle` if absent, inserts/appends into `site_context['notices']`. `sys.exit(1)` if no `message`. Otherwise pure-ish (mutates the passed dict).
- `add_news_item(news_item: dict, from_where='check') -&gt; None` (80) — same pattern, appends/prepends to global `news`. `sys.exit(1)` on missing `message`.

Note: there is **no `add_substitution` helper** — plugins append to `sc.substitutions` directly.

## 5. Plugin / check module system

- **`find_modules(module_type) -&gt; list[str]`** (739) — `os.walk` over `plugin/` or `check/`, selects **non-empty `__init__.py`** files (`st.st_size != 0`), converts path to dotted module name, returns sorted list. **Filesystem read; deterministic.** The empty top-level `plugin/__init__.py` and `check/__init__.py` are skipped by the size check.
- **Self-registration at import** — each package `__init__.py` guards on `sc.config` and registers:
  - `plugin/cloudflare/__init__.py`: if `[Cloudflare].enabled`, reads env `CLOUDFLARE_EMAIL`/`CLOUDFLARE_API_KEY`, sets `sc.plugin_context['plugin.cloudflare']={}`, appends a **setup hook** `get_cloudflare_ips` directly to `sc.hooks['setup']`.
  - `plugin/aws/__init__.py`: if `[AWS].enabled`, sets `AWS_PROFILE`/`AWS_DEFAULT_REGION` env, appends a **substitution** `{'args':['secret','aws','$name','$key'], 'func':get_secret, 'func_args':['$name','$key']}`.
  - `plugin/umich/__init__.py`: if `[UMich].enabled`, adds **setup hook** `setup_portal_db` and a **substitution** `{'args':['umich','portal','plan_info','$plan','$field'], ...}`.
  - `check/umich/__init__.py`: if `[UMich].enabled`, registers **setup hook** under a *custom hook name* `'setup.umich.portal'` plus two **check hooks** (`check_sitelens_urls`, `check_sitelens_scores`). (Bug note: the `else` branch calls `sc.console(...)` as if callable — would raise if hit.)
- **Custom hook chaining:** `plugin/umich/portal.py:55` invokes `sc.invoke_hooks('setup.umich.portal', connection)` — i.e. the umich portal setup hook fans out to the sitelens setup hook, passing the DB connection. So there are effectively three hook phases: `setup`, the nested `setup.umich.portal`, and per-site `check`.
- **Config substitutions (`&lt;{ ... }&gt;`):**
  - `config_substitution(expr: str, path) -&gt; str` (653) — `shlex`-tokenizes the expression, scores it against every registered `sc.substitutions` entry (supports `$var` wildcards), calls the best match's `func`, `str()`-ifies the result. `sys.exit(1)` on no/ambiguous match or `None` result. **Effects depend on the matched func (AWS `get_secret` = network; umich `plan_info` = DB).**
  - `config_substitution_re = re.compile(r"&lt;\{(.*?)(?&lt;!\\)}")` (718).
  - `process_config(data, path="") -&gt; Any` (721) — recursively walks dict/list/str, `re.sub`-ing each `&lt;{...}&gt;` via `config_substitution`. Mutates in place. **Called twice** in `main()` (775 pre-setup, 806 post-setup).

## Function catalog — signatures, line numbers, external effects

House style: return-type hints use tuple syntax `-&gt; (str, str, bool)`.

**Pure / easily unit-testable (no network/DB/FS; at most stdout):**
- `escape_url(url)` (222) → str. Pure (`urllib.parse.quote`).
- `wp_error(site, code, message, errors: str) -&gt; list[dict]` (365). Pure notice builder.
- `fix_drush_output(output: str, errors: str) -&gt; (str, str)` (391). **Pure** (verified: no external calls).
- `drush_error(site, code, message, errors: str) -&gt; list[dict]` (443). Pure builder.
- `check_wordpress_plugin(site, installed_plugins: list, name, display_name, url, reason) -&gt; list` (533). Logic-only; receives installed list as a param; only side effect is `sc.console.print` (stdout). Testable.
- `check_drupal_module(site, installed_mods: dict, name, display_name, url, reason, level="warning") -&gt; list` (601). Same — pure logic + stdout.
- `sc.add_notice` / `sc.add_news_item` (script_context 65/80) — mutate passed dict / global list; `sys.exit` on missing `message`. Testable with care.

**Impure — hit external systems:**
- `run_terminus(command: list, input_data=None) -&gt; (str, str, bool)` (226). **subprocess.Popen → `terminus` CLI (network to Pantheon), 300s timeout**, stdout/stderr filtering, `sc.console` output. The single lowest-level external seam.
- `terminus(*args) -&gt; Any` (316). Wraps `run_terminus`; `json.loads`; **retry with `time.sleep(5)`** on expired session. (Has a latent bug: `args.push(...)` on a tuple.)
- `wp(siteenv, *args) -&gt; (Any, str)` (342), `wp_eval(siteenv, *args) -&gt; (str, str)` (356) — via `run_terminus`.
- `drush(siteenv, *args) -&gt; (Any, str)` (413), `drush_php_script(siteenv, script) -&gt; (Any, str)` (428) — via `run_terminus`.
- `get_old_metrics(site_env, site: dict, period, end_date) -&gt; list` (469). Calls `terminus("env:metrics", ...)` (network); builds DB row dicts. Logic testable if `terminus` is mocked.
- `config_substitution` (653) / `process_config` (721) — effects flow through registered substitution funcs (AWS/umich).
- `find_modules(module_type) -&gt; list[str]` (739). Filesystem walk; deterministic.
- `smtp_login() -&gt; SMTP_SSL` (755). **SMTP_SSL network + `os.environ["SMTP_PASSWORD"]`.** Currently dead (send is commented out).
- `main() -&gt; None` (762). Orchestrates everything: config FS read, module imports, DB engine, terminus/network, matplotlib, Jinja2, PHP subprocess, `.eml`/CSV/JSON file writes.

## Key testing-seam takeaways
1. **Import-time `parse_args()` (line 219)** and import-time ORM/argparse execution mean the module cannot be imported cleanly for unit tests without controlling `sys.argv`; the file also lacks a `.py` extension.
2. **All Pantheon/WP/Drupal I/O funnels through one function, `run_terminus` (226)** — the ideal mock point. `terminus`/`wp`/`drush`/`get_old_metrics` sit above it.
3. **`main()` is a ~2900-line monolith** (762–3669) mixing validation, DB, network, chart rendering, templating, a PHP subprocess, and file writes — the main refactor/seam target. Distinct terminal branches (`--create-tables` at 838, `--import-older-metrics` at 1100, `--update` at 1139) are the natural cut points.
4. **Genuinely pure, directly unit-testable today:** `escape_url`, `fix_drush_output`, `wp_error`, `drush_error`, `check_wordpress_plugin`, `check_drupal_module`, and the notice/news builders in `script_context.py`.
5. **Email send is disabled** (3627–3631) — tests should assert on `build/&lt;site&gt;.eml`/`.html`/`.txt` artifacts and the `.render` output, not on SMTP.
6. **Global mutable state in `sc`** (options/config/hooks/substitutions/news) must be reset between tests; hook/substitution registration happens as an import side effect of the `plugin`/`check` packages guarded by config flags.</result>

</task-notification>

## Assistant

All three agents reported. I now have a thorough picture:

- **Structure:** ~3,700-line monolith (`pantheon-sitehealth-emails`, no `.py` extension) + `script_context.py` (global `sc` state) + `plugin/`/`check/` packages. **argparse runs at import time** (line 219) and the file has no `.py` extension → the module can't be cleanly imported for unit tests without controlling `sys.argv` and loading via `importlib`.
- **The one great seam:** every Pantheon/WP/Drush call funnels through `run_terminus()` (line 226, `subprocess.Popen`, no shell). A second independent subprocess seam is the `php inline-styles.php` CSS inliner (line 3554).
- **Email send is disabled** (lines 3627-3631 commented out) — today the program only writes `build/<site>.{html,txt,eml}`. Tests must assert on those artifacts, not on SMTP.
- **DB** is injectable via config (`sqlite:///`, could point at `:memory:`/temp). **Genuinely pure functions** today: `escape_url`, `fix_drush_output`, `wp_error`, `drush_error`, `check_wordpress_plugin`, `check_drupal_module`, the notice/news builders.
- **Greenfield:** no tests, no CI, no pytest. uv-managed, Python 3.13, Node 24 present. The dev-container **firewall blocks** Pantheon/SMTP/AWS/PyPI/Playwright-CDN when active → offline tests must mock all network; a live tier needs network + auth.
- Found **real latent bugs** (the `terminus()` retry uses `args.push()`/`del args[...]` on a tuple; a `check/umich` else-branch calls `sc.console(...)` as if callable).
- Output `SPEC.md` goes in `development/2026-07-04-test-harness/` per the archive convention.

Now the interview. These first four are the load-bearing architectural forks that shape the entire design.

## Assistant

Clear. Key reframing noted: **the firewall stays off, so live tests against real test sites are the default; mocked/offline tests are used only where they add clear value** (fault injection, deterministic edge cases, pure-logic speed). And **bugs get fixed now with regression tests**. That reshapes the design toward live-first integration with monkeypatch/shim fakes reserved for error paths the real test sites can't be coaxed into.

Now the expansion opportunities — neutral posture, you cherry-pick. Note one hard fact that constrains the email work: since SMTP send is commented out and must stay disabled, the GMail send→receive round-trip **cannot actually run yet**, so its phasing matters.

```
Your questions have been answered: "Email send is disabled (and must stay disabled until SMTP/SendGrid lands), so the GMail send→receive→error-detection test can't actually run yet. Loading a report's HTML from disk in a browser, however, works now. What browser/email testing scope should the harness build now?"="Render-from-disk now; scaffold + defer GMail", "When the email round-trip test is eventually activated, how should the harness authenticate to the GMail test account? ## Assistant

All decisions locked. Here's the consolidated direction:

| Decision | Choice |
|---|---|
| Seam strategy | Hybrid: tiny behavior-preserving importability refactor + black-box CLI tests |
| External-tool interception | Both — Python monkeypatch (unit/integration) + PATH-shim fakes (e2e) |
| Live tests | **Default** (firewall stays off); offline/mocked only where clearly beneficial (fault injection, deterministic edge cases, pure-logic speed) |
| Discovered bugs | Fix now, each with a regression test |
| Browser/email | Render-from-disk now; scaffold + defer GMail round-trip (send is disabled) |
| GMail auth (deferred) | Gmail API + OAuth token stored as a secret |
| Output | Thin `run-tests` wrapper with `--human` (default) + `--llm` modes |
| Rigor add-ons | All three: golden snapshots, Hypothesis property tests, pytest-cov (no gate) |

One scope clarity I'll bake in: **this task's deliverable is `SPEC.md`, not the harness itself.** Approving the plan authorizes me to write `SPEC.md` (+ run the adversarial-review loop) — not to build the `tests/` tree or touch the main script. That happens in a later prompt.

Let me write the plan file.

```json
{
  "file_path": "/home/node/.claude/plans/development-2026-07-04-test-harness-pro-wiggly-lobster.md",
  "content": "# Plan: Design a Test Harness for `pantheon-sitehealth-emails`\n\n## Context\n\n`pantheon-sitehealth-emails` is a ~3,700-line single-file Python program (plus\n`script_context.py` and `plugin/`/`check/` packages) that pulls Pantheon traffic/site-health\ndata via Terminus/WP-CLI/Drush and emails monthly reports. **It has zero tests, zero CI, and\nno test tooling** — `README.md`'s top two open TODOs are literally \"test harness\" and \"test\nsuite.\"\n\nSeveral **major** changes are planned next: a large modularization refactor of the monolith,\na push to move logic into the plugin/config framework, and re-enabling SMTP + adding SendGrid.\nThe purpose of this work is to build the **safety net first**: a test harness (and initial\nsmoke tests) that proves the code works as designed today and keeps proving it as those\nrefactors land — so a regression is caught early, when it is cheap to fix.\n\n**This task designs the harness. The single deliverable is a specification document,\n`development/2026-07-04-test-harness/SPEC.md`.** Approving this plan authorizes writing that\nspec and running an adversarial review of it — **not** building the `tests/` tree or modifying\nthe program. Implementing the harness is a later, separate prompt.\n\nTwo absolute constraints govern all design and every future test run:\n- **NEVER** run the program with `--all` (can take ~6 hours).\n- **NEVER** run the program with `--for-real` (can email real customers).\nTests use only `its-wws-test1` (WordPress) / `its-wws-test2` (Drupal), or a deliberately\nchosen real site, all **read-only**.\n\n## Decisions locked via interview (these drive the whole design)\n\n1. **Seam strategy — Hybrid.** A tiny, behavior-preserving refactor to make the script\n   importable, enabling real unit tests, **plus** black-box CLI tests. Not black-box-only\n   (too coarse); not a full refactor-now (too big a diff before a safety net exists).\n2. **External-tool interception — Both.** Monkeypatch `run_terminus`/`terminus` for fast\n   in-process tests; PATH-shim fake executables (fake `terminus`) for deterministic full-script\n   end-to-end runs.\n3. **Live-first.** The dev-container firewall is off and will stay off; network + Pantheon auth\n   are always available. **Live tests against the real test sites are the default tier.**\n   Offline/mocked tests are written only where they add clear value: fault injection, edge\n   cases the live sites can't be coaxed into, and fast pure-logic checks.\n4. **Fix discovered bugs now, with regression tests** (not xfail-and-defer).\n5. **Browser/email:** implement headless-browser \"render report HTML from disk\" now; **design\n   and scaffold** the GMail send→receive→error-detection round-trip but leave it skipped/deferred\n   (email send is commented out and must stay disabled until SMTP/SendGrid lands).\n6. **GMail auth (for the deferred tier):** Gmail API + OAuth refresh token stored as a secret.\n7. **Output:** a thin `run-tests` wrapper over pytest with `--human` (default, rich) and\n   `--llm` (terse, failures-first, machine-parseable) modes.\n8. **Rigor add-ons (all in):** golden-file snapshots for rendered reports; Hypothesis\n   property tests for pure math; pytest-cov coverage (measured, reported, **no gate**).\n\n## What the code review established (load-bearing facts SPEC.md relies on)\n\n- **One golden seam:** every Pantheon/WP/Drush call funnels through `run_terminus()`\n  (`pantheon-sitehealth-emails:226`, `subprocess.Popen`, argument-list form, no `shell=True`,\n  300s timeout). `terminus()` (:316), `wp()`/`wp_eval()` (:342/:356), `drush()`/\n  `drush_php_script()` (:413/:428) all sit above it. WP/Drush are invoked *as* Terminus\n  subcommands (`terminus wp …`, `terminus drush …`), so faking `terminus` alone covers all three.\n- **Second independent subprocess seam:** the CSS inliner `subprocess.run([\"php\",\n  \"inline-styles.php\", …], check=True)` at `:3554`. `php` is local, deterministic, and fast —\n  tests use **real php**, not a shim.\n- **Email send is disabled** (`:3627-3631`, commented out). Today the program only writes\n  `build/<site>.{html,txt,eml}`. Tests assert on those artifacts, never on SMTP.\n- **Import-time side effects:** argparse builds and `sc.options = parse_args()` runs at module\n  scope (`:141-219`); the file has **no `.py` extension**. Importing it today calls `parse_args`\n  against live `sys.argv`. SQLAlchemy models are defined at import.\n- **Genuinely pure / directly unit-testable today:** `escape_url` (:222),\n  `fix_drush_output` (:391), `wp_error` (:365), `drush_error` (:443),\n  `check_wordpress_plugin` (:533), `check_drupal_module` (:601), and the notice/news builders\n  in `script_context.py` (`add_notice`:65, `add_news_item`:80).\n- **DB is injectable via config** — engine built at `:818-836` purely from\n  `sc.config[\"Database\"]`; point it at a temp sqlite file. `--create-tables` runs\n  `Base.metadata.create_all`.\n- **Global mutable state** lives in `script_context.py` (`sc.options/config/plugin/check/news/\n  hooks/substitutions/plugin_context`) and must be reset between tests.\n- **Confirmed latent bugs to fix (with regression tests):**\n  - `terminus()` session-expiry retry (`:333-337`) calls `args.push(...)` / `del args[...]`\n    on a **tuple** — `*args` is a tuple, so this path would crash if ever hit.\n  - `check/umich/__init__.py` `else` branch calls `sc.console(...)` as if callable (should be\n    `sc.console.print(...)`).\n  - (SPEC.md re-verifies each against current source before asserting the fix.)\n\n## The minimal seam refactor (behavior-preserving)\n\nMake the module importable without executing argparse at import:\n\n```python\ndef build_arg_parser() -> argparse.ArgumentParser: ...   # all add_argument calls\ndef parse_args(argv=None): return build_arg_parser().parse_args(argv)\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    sc.options = parse_args()\n    main()\n```\n\n- Functions read `sc.options` at *call* time, so moving the `parse_args()` call into the\n  `__main__` guard is safe: tests import the module, set `sc.options` (a real parsed namespace\n  or a fake), then call functions or `main()`.\n- **No rename** (keeps `./pantheon-sitehealth-emails` runnable exactly as documented). Tests\n  load the extension-less file via `importlib.util` + `SourceFileLoader`, cached in one\n  session-scoped fixture (avoids re-registering SQLAlchemy models).\n- **Verification gate:** for `its-wws-test1` at a fixed `--date`, `build/` artifacts must be\n  identical before vs. after the refactor (modulo known-volatile `make_msgid` CIDs and the\n  `Date:` header, which are normalized).\n\n## Harness architecture\n\n### Framework choices (SPEC.md justifies vs. alternatives)\n- **pytest** as the spine (fixtures, marks, parametrize, ecosystem). Rejected: `unittest`\n  (verbose, weak fixtures), `nose2` (unmaintained).\n- **syrupy** for golden snapshots; **Hypothesis** for property tests; **pytest-cov** for\n  coverage; **pytest-playwright** (Python Playwright) for the browser render tier (one language,\n  one runner; downloads its own Chromium — fine, firewall is off).\n- **PHP:** no PHP test framework — `inline-styles.php` is exercised via subprocess with\n  sample-HTML-in / golden-HTML-out.\n\n### Directory layout\n```\ntests/\n  conftest.py          # load-module fixture, sc-reset, temp cwd/build, temp sqlite, config fixtures,\n                       #   run_program() helper (with the --all/--for-real interlock)\n  README.md            # dev-facing testing docs (NOT docs/, which is end-user only)\n  fixtures/\n    config/            # minimal.toml + full.toml (self-contained; never depend on the private config symlink)\n    terminus/          # recorded JSON responses keyed by argv (org:site:list, env:info, env:metrics, wp/ drush lists)\n    db/                # seed PantheonTraffic rows\n  shims/               # fake `terminus` executable (reads fixtures/terminus manifest, prints canned JSON)\n  goldens/             # syrupy snapshot baselines for rendered reports\n  unit/                # pure functions: plan-rec math, fix_drush_output, escape_url, notices, config_substitution\n  integration/         # in-process; run_terminus monkeypatched or live; temp DB; check hooks; the 2 bug regressions\n  e2e/                 # full-script subprocess runs — live (default) + shim-backed (deterministic/edge)\n  render/              # pytest-playwright: load build/*.html from disk, assert structure + no console errors\n  email/               # GMail round-trip — scaffolded, @pytest.mark.skip(\"email send disabled until SMTP/SendGrid\")\n```\n\n### Test tiers & marks\n`unit`, `integration`, `e2e`, `live`, `render`, `email`, `slow`. Per the live-first decision,\nthe **default `run-tests` run includes live tiers**; `run-tests --fast` selects the offline\nsubset (`-m \"not live and not slow\"`) for the inner loop. Claude Code picks the relevant\nsubset per change (e.g. touched a Drupal check → run unit + integration + the Drupal e2e/live).\n\n### Seam & fixture flow (ASCII)\n```\n            ┌─────────────── unit ───────────────┐   pure funcs, no I/O\n            │                                     │\n monkeypatch│  run_terminus() / terminus()  ◄─────┤ integration (fault injection,\n            │        │                            │   edge cases, bug regressions)\n            ▼        ▼                            │\n      ┌───────────────────┐                       │\n      │  program logic    │                       │\n      └───────────────────┘                       │\n            ▲        ▲                            │\n PATH shim  │        │  real terminus (live)      │\n fake       │        │                            ▼\n `terminus` │        └──────────► e2e / live: full subprocess run of\n            │                     ./pantheon-sitehealth-emails <site> --date …\n            ▼                              │\n     build/<site>.{html,txt,eml}  ─────────┼─► golden snapshots (syrupy, CIDs/Date normalized)\n                                           └─► render tier (Playwright loads .html from disk)\n```\n\n### Safety interlock (Prime Directive: zero silent failures)\nA `run_program(args)` helper is the **only** sanctioned way to invoke the program in tests. It\nhard-fails (raises, never silently) if `--all`, `-a`, or `--for-real` appears in argv. This\ninterlock is itself covered by a test. When the email tier activates, an analogous guard will\nassert the recipient is the GMail test identity, never a customer address.\n\n### run-tests wrapper (thin)\n`./run-tests` wraps pytest: default `--human` (rich); `--llm` (terse, `-q`, no color,\nfailures-first, machine-parseable summary via a small conftest hook); `--fast` (offline\nsubset); `--record` (refresh `fixtures/terminus/` from the live test sites); `--update-goldens`\n(syrupy update); `--coverage` (pytest-cov, no gate); passes through `-m`/`-k`/paths.\n\n### Determinism notes (for goldens)\nNormalize/strip volatile bits before snapshotting: `make_msgid` CIDs, the `Date:` header, and\nembedded PNG bytes (assert charts *exist* rather than byte-compare matplotlib output). Fix\n`--date` and seed the DB so traffic-derived output is stable.\n\n### Property tests (honest scope)\nHypothesis targets genuinely pure/extractable functions (`fix_drush_output`, `escape_url`,\ntraffic aggregation). The plan-recommendation cost model is currently **inline in `main()`\n(`:3095-3211`)** — SPEC.md flags a small optional extraction to a pure `recommend_plan(...)`\nfunction as the enabler; if not extracted now, that math is instead pinned via parametrized\ne2e cases.\n\n## Smoke coverage the harness must ship with (proves the harness works — not the full suite)\n- 1 **unit** (e.g. `fix_drush_output` / `escape_url`).\n- 1 **integration** (monkeypatched `run_terminus` + temp sqlite DB + a check hook).\n- 1 **e2e** (shim `terminus`, full subprocess run, asserts `build/<site>.eml` produced).\n- 1 **live** (real `terminus self:info` or read-only `env:info` on `its-wws-test1`).\n- 1 **render** (Playwright loads a committed sample `build/*.html`, asserts key elements + no console errors).\n- 1 **email** (scaffolded, skipped/deferred).\n- 2 **bug regressions** (the `terminus()` retry tuple bug; the `check/umich` `sc.console` bug) — plus the fixes.\n- 1 **interlock** test (`run_program` refuses `--all`/`--for-real`).\n\n## Documentation updates (instructions to include in SPEC.md, executed at implementation time)\n- **README.md:** add a \"Testing\" section (install `.[test]` + `playwright install chromium`;\n  `run-tests` modes/tiers; live vs `--fast`; `--record`, `--update-goldens`, `--coverage`).\n  Retire the two TODO bullets.\n- **CLAUDE.md:** add testing conventions — the importability seam, the `run_terminus`/`php`\n  mock seams, the `--all`/`--for-real` interlock, fixture/golden refresh commands, and the\n  standing policy \"design + implement appropriate tests for each change.\"\n- **tests/README.md:** dev-facing detail (layout, marks, writing a new test, recording fixtures).\n- **docs/**: **no** testing docs — `docs/` is end-user only, per the repo convention.\n- **pyproject.toml:** add `[project.optional-dependencies] test = [...]`,\n  `[tool.pytest.ini_options]` (markers, testpaths), `[tool.coverage.run]` (source points at the\n  extension-less script).\n\n## Acceptance criteria for the harness (SPEC.md states these as the \"done\" bar)\n- `uv pip install .[test] && playwright install chromium` succeeds.\n- `./run-tests --fast` is green offline (unit + shim e2e + render on committed HTML), no network.\n- `./run-tests` is green including live read-only smoke against `its-wws-test1/2` — provably\n  never using `--all`/`--for-real`.\n- One passing smoke test per tier (list above); the two bug fixes + regressions pass; the\n  interlock test passes.\n- `./run-tests --llm` emits terse, machine-parseable output; `--coverage` reports coverage\n  (no gate); `--update-goldens` regenerates snapshots and a re-run is green.\n- Seam-refactor byte-identity check passes for `its-wws-test1` (volatile bits normalized).\n\n## SPEC.md structure (what the deliverable contains, per PROMPT methodology)\nFull spec including: the three approaches considered (black-box-only; hybrid; full-refactor-now)\nscored 0–1 on Correctness / Completeness / Ability-to-implement / Maintainability / Clarity,\nwith the hybrid selected and refined to ≥0.9 on each; the architecture above with ASCII\ndiagrams for tier pyramid, seam/fixture flow, and the `run-tests` decision tree; the shadow-path\nand edge-case analysis (nil/empty/upstream-error for each new data flow; user-interrupt, slow\nconnection, stale fixture for interactions); concrete acceptance criteria; and the doc-update\ninstructions. Everything deferred (GMail activation, CI next year, plan-rec extraction) is\nwritten down explicitly.\n\n## Execution steps once this plan is approved (produces the deliverable — NOT the harness)\n1. Write `development/2026-07-04-test-harness/SPEC.md` per the structure above.\n2. Run the adversarial review: dispatch a fresh reviewer subagent (no brainstorming context)\n   to score SPEC.md 1–10 across Completeness / Consistency / Clarity / Scope / Feasibility and\n   list issues; fix issues on disk; re-dispatch (max 3 iterations; convergence guard →\n   persist unresolved items as \"## Reviewer Concerns\"). If the subagent is unavailable, skip\n   and note \"Spec review unavailable — presenting unreviewed doc.\"\n3. Report the review result (rounds survived, issues fixed, score) and present SPEC.md.\n4. **Stop.** Do not write any test code or modify `pantheon-sitehealth-emails` — that is the\n   next prompt.\n\n## Verification of the deliverable\n- `SPEC.md` exists in `development/2026-07-04-test-harness/`, follows the archive convention,\n  and contains all sections above (three scored approaches, diagrams, acceptance criteria,\n  doc-update instructions, deferred-items list).\n- The adversarial-review loop ran (or was explicitly reported unavailable), with the final\n  score and any \"Reviewer Concerns\" recorded in the document.\n- No source files changed; no test code written (this task is design-only).\n\n## Explicitly NOT in scope (deferred, written down)\n- Building the `tests/` tree, the `run-tests` wrapper, shims, fixtures, or any test code.\n- The importability seam refactor and the two bug fixes (specified here, implemented later).\n- Re-enabling SMTP; implementing SendGrid; activating the GMail email tier.\n- Regenerating `fqdns.json` / the 24-hour staleness handling.\n- CI/CD (planned next year; the design keeps tests CI-portable so adding it later is trivial).\n- Performance/parallel-check testing.\n"
}

SQLAlchemy models are defined at import.\n- **Genuinely pure / directly unit-testable today:** `escape_url` (:222),\n  `fix_drush_output` (:391), `wp_error` (:365), `drush_error` (:443),\n  `check_wordpress_plugin` (:533), `check_drupal_module` (:601), and the notice/news builders\n  in `script_context.py` (`add_notice`:65, `add_news_item`:80).\n- **DB is injectable via config** — engine built at `:818-836` purely from\n  `sc.config[\"Database\"]`; point it at a temp sqlite file. `--create-tables` runs\n  `Base.metadata.create_all`.\n- **Global mutable state** lives in `script_context.py` (`sc.options/config/plugin/check/news/\n  hooks/substitutions/plugin_context`) and must be reset between tests.\n- **Confirmed latent bugs to fix (with regression tests):**\n  - `terminus()` session-expiry retry (`:333-337`) calls `args.push(...)` / `del args[...]`\n    on a **tuple** — `*args` is a tuple, so this path would crash if ever hit.\n  - `check/umich/__init__.py` `else` branch calls `sc.console(...)` as if callable (should be\n    `sc.console.print(...)`).\n  - (SPEC.md re-verifies each against current source before asserting the fix.)\n\n## The minimal seam refactor (behavior-preserving)\n\nMake the module importable without executing argparse at import:\n\n```python\ndef build_arg_parser() -> argparse.ArgumentParser: ...   # all add_argument calls\ndef parse_args(argv=None): return build_arg_parser().parse_args(argv)\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    sc.options = parse_args()\n    main()\n```\n\n- Functions read `sc.options` at *call* time, so moving the `parse_args()` call into the\n  `__main__` guard is safe: tests import the module, set `sc.options` (a real parsed namespace\n  or a fake), then call functions or `main()`.\n- **No rename** (keeps `./pantheon-sitehealth-emails` runnable exactly as documented). Tests\n  load the extension-less file via `importlib.util` + `SourceFileLoader`, cached in one\n  session-scoped fixture (avoids re-registering SQLAlchemy models).\n- **Verification gate:** for `its-wws-test1` at a fixed `--date`, `build/` artifacts must be\n  identical before vs. after the refactor (modulo known-volatile `make_msgid` CIDs and the\n  `Date:` header, which are normalized).\n\n## Harness architecture\n\n### Framework choices (SPEC.md justifies vs. alternatives)\n- **pytest** as the spine (fixtures, marks, parametrize, ecosystem). Rejected: `unittest`\n  (verbose, weak fixtures), `nose2` (unmaintained).\n- **syrupy** for golden snapshots; **Hypothesis** for property tests; **pytest-cov** for\n  coverage; **pytest-playwright** (Python Playwright) for the browser render tier (one language,\n  one runner; downloads its own Chromium — fine, firewall is off).\n- **PHP:** no PHP test framework — `inline-styles.php` is exercised via subprocess with\n  sample-HTML-in / golden-HTML-out.\n\n### Directory layout\n```\ntests/\n  conftest.py          # load-module fixture, sc-reset, temp cwd/build, temp sqlite, config fixtures,\n                       #   run_program() helper (with the --all/--for-real interlock)\n  README.md            # dev-facing testing docs (NOT docs/, which is end-user only)\n  fixtures/\n    config/            # minimal.toml + full.toml (self-contained; never depend on the private config symlink)\n    terminus/          # recorded JSON responses keyed by argv (org:site:list, env:info, env:metrics, wp/ drush lists)\n    db/                # seed PantheonTraffic rows\n  shims/               # fake `terminus` executable (reads fixtures/terminus manifest, prints canned JSON)\n  goldens/             # syrupy snapshot baselines for rendered reports\n  unit/                # pure functions: plan-rec math, fix_drush_output, escape_url, notices, config_substitution\n  integration/         # in-process; run_terminus monkeypatched or live; temp DB; check hooks; the 2 bug regressions\n  e2e/                 # full-script subprocess runs — live (default) + shim-backed (deterministic/edge)\n  render/              # pytest-playwright: load build/*.html from disk, assert structure + no console errors\n  email/               # GMail round-trip — scaffolded, @pytest.mark.skip(\"email send disabled until SMTP/SendGrid\")\n```\n\n### Test tiers & marks\n`unit`, `integration`, `e2e`, `live`, `render`, `email`, `slow`. Per the live-first decision,\nthe **default `run-tests` run includes live tiers**; `run-tests --fast` selects the offline\nsubset (`-m \"not live and not slow\"`) for the inner loop. Claude Code picks the relevant\nsubset per change (e.g. touched a Drupal check → run unit + integration + the Drupal e2e/live).\n\n### Seam & fixture flow (ASCII)\n```\n            ┌─────────────── unit ───────────────┐   pure funcs, no I/O\n            │                                     │\n monkeypatch│  run_terminus() / terminus()  ◄─────┤ integration (fault injection,\n            │        │                            │   edge cases, bug regressions)\n            ▼        ▼                            │\n      ┌───────────────────┐                       │\n      │  program logic    │                       │\n      └───────────────────┘                       │\n            ▲        ▲                            │\n PATH shim  │        │  real terminus (live)      │\n fake       │        │                            ▼\n `terminus` │        └──────────► e2e / live: full subprocess run of\n            │                     ./pantheon-sitehealth-emails <site> --date …\n            ▼                              │\n     build/<site>.{html,txt,eml}  ─────────┼─► golden snapshots (syrupy, CIDs/Date normalized)\n                                           └─► render tier (Playwright loads .html from disk)\n```\n\n### Safety interlock (Prime Directive: zero silent failures)\nA `run_program(args)` helper is the **only** sanctioned way to invoke the program in tests. It\nhard-fails (raises, never silently) if `--all`, `-a`, or `--for-real` appears in argv. This\ninterlock is itself covered by a test. When the email tier activates, an analogous guard will\nassert the recipient is the GMail test identity, never a customer address.\n\n### run-tests wrapper (thin)\n`./run-tests` wraps pytest: default `--human` (rich); `--llm` (terse, `-q`, no color,\nfailures-first, machine-parseable summary via a small conftest hook); `--fast` (offline\nsubset); `--record` (refresh `fixtures/terminus/` from the live test sites); `--update-goldens`\n(syrupy update); `--coverage` (pytest-cov, no gate); passes through `-m`/`-k`/paths.\n\n### Determinism notes (for goldens)\nNormalize/strip volatile bits before snapshotting: `make_msgid` CIDs, the `Date:` header, and\nembedded PNG bytes (assert charts *exist* rather than byte-compare matplotlib output). Fix\n`--date` and seed the DB so traffic-derived output is stable.\n\n### Property tests (honest scope)\nHypothesis targets genuinely pure/extractable functions (`fix_drush_output`, `escape_url`,\ntraffic aggregation). The plan-recommendation cost model is currently **inline in `main()`\n(`:3095-3211`)** — SPEC.md flags a small optional extraction to a pure `recommend_plan(...)`\nfunction as the enabler; if not extracted now, that math is instead pinned via parametrized\ne2e cases.\n\n## Smoke coverage the harness must ship with (proves the harness works — not the full suite)\n- 1 **unit** (e.g. `fix_drush_output` / `escape_url`).\n- 1 **integration** (monkeypatched `run_terminus` + temp sqlite DB + a check hook).\n- 1 **e2e** (shim `terminus`, full subprocess run, asserts `build/<site>.eml` produced).\n- 1 **live** (real `terminus self:info` or read-only `env:info` on `its-wws-test1`).\n- 1 **render** (Playwright loads a committed sample `build/*.html`, asserts key elements + no console errors).\n- 1 **email** (scaffolded, skipped/deferred).\n- 2 **bug regressions** (the `terminus()` retry tuple bug; live vs `--fast`; `--record`, `--update-goldens`, `--coverage`).\n  Retire the two TODO bullets.\n- **CLAUDE.md:** add testing conventions — the importability seam, the `run_terminus`/`php`\n  mock seams, the `--all`/`--for-real` interlock, fixture/golden refresh commands, and the\n  standing policy \"design + implement appropriate tests for each change.\"\n- **tests/README.md:** dev-facing detail (layout, marks, writing a new test, recording fixtures).\n- **docs/**: **no** testing docs — `docs/` is end-user only, per the repo convention.\n- **pyproject.toml:** add `[project.optional-dependencies] test = [...]`,\n  `[tool.pytest.ini_options]` (markers, testpaths), `[tool.coverage.run]` (source points at the\n  extension-less script).\n\n## Acceptance criteria for the harness (SPEC.md states these as the \"done\" bar)\n- `uv pip install .[test] && playwright install chromium` succeeds.\n- `./run-tests --fast` is green offline (unit + shim e2e + render on committed HTML), no network.\n- `./run-tests` is green including live read-only smoke against `its-wws-test1/2` — provably\n  never using `--all`/`--for-real`.\n- One passing smoke test per tier (list above);
