## Approved Plan (edited by user):
# Plan: Design a Test Harness for `pantheon-sitehealth-emails`

## Context

`pantheon-sitehealth-emails` is a ~3,700-line single-file Python program (plus
`script_context.py` and `plugin/`/`check/` packages) that pulls Pantheon traffic/site-health
data via Terminus/WP-CLI/Drush and emails monthly reports. **It has zero tests, zero CI, and
no test tooling** — `README.md`'s top two open TODOs are literally "test harness" and "test
suite."

Several **major** changes are planned next: a large modularization refactor of the monolith,
a push to move logic into the plugin/config framework, and re-enabling SMTP + adding SendGrid.
The purpose of this work is to build the **safety net first**: a test harness (and initial
smoke tests) that proves the code works as designed today and keeps proving it as those
refactors land — so a regression is caught early, when it is cheap to fix.

**This task designs the harness. The single deliverable is a specification document,
`development/2026-07-04-test-harness/SPEC.md`.** Approving this plan authorizes writing that
spec and running an adversarial review of it — **not** building the `tests/` tree or modifying
the program. Implementing the harness is a later, separate prompt.

Two absolute constraints govern all design and every future test run:
- **NEVER** run the program with `--all` (can take ~6 hours).
- **NEVER** run the program with `--for-real` (can email real customers).
Tests use only `its-wws-test1` (WordPress) / `its-wws-test2` (Drupal), or a deliberately
chosen real site, all **read-only**.

## Decisions locked via interview (these drive the whole design)

1. **Seam strategy — Hybrid.** A tiny, behavior-preserving refactor to make the script
   importable, enabling real unit tests, **plus** black-box CLI tests. Not black-box-only
   (too coarse); not a full refactor-now (too big a diff before a safety net exists).
2. **External-tool interception — Both.** Monkeypatch `run_terminus`/`terminus` for fast
   in-process tests; PATH-shim fake executables (fake `terminus`) for deterministic full-script
   end-to-end runs.
3. **Live-first.** The dev-container firewall is off and will stay off; network + Pantheon auth
   are always available. **Live tests against the real test sites are the default tier.**
   Offline/mocked tests are written only where they add clear value: fault injection, edge
   cases the live sites can't be coaxed into, and fast pure-logic checks.
4. **Fix discovered bugs now, with regression tests** (not xfail-and-defer).
5. **Browser/email:** implement headless-browser "render report HTML from disk" now; **design
   and scaffold** the GMail send→receive→error-detection round-trip but leave it skipped/deferred
   (email send is commented out and must stay disabled until SMTP/SendGrid lands).
6. **GMail auth (for the deferred tier):** Gmail API + OAuth refresh token stored as a secret.
7. **Output:** a thin `run-tests` wrapper over pytest with `--human` (default, rich) and
   `--llm` (terse, failures-first, machine-parseable) modes.
8. **Rigor add-ons (all in):** golden-file snapshots for rendered reports; Hypothesis
   property tests for pure math; pytest-cov coverage (measured, reported, **no gate**).

## What the code review established (load-bearing facts SPEC.md relies on)

- **One golden seam:** every Pantheon/WP/Drush call funnels through `run_terminus()`
  (`pantheon-sitehealth-emails:226`, `subprocess.Popen`, argument-list form, no `shell=True`,
  300s timeout). `terminus()` (:316), `wp()`/`wp_eval()` (:342/:356), `drush()`/
  `drush_php_script()` (:413/:428) all sit above it. WP/Drush are invoked *as* Terminus
  subcommands (`terminus wp …`, `terminus drush …`), so faking `terminus` alone covers all three.
- **Second independent subprocess seam:** the CSS inliner `subprocess.run(["php",
  "inline-styles.php", …], check=True)` at `:3554`. `php` is local, deterministic, and fast —
  tests use **real php**, not a shim.
- **Email send is disabled** (`:3627-3631`, commented out). Today the program only writes
  `build/<site>.{html,txt,eml}`. Tests assert on those artifacts, never on SMTP.
- **Import-time side effects:** argparse builds and `sc.options = parse_args()` runs at module
  scope (`:141-219`); the file has **no `.py` extension**. Importing it today calls `parse_args`
  against live `sys.argv`. SQLAlchemy models are defined at import.
- **Genuinely pure / directly unit-testable today:** `escape_url` (:222),
  `fix_drush_output` (:391), `wp_error` (:365), `drush_error` (:443),
  `check_wordpress_plugin` (:533), `check_drupal_module` (:601), and the notice/news builders
  in `script_context.py` (`add_notice`:65, `add_news_item`:80).
- **DB is injectable via config** — engine built at `:818-836` purely from
  `sc.config["Database"]`; point it at a temp sqlite file. `--create-tables` runs
  `Base.metadata.create_all`.
- **Global mutable state** lives in `script_context.py` (`sc.options/config/plugin/check/news/
  hooks/substitutions/plugin_context`) and must be reset between tests.
- **Confirmed latent bugs to fix (with regression tests):**
  - `terminus()` session-expiry retry (`:333-337`) calls `args.push(...)` / `del args[...]`
    on a **tuple** — `*args` is a tuple, so this path would crash if ever hit.
  - `check/umich/__init__.py` `else` branch calls `sc.console(...)` as if callable (should be
    `sc.console.print(...)`).
  - (SPEC.md re-verifies each against current source before asserting the fix.)

## The minimal seam refactor (behavior-preserving)

Make the module importable without executing argparse at import:

```python
def build_arg_parser() -> argparse.ArgumentParser: ...   # all add_argument calls
def parse_args(argv=None): return build_arg_parser().parse_args(argv)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    sc.options = parse_args()
    main()
```

- Functions read `sc.options` at *call* time, so moving the `parse_args()` call into the
  `__main__` guard is safe: tests import the module, set `sc.options` (a real parsed namespace
  or a fake), then call functions or `main()`.
- **No rename** (keeps `./pantheon-sitehealth-emails` runnable exactly as documented). Tests
  load the extension-less file via `importlib.util` + `SourceFileLoader`, cached in one
  session-scoped fixture (avoids re-registering SQLAlchemy models).
- **Verification gate:** for `its-wws-test1` at a fixed `--date`, `build/` artifacts must be
  identical before vs. after the refactor (modulo known-volatile `make_msgid` CIDs and the
  `Date:` header, which are normalized).

## Harness architecture

### Framework choices (SPEC.md justifies vs. alternatives)
- **pytest** as the spine (fixtures, marks, parametrize, ecosystem). Rejected: `unittest`
  (verbose, weak fixtures), `nose2` (unmaintained).
- **syrupy** for golden snapshots; **Hypothesis** for property tests; **pytest-cov** for
  coverage; **pytest-playwright** (Python Playwright) for the browser render tier (one language,
  one runner; downloads its own Chromium — fine, firewall is off).
- **PHP:** no PHP test framework — `inline-styles.php` is exercised via subprocess with
  sample-HTML-in / golden-HTML-out.

### Directory layout
```
tests/
  conftest.py          # load-module fixture, sc-reset, temp cwd/build, temp sqlite, config fixtures,
                       #   run_program() helper (with the --all/--for-real interlock)
  README.md            # dev-facing testing docs (NOT docs/, which is end-user only)
  fixtures/
    config/            # minimal.toml + full.toml (self-contained; never depend on the private config symlink)
    terminus/          # recorded JSON responses keyed by argv (org:site:list, env:info, env:metrics, wp/ drush lists)
    db/                # seed PantheonTraffic rows
  shims/               # fake `terminus` executable (reads fixtures/terminus manifest, prints canned JSON)
  goldens/             # syrupy snapshot baselines for rendered reports
  unit/                # pure functions: plan-rec math, fix_drush_output, escape_url, notices, config_substitution
  integration/         # in-process; run_terminus monkeypatched or live; temp DB; check hooks; the 2 bug regressions
  e2e/                 # full-script subprocess runs — live (default) + shim-backed (deterministic/edge)
  render/              # pytest-playwright: load build/*.html from disk, assert structure + no console errors
  email/               # GMail round-trip — scaffolded, @pytest.mark.skip("email send disabled until SMTP/SendGrid")
```

### Test tiers & marks
`unit`, `integration`, `e2e`, `live`, `render`, `email`, `slow`. Per the live-first decision,
the **default `run-tests` run includes live tiers**; `run-tests --fast` selects the offline
subset (`-m "not live and not slow"`) for the inner loop. Claude Code picks the relevant
subset per change (e.g. touched a Drupal check → run unit + integration + the Drupal e2e/live).

### Seam & fixture flow (ASCII)
```
            ┌─────────────── unit ───────────────┐   pure funcs, no I/O
            │                                     │
 monkeypatch│  run_terminus() / terminus()  ◄─────┤ integration (fault injection,
            │        │                            │   edge cases, bug regressions)
            ▼        ▼                            │
      ┌───────────────────┐                       │
      │  program logic    │                       │
      └───────────────────┘                       │
            ▲        ▲                            │
 PATH shim  │        │  real terminus (live)      │
 fake       │        │                            ▼
 `terminus` │        └──────────► e2e / live: full subprocess run of
            │                     ./pantheon-sitehealth-emails <site> --date …
            ▼                              │
     build/<site>.{html,txt,eml}  ─────────┼─► golden snapshots (syrupy, CIDs/Date normalized)
                                           └─► render tier (Playwright loads .html from disk)
```

### Safety interlock (Prime Directive: zero silent failures)
A `run_program(args)` helper is the **only** sanctioned way to invoke the program in tests. It
hard-fails (raises, never silently) if `--all`, `-a`, or `--for-real` appears in argv. This
interlock is itself covered by a test. When the email tier activates, an analogous guard will
assert the recipient is the GMail test identity, never a customer address.

### run-tests wrapper (thin)
`./run-tests` wraps pytest: default `--human` (rich); `--llm` (terse, `-q`, no color,
failures-first, machine-parseable summary via a small conftest hook); `--fast` (offline
subset); `--record` (refresh `fixtures/terminus/` from the live test sites); `--update-goldens`
(syrupy update); `--coverage` (pytest-cov, no gate); passes through `-m`/`-k`/paths.

### Determinism notes (for goldens)
Normalize/strip volatile bits before snapshotting: `make_msgid` CIDs, the `Date:` header, and
embedded PNG bytes (assert charts *exist* rather than byte-compare matplotlib output). Fix
`--date` and seed the DB so traffic-derived output is stable.

### Property tests (honest scope)
Hypothesis targets genuinely pure/extractable functions (`fix_drush_output`, `escape_url`,
traffic aggregation). The plan-recommendation cost model is currently **inline in `main()`
(`:3095-3211`)** — SPEC.md flags a small optional extraction to a pure `recommend_plan(...)`
function as the enabler; if not extracted now, that math is instead pinned via parametrized
e2e cases.

## Smoke coverage the harness must ship with (proves the harness works — not the full suite)
- 1 **unit** (e.g. `fix_drush_output` / `escape_url`).
- 1 **integration** (monkeypatched `run_terminus` + temp sqlite DB + a check hook).
- 1 **e2e** (shim `terminus`, full subprocess run, asserts `build/<site>.eml` produced).
- 1 **live** (real `terminus self:info` or read-only `env:info` on `its-wws-test1`).
- 1 **render** (Playwright loads a committed sample `build/*.html`, asserts key elements + no console errors).
- 1 **email** (scaffolded, skipped/deferred).
- 2 **bug regressions** (the `terminus()` retry tuple bug; the `check/umich` `sc.console` bug) — plus the fixes.
- 1 **interlock** test (`run_program` refuses `--all`/`--for-real`).

## Documentation updates (instructions to include in SPEC.md, executed at implementation time)
- **README.md:** add a "Testing" section (install `.[test]` + `playwright install chromium`;
  `run-tests` modes/tiers; live vs `--fast`; `--record`, `--update-goldens`, `--coverage`).
  Retire the two TODO bullets.
- **CLAUDE.md:** add testing conventions — the importability seam, the `run_terminus`/`php`
  mock seams, the `--all`/`--for-real` interlock, fixture/golden refresh commands, and the
  standing policy "design + implement appropriate tests for each change."
- **tests/README.md:** dev-facing detail (layout, marks, writing a new test, recording fixtures).
- **docs/**: **no** testing docs — `docs/` is end-user only, per the repo convention.
- **pyproject.toml:** add `[project.optional-dependencies] test = [...]`,
  `[tool.pytest.ini_options]` (markers, testpaths), `[tool.coverage.run]` (source points at the
  extension-less script).

## Acceptance criteria for the harness (SPEC.md states these as the "done" bar)
- `uv pip install .[test] && playwright install chromium` succeeds.
- `./run-tests --fast` is green offline (unit + shim e2e + render on committed HTML), no network.
- `./run-tests` is green including live read-only smoke against `its-wws-test1/2` — provably
  never using `--all`/`--for-real`.
- One passing smoke test per tier (list above); the two bug fixes + regressions pass; the
  interlock test passes.
- `./run-tests --llm` emits terse, machine-parseable output; `--coverage` reports coverage
  (no gate); `--update-goldens` regenerates snapshots and a re-run is green.
- Seam-refactor byte-identity check passes for `its-wws-test1` (volatile bits normalized).

## SPEC.md structure (what the deliverable contains, per PROMPT methodology)
Full spec including: the three approaches considered (black-box-only; hybrid; full-refactor-now)
scored 0–1 on Correctness / Completeness / Ability-to-implement / Maintainability / Clarity,
with the hybrid selected and refined to ≥0.9 on each; the architecture above with ASCII
diagrams for tier pyramid, seam/fixture flow, and the `run-tests` decision tree; the shadow-path
and edge-case analysis (nil/empty/upstream-error for each new data flow; user-interrupt, slow
connection, stale fixture for interactions); concrete acceptance criteria; and the doc-update
instructions. Everything deferred (GMail activation, CI next year, plan-rec extraction) is
written down explicitly.

## Execution steps once this plan is approved (produces the deliverable — NOT the harness)
1. Write `development/2026-07-04-test-harness/SPEC.md` per the structure above.
2. Run the adversarial review: dispatch a fresh reviewer subagent (no brainstorming context)
   to score SPEC.md 1–10 across Completeness / Consistency / Clarity / Scope / Feasibility and
   list issues; fix issues on disk; re-dispatch (max 3 iterations; convergence guard →
   persist unresolved items as "## Reviewer Concerns"). If the subagent is unavailable, skip
   and note "Spec review unavailable — presenting unreviewed doc."
3. Report the review result (rounds survived, issues fixed, score) and present SPEC.md.
4. **Stop.** Do not write any test code or modify `pantheon-sitehealth-emails` — that is the
   next prompt.

## Verification of the deliverable
- `SPEC.md` exists in `development/2026-07-04-test-harness/`, follows the archive convention,
  and contains all sections above (three scored approaches, diagrams, acceptance criteria,
  doc-update instructions, deferred-items list).
- The adversarial-review loop ran (or was explicitly reported unavailable), with the final
  score and any "Reviewer Concerns" recorded in the document.
- No source files changed; no test code written (this task is design-only).

## Explicitly NOT in scope (deferred, written down)
- Building the `tests/` tree, the `run-tests` wrapper, shims, fixtures, or any test code.
- The importability seam refactor and the two bug fixes (specified here, implemented later).
- Re-enabling SMTP; implementing SendGrid; activating the GMail email tier.
- Regenerating `fqdns.json` / the 24-hour staleness handling.
- CI/CD (planned next year; the design keeps tests CI-portable so adding it later is trivial).
- Performance/parallel-check testing.
```

316	def terminus(*args) -> Any:
317	    """
318	    Run Terminus with the given arguments and return the result as a JSON object.
319	    """
320	    retry = True
321	    if "pshe-no-retry" in args:
322	        del args["pshe-no-retry"]
323	        retry = False
324	    command = [*args, "--format=json"]
325	    output, errors, fatal = run_terminus(command)
326	    try:
327	        result = json.loads(output)
328	    except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
329	        result = ""  # TODO: set to None
330	        errors += "\n" + output + "\n" + str(e)
331	    if errors != "":
332	        sc.console.print(f"[bold red]Terminus error: {errors}")
333	        if retry and "Invalid or expired session header: X-Pantheon-Session" in errors:
334	            sc.console.print("Sleeping for 5 seconds and then retrying...")
335	            time.sleep(5)
336	            args.push("pshe-no-retry")
337	            return terminus(*args)
338	    # return result, errors.strip(), fatal  # TODO

342	def wp(siteenv: str, *args) -> (Any, str):
343	    """
344	    Run a "wp eval" command through Terminus and return the result as JSON.
345	    """
346	    command = ["wp", siteenv, "--", *args, "--format=json"]
347	    output, errors, fatal = run_terminus(command)
348	    try:
349	        result = json.loads(output)
350	    except json.JSONDecodeError as e:
351	        result = None
352	        errors += "\n" + output + "\n" + str(e)
353	    return result, errors.strip(), fatal
354

357	    """
358	    Run a "wp eval" command through Terminus and return the result as a string.
359	    """
360	    command = ["wp", siteenv, "--", "eval", *args]

## Assistant

All three load-bearing claims verified against current source:
- **`terminus()` retry (lines 320-337):** doubly broken — `del args["pshe-no-retry"]` indexes a tuple with a string (`TypeError`), and `args.push(...)` calls a nonexistent method on a tuple (`AttributeError`). The retry path crashes if ever reached.
- **`check/umich/__init__.py:11`:** `sc.console('...')` treats the rich `Console` as callable — should be `sc.console.print(...)`.
- **Disabled send (3627-3631):** confirmed commented out; `.eml` written at 3624.

```json
{
  "file_path": "/workspace/development/2026-07-04-test-harness/SPEC.md",
  "content": "# SPEC — Test Harness for `pantheon-sitehealth-emails`\n\n> **Status:** Design approved 2026-07-04. This document specifies the test *harness* (plus\n> initial smoke tests). It is a decision record and an implementation brief for a later\n> session — **not** primary documentation of how the program works.\n>\n> **Scope of the implementation this spec authorizes:** build the harness (runner, fixtures,\n> mocking utilities, shims, marks, the `run-tests` wrapper), apply one minimal\n> importability refactor, fix the confirmed bugs with regressions, and ship one smoke test\n> per tier. It does **not** authorize the full test suite (a later stage), re-enabling SMTP,\n> or implementing SendGrid.\n\n---\n\n## 1. Purpose\n\nThe program has **zero tests, zero CI, no test tooling** (confirmed: no `tests/`, no\n`conftest.py`, no `pytest` dependency, no `.github/`; `README.md`'s top two TODOs are \"test\nharness\" and \"test suite\"). Major changes are queued next — a large modularization of the\n~3,700-line monolith, moving logic into the plugin/config framework, and re-enabling SMTP +\nadding SendGrid.\n\nThe harness is the **safety net built first**, so those changes are made against a suite that\nproves the code still works as designed. The immediate intent (verbatim from the task): *ensure\nthat all code works as designed and continues to work as designed even in the face of other,\nmajor planned future changes and the addition of new features.*\n\n---\n\n## 2. Hard constraints (govern design and every run, now and forever)\n\n| # | Constraint | Enforcement |\n|---|---|---|\n| C1 | **NEVER** run the program with `--all` / `-a` (can take ~6 h). | A `run_program()` interlock raises before exec if `--all`/`-a` appears; covered by a test. |\n| C2 | **NEVER** run the program with `--for-real` (can email real customers). | Same interlock also refuses `--for-real`; covered by a test. |\n| C3 | Tests target only `its-wws-test1` (WordPress), `its-wws-test2` (Drupal), or a deliberately chosen real site — all **read-only**. | Live-tier fixtures hardcode these site names; no write/deploy Terminus verbs are ever issued. |\n| C4 | Do **not** re-enable the disabled SMTP send block (lines 3627-3631). | No test un-comments it; the email round-trip tier stays skipped until SMTP/SendGrid lands. |\n| C5 | Do **not** touch the `fqdns.json` 24-h staleness check. | Only reachable under `--all`, which C1 forbids; irrelevant to tests. |\n\nThese constraints are accepted to produce coverage gaps (e.g. the `--all` aggregation path and\nreal email delivery are untestable now). The gaps are listed in §13.\n\n---\n\n## 3. Current state (facts verified against source on 2026-07-04)\n\nAll line numbers are in the main script `pantheon-sitehealth-emails` (3,673 lines, shebang\n`#!/usr/bin/env python`, **no `.py` extension**) unless noted.\n\n- **One golden subprocess seam.** Every Pantheon/WP/Drush interaction funnels through\n  `run_terminus(command, input_data=None) -> (str, str, bool)` (`:226`), which uses\n  `subprocess.Popen` in argument-list form (no `shell=True`), with a 300 s\n  `communicate(timeout=…)`. Above it: `terminus()` (`:316`), `wp()`/`wp_eval()` (`:342`/`:356`),\n  `drush()`/`drush_php_script()` (`:413`/`:428`). WP and Drush are dispatched *as* Terminus\n  subcommands (`terminus wp …`, `terminus drush …`), so a single fake `terminus` covers all three.\n- **Second, independent subprocess seam.** The CSS inliner\n  `subprocess.run([\"php\", \"inline-styles.php\", <in>, <out>], check=True)` (`:3554`). `php` is\n  local, deterministic, fast → tests use **real php**, no shim.\n- **No direct HTTP to Pantheon.** No `requests`/`httpx`/`urllib.request` for Pantheon; auth is\n  delegated to the Terminus binary. The only auth logic in-script is the (broken) session-expiry\n  retry in `terminus()`.\n- **Other genuine network seams** (only when their plugin is enabled in config):\n  `dns.resolver.resolve` (`:1218`/`:1248`) in the FQDN/Cloudflare check; the Cloudflare SDK\n  `Cloudflare(...).ips.list()` (`plugin/cloudflare/ips.py`); boto3 Secrets Manager\n  (`plugin/aws/get_secret.py`). Test configs disable these plugins unless a test targets them.\n- **Email send is disabled.** Lines 3627-3631 are commented out; the program's only email output\n  today is `build/<site>.eml` (written unconditionally at `:3624`) plus `build/<site>.{html,txt}`\n  and the inlined `-inline2.html`. **Tests assert on artifacts, never on SMTP.**\n- **Import-time side effects.** `build`+`parse_args()` run at module scope\n  (`:141-219`, ending `sc.options = args_parser.parse_args()`); the file has no `.py` extension.\n  Importing it today parses live `sys.argv`. SQLAlchemy models (`Base`, `PantheonTraffic`,\n  `PantheonOverageProtection`) are defined at import (`:93-135`).\n- **DB is config-injectable.** Engine built at `:818-836` purely from `sc.config[\"Database\"]`\n  (`sqlite:///{name}` or `mysql+mysqldb://…`). `--create-tables` runs\n  `Base.metadata.create_all` then `sys.exit`.\n- **Global mutable state** in `script_context.py` (imported everywhere as `sc`):\n  `options, config, plugin, check, news, console, substitutions, hooks, plugin_context`, plus\n  `icon` and a configured `text_maker` (html2text). Must be reset between in-process tests.\n- **Genuinely pure / directly unit-testable today:** `escape_url` (`:222`),\n  `fix_drush_output` (`:391`), `wp_error` (`:365`), `drush_error` (`:443`),\n  `check_wordpress_plugin` (`:533`, logic + stdout), `check_drupal_module` (`:601`, logic +\n  stdout), and `sc.add_notice`/`sc.add_news_item` (`script_context.py:65`/`:80`).\n- **Tooling on hand:** Python 3.13 via uv (`pyproject.toml requires-python >=3.11`; deps `rich,\n  SQLAlchemy, matplotlib, Jinja2, dnspython, html2text, semver`; extras `mysql/aws/cloudflare`);\n  Node 24; PHP + Composer (`pelago/emogrifier ^7.2`); Terminus authenticated; **dev-container\n  firewall is OFF and will stay off** (network + Pantheon auth always available).\n\n### 3.1 Confirmed bugs to fix now (with regressions) — re-verified against source\n\n1. **`terminus()` session-expiry retry is doubly broken (`:320-337`).** `*args` is a *tuple*, yet\n   the retry path does `del args[\"pshe-no-retry\"]` (indexing a tuple with a `str` → `TypeError`)\n   and `args.push(\"pshe-no-retry\")` (`.push` is not a tuple/list method → `AttributeError`). Any\n   time Pantheon returns `Invalid or expired session header: X-Pantheon-Session`, this path is\n   entered and **crashes** instead of retrying.\n2. **`check/umich/__init__.py:11`** `else` branch calls `sc.console('…')` — `sc.console` is a\n   rich `Console` instance; the callable form raises `TypeError`. Should be `sc.console.print(…)`.\n   Reached whenever the `[UMich]` plugin is loaded but not `enabled`.\n\nBoth are fixed as part of harness implementation, each pinned by a regression test (§9).\n\n---\n\n## 4. Approaches considered and evaluated\n\nThree approaches were weighed. Scores are 0–1 on Correctness, Completeness, Ability-to-implement,\nMaintainability, Clarity (the task's quality-control axes). \"Correctness\" here = *does the\napproach actually catch the regressions we care about*; \"Completeness\" = *coverage breadth\nachievable*.\n\n### Approach A — Black-box only (zero source changes)\nRun the script as a subprocess with a fake `terminus` on PATH; assert on `build/` artifacts,\nexit codes, stdout. No code touched before a suite exists.\n\n| Axis | Score | Note |\n|---|---|---|\n| Correctness | 0.80 | Catches end-to-end breakage but blind to internal-logic regressions. |\n| Completeness | 0.55 | Cannot unit-test pure functions, fault-inject `run_terminus`, or exercise the retry/error paths deterministically. |\n| Ability-to-implement | 0.95 | Simplest; no refactor risk. |\n| Maintainability | 0.70 | Every test pays subprocess cost; failures are coarse (\"artifact differs\") and hard to localize. |\n| Clarity | 0.85 | Simple mental model. |\n\n**Rejected:** Completeness 0.55 — the upcoming modularization refactor will move internal logic\naround, and a black-box-only net can't localize what broke.\n\n### Approach B — Full unit-test refactor now\nAggressively split the monolith into importable modules, then unit-test broadly.\n\n| Axis | Score | Note |\n|---|---|---|\n| Correctness | 0.75 | The large diff *before* a safety net risks introducing the very regressions we're trying to prevent. |\n| Completeness | 0.95 | Highest achievable coverage. |\n| Ability-to-implement | 0.55 | Large, risky diff; contradicts \"don't break things before tests.\" |\n| Maintainability | 0.90 | Clean long-term. |\n| Clarity | 0.80 | Big conceptual change up front. |\n\n**Rejected:** Ability-to-implement 0.55 and Correctness 0.75 — it inverts the plan's ordering\n(net first, refactor second) and front-loads the biggest risk.\n\n### Approach C — Hybrid: minimal importability seam + both mock styles ✅ SELECTED\nOne tiny, behavior-preserving change makes the module importable (§5.1). Then: monkeypatch\n`run_terminus`/`terminus` for fast in-process unit/integration tests, **and** a PATH-shim fake\n`terminus` for deterministic full-script e2e, **and** live tiers that run real Terminus read-only\nagainst the test sites (the default per the live-first decision).\n\n| Axis | Score (pre-refine) | Refined | Note |\n|---|---|---|---|\n| Correctness | 0.90 | **0.95** | Localizes regressions at unit + integration level; live tier catches real API drift. |\n| Completeness | 0.88 | **0.92** | Covers pure logic, error/edge injection, full pipeline, rendering, and real integration. Gaps only where C1–C4 forbid. |\n| Ability-to-implement | 0.90 | **0.93** | One ~15-line refactor is the only source change; everything else is additive test code. |\n| Maintainability | 0.88 | **0.92** | Fast inner loop (monkeypatch) + realistic outer loop (live/shim); golden/fixture refresh scripted. |\n| Clarity | 0.90 | **0.94** | Explicit tiers and one sanctioned invocation path. |\n\n**Refinements applied to reach ≥0.90 on every axis:** (a) added the `run_program()` safety\ninterlock so C1/C2 can never be violated even by a mistaken test; (b) added golden-output\nnormalization rules (§5.9) so rendering snapshots are stable despite volatile CIDs/dates; (c)\nscoped property testing honestly to pure/extractable functions (§5.10); (d) specified `sc`-state\nreset (§5.2) so in-process tests don't leak global state; (e) pinned a byte-identity verification\ngate for the seam refactor (§5.1) so \"behavior-preserving\" is *proven*, not asserted.\n\n**Selected: Approach C (Hybrid).**\n\n---\n\n## 5. Architecture\n\n### 5.0 Framework choices (and why, over alternatives)\n- **pytest** — the spine. Fixtures, marks, `parametrize`, and the richest plugin ecosystem.\n  *Rejected:* `unittest` (verbose, weak fixtures/parametrization), `nose2` (unmaintained).\n- **syrupy** — golden/snapshot assertions for rendered reports, with `--snapshot-update`.\n- **Hypothesis** — property-based tests for pure math.\n- **pytest-cov** — coverage measurement (reported, **no gate**).\n- **pytest-playwright** (Python Playwright) — the browser render tier. One language, one runner;\n  it manages its own Chromium (`playwright install chromium`); firewall is off so the download\n  works. *Rejected:* a separate Node/Puppeteer toolchain (second language + second runner for\n  no gain).\n- **PHP:** no PHP test framework. `inline-styles.php` is a pure file-in/file-out transform,\n  exercised via subprocess with sample HTML and a golden output.\n\n### 5.1 The minimal seam refactor (the only source change, behavior-preserving)\nMake the module importable without executing argparse at import:\n\n```python\ndef build_arg_parser() -> argparse.ArgumentParser:\n    p = argparse.ArgumentParser(...)\n    ...   # every existing add_argument call, unchanged\n    return p\n\ndef parse_args(argv=None):\n    return build_arg_parser().parse_args(argv)\n\n# bottom of file:\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    sc.options = parse_args()\n    main()\n```\n\n- Functions read `sc.options` at *call* time, so relocating the `parse_args()` call into the\n  `__main__` guard is safe: a test imports the module (no argv parsing), sets `sc.options` to a\n  parsed namespace or a fake, then calls functions or `main()`.\n- **No rename.** `./pantheon-sitehealth-emails` still runs exactly as documented. The\n  extension-less file is loaded in tests via `importlib.util.spec_from_file_location` +\n  `SourceFileLoader`, once, cached by a session-scoped fixture (§5.2) to avoid re-registering the\n  SQLAlchemy models.\n- **Verification gate (proves \"behavior-preserving\"):** for `its-wws-test1` at a fixed `--date`,\n  the pre-refactor and post-refactor `build/` artifacts must be identical after normalizing the\n  known-volatile bits (§5.9). This diff is run once during implementation and recorded in the\n  handoff notes; it is not a standing test (it needs a live run).\n\n```\n   argv ──► build_arg_parser() ──► parse_args(argv) ──► sc.options\n                                          ▲                  │\n   test: import module (no parse) ────────┘                  ▼\n   test: sc.options = fake/parsed ───────────────────► call any function / main()\n```\n\n### 5.2 Global-state isolation\n`script_context.py` holds process-global mutable state. A `conftest.py` autouse fixture\nsnapshots and restores, per test: `sc.options, sc.config, sc.news, sc.hooks, sc.substitutions,\nsc.plugin, sc.check, sc.plugin_context`. The module-load fixture is **session-scoped** (import\nonce); the state-reset fixture is **function-scoped** (fresh state each test). Plugin/check\nself-registration is an import side effect gated by config flags — tests that need a plugin\nregistered import the relevant package *after* setting a config that enables it, inside an\nisolated `sc` state.\n\n### 5.3 Directory layout\n```\ntests/\n  conftest.py          # module-load fixture, sc-reset, temp cwd+build, temp sqlite,\n                       #   config-fixture loader, run_program() interlock, --llm reporter hook\n  README.md            # dev-facing testing docs (NOT docs/, which is end-user only)\n  fixtures/\n    config/            # minimal.toml, full.toml — self-contained; NEVER depend on the private config symlink\n    terminus/          # recorded JSON keyed by argv: org:site:list, env:info, env:metrics, wp plugin list, drush pm:list …\n    db/                # seed PantheonTraffic / PantheonOverageProtection rows\n    html/              # committed sample build/*.html for the render tier (no live run needed)\n  shims/\n    terminus           # fake executable: maps argv → fixtures/terminus/<key>.json, prints it\n  __snapshots__/       # syrupy golden baselines (rendered reports, normalized)\n  unit/                # pure funcs: fix_drush_output, escape_url, notices, config_substitution, plan-rec math\n  integration/         # in-process; run_terminus monkeypatched (or live); temp DB; check hooks; the 2 bug regressions\n  e2e/                 # full-script subprocess runs: shim-backed (deterministic) + live (default)\n  render/              # pytest-playwright: load build/*.html from disk, assert structure + zero console errors\n  email/               # GMail round-trip — scaffolded, @pytest.mark.skip(reason=…), see §11\nrun-tests              # thin wrapper over pytest (executable)\n```\n\n### 5.4 Test tiers & marks\nRegistered marks: `unit`, `integration`, `e2e`, `live`, `render`, `email`, `slow`.\n\n- **Default `./run-tests` includes live tiers** (live-first decision: real Terminus read-only\n  against the test sites is the primary confidence signal).\n- **`./run-tests --fast`** selects the offline subset `-m \"not live and not slow\"` for the inner\n  loop (unit + shim-backed integration/e2e + render on committed HTML) — fully offline,\n  deterministic.\n- Claude Code selects the relevant subset per change (e.g. a Drupal-check edit → `unit` +\n  `integration` + the Drupal `e2e`/`live` cases via `-k drupal`).\n\n```\n                 ▲ realism / cost\n      live       │  real terminus, read-only, its-wws-test1/2   (default; slow; catches API drift)\n      e2e        │  full subprocess run, shim terminus + real php (deterministic pipeline)\n      integration│  in-process, run_terminus monkeypatched, temp DB, check hooks (fault injection)\n      render     │  Playwright over build/*.html from disk (rendering correctness)\n      unit       │  pure functions, no I/O                        (fast; many; localizes bugs)\n                 ▼ speed / count\n```\n\n### 5.5 External-tool interception (both styles)\n- **Monkeypatch (unit/integration):** patch `run_terminus` (and/or `terminus`) on the loaded\n  module to return canned `(stdout, stderr, fatal)` or raise/inject faults — the deterministic\n  way to exercise error paths: `fatal=True` timeouts, malformed JSON (`json.JSONDecodeError`),\n  and the expired-session retry. This is the primary seam because all Pantheon I/O funnels\n  through it.\n- **PATH-shim fake `terminus` (e2e):** `tests/shims/terminus` is prepended to `PATH`; it reads a\n  manifest mapping the invoked argv to a `fixtures/terminus/*.json` file and prints it. Real\n  `php` is used (local, fast). This exercises the *real* subprocess/argument-building path and\n  the full render→MIME→`.eml` pipeline without network.\n- **Live (default):** no interception — real `terminus` runs read-only against `its-wws-test1/2`.\n\n### 5.6 DB fixtures\nA `temp_db` fixture points `sc.config[\"Database\"]` at `type=\"sqlite\", name=<tmp file>`, runs\n`Base.metadata.create_all`, and seeds rows from `fixtures/db/`. In-process tests of DB-touching\nhelpers get a live SQLAlchemy session bound to that temp engine. No test touches the repo's real\n`database.db`.\n\n### 5.7 Config fixtures\n`fixtures/config/minimal.toml` (plan_info, plan_sku_to_name, `[Database]` sqlite, `[News]` →\ntemp folder, **all plugins disabled**) and `full.toml` (umich/cloudflare/aws enabled, with those\nexternal calls mocked) let tests run without the private, symlinked production config. **No test\ndepends on the symlinked `pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml`.**\n\n### 5.8 The `run-tests` wrapper (thin)\nExecutable wrapping pytest. Flags:\n\n| Flag | Effect |\n|---|---|\n| (none) | `--human`: default rich pytest output, all tiers incl. live. |\n| `--llm` | terse, `-q`, `--tb=short`, no color, failures-first, plus a machine-parseable summary line emitted by a conftest `pytest_terminal_summary` hook (counts + `FAILED <nodeid>` list, no fluff). |\n| `--fast` | offline subset (`-m \"not live and not slow\"`). |\n| `--record` | refresh `fixtures/terminus/` from the live test sites (read-only). |\n| `--update-goldens` | pass `--snapshot-update` to syrupy. |\n| `--coverage` | enable pytest-cov (reported, no gate). |\n| passthrough | `-m`, `-k`, and paths forwarded to pytest. |\n\n```\n        ./run-tests\n             │\n   ┌─────────┼───────────┬───────────┬──────────────┬───────────┐\n default   --llm       --fast     --record      --update-       --coverage\n (human)  (terse,    (offline   (real         goldens          (pytest-cov,\n  all      machine    subset)   terminus,     (syrupy           no gate)\n tiers)    summary)             read-only)     update)\n```\n\n### 5.9 Determinism / golden normalization\nBefore snapshotting `build/<site>.{html,txt}` and `-inline2.html`, normalize volatile content:\n- **`make_msgid` CIDs** (`:3505-3506`, `domain=\"webservices.umich.edu\"`) → replace with a\n  stable placeholder.\n- **`Date:` header** in the `.eml` → strip/normalize.\n- **matplotlib PNG bytes** (chart, SiteLens gauges) → do **not** byte-compare; assert the inline\n  image parts *exist* with the expected CIDs/content-types. (Matplotlib output is not\n  byte-stable across versions/backends; force the `Agg` backend for determinism of *presence*.)\n- Fix `--date` and seed the DB so all traffic-derived text is stable.\n\n### 5.10 Property-based testing (honest scope)\nHypothesis targets genuinely pure/deterministic functions: `fix_drush_output` (string→(str,str)),\n`escape_url`, and the day/month **traffic aggregation** helper. The **plan-recommendation cost\nmodel is currently inline in `main()` (`:3095-3211`)** and is not directly callable. SPEC records\ntwo options, chosen at implementation time:\n- (preferred) a *small* pure extraction `recommend_plan(traffic, plan_info, current_plan) -> …`\n  that `main()` then calls — enabling direct property tests; or\n- (fallback) pin the math via `parametrize`d e2e cases with fixed traffic fixtures, no extraction.\nThe extraction is the only candidate to pull a later-stage refactor forward, and only if it\nstays small and behavior-preserving (task permits this \"only as necessary\").\n\n### 5.11 Safety interlock (Prime Directive #1: zero silent failures)\n`run_program(args: list[str], **kw)` in `conftest.py` is the **only** sanctioned way tests invoke\nthe program. Before exec it asserts none of `--all`, `-a`, `--for-real` is present and **raises\n`ForbiddenFlagError`** (a named exception, not a bare assert, not a silent skip) otherwise. It is\nitself covered by a test that feeds it each forbidden flag and asserts the raise. When the email\ntier activates, an analogous guard asserts the recipient is the GMail test identity, never a\ncustomer address.\n\n---\n\n## 6. Shadow-path & edge-case analysis (Prime Directives #2–#4)\n\nFor each **new** data flow the harness introduces, the happy path plus three shadow paths\n(nil / empty / upstream-error) are traced; named exceptions are specified.\n\n| New flow | Happy | Nil input | Empty input | Upstream error |\n|---|---|---|---|---|\n| Fake `terminus` shim reads manifest | argv → fixture JSON printed | argv not in manifest → exit non-zero + stderr `no fixture for: <argv>` (never silent empty) | empty fixture file → shim prints `{}`; test asserts caller handles empty JSON | corrupt fixture → shim exits 1; e2e test sees non-zero exit and fails loudly |\n| Monkeypatched `run_terminus` | returns seeded `(out,\"\",False)` | `out=None` guard → test asserts `json.loads` path raises `JSONDecodeError`, caught at `:328` | `out=\"\"` → `terminus()` sets `result=\"\"` (current behavior) — pinned by test | inject `fatal=True` → assert caller treats as fatal |\n| `terminus()` retry (post-fix) | expired-session once → retry → success | — | — | expired-session twice → no infinite loop (sentinel honored); asserted |\n| `temp_db` seed | rows inserted, queried | no rows → report path with zero traffic renders without crash (asserts empty-traffic handling) | empty seed file → create_all only, no rows | bad DSN → `create_engine` raises; test asserts named failure |\n| Golden snapshot | normalized HTML matches baseline | missing baseline → syrupy reports \"snapshot not found\" (run `--update-goldens`) | empty render → test fails (report must have content) | template error → Jinja2 raises; test asserts render fails loudly |\n| Render tier (Playwright) | page loads, key selectors present, zero console errors | missing HTML file → test fails with path | empty HTML → assertion on required elements fails | browser launch failure → pytest-playwright errors (not skipped silently) |\n\n**Interaction edge cases (Prime Directive #4):** user interrupts a live run (Ctrl-C) → pytest\nreports KeyboardInterrupt, no partial artifact is asserted as success; slow Pantheon → live tests\ninherit the program's 300 s Terminus timeout and are marked `slow`; stale fixture → `--record`\nrefreshes, and a fixture's provenance/date is recorded in a header comment so staleness is visible.\n\n**Catch-all smell (Prime Directive #2):** the harness itself uses **named** exceptions\n(`ForbiddenFlagError`, `FixtureNotFoundError`); it must not wrap test bodies in bare\n`except Exception`. The program's own broad handling (e.g. `terminus()` swallowing\n`JSONDecodeError` into `result=\"\"`) is *documented and pinned* by tests, not \"fixed\" here beyond\nthe two confirmed bugs — behavior changes belong to the later refactor.\n\n---\n\n## 7. Best practices baked in\n- **Test pyramid** (many fast unit, fewer integration, fewest e2e/live) — §5.4.\n- **One sanctioned invocation path** with a fail-closed safety interlock — §5.11.\n- **Golden/snapshot testing** with explicit volatile-field normalization — §5.9.\n- **Fixtures recorded from reality, refreshable by one command** (`--record`), with provenance\n  headers so they don't rot silently — §5.8, §6.\n- **Dual-audience output** (human default, `--llm` terse/parseable) — §5.5/§5.8; both are\n  LLM-friendly (a human pasting a failure into Claude Code gets clean, localizable output).\n- **CI-portable by construction:** everything is pytest + marks; adding GitHub Actions later is a\n  workflow file that runs `run-tests --fast` (offline) plus, optionally, a credentialed live job.\n  (CI itself is out of scope — §13.)\n- **Coverage measured, never chased** (no gate) — §5.0.\n\n---\n\n## 8. Maintenance strategy (keep tests relevant as the program changes)\n- **Standing policy** (added to CLAUDE.md): every change designs + implements appropriate tests\n  at the time the change is made (the program is not adopting TDD; tests follow the change).\n- **Fixture provenance + refresh:** each recorded fixture carries a `// recorded <date> from\n  <site> via <terminus argv>` header; `run-tests --record` regenerates the set; a fixture older\n  than a chosen horizon prints a notice when used in a live-diff check.\n- **Goldens updated deliberately:** rendering changes require `--update-goldens` and show up as a\n  reviewable snapshot diff — unintended rendering drift fails loudly.\n- **Reusable prompt templates** (stored in this feature folder for later stages, not executed\n  now): `add-tests-for-change.prompt.md` (design+add tests for a diff) and\n  `refresh-fixtures.prompt.md` (re-record + update goldens, review the diff). These make routine\n  test maintenance a repeatable Claude Code task.\n\n---\n\n## 9. Smoke tests the harness ships with (prove the harness works — NOT the suite)\n| Tier | Smoke test | Asserts |\n|---|---|---|\n| unit | `fix_drush_output` / `escape_url` | pure input→output; no I/O. |\n| integration | monkeypatched `run_terminus` + `temp_db` + a `check` hook | in-process pipeline step works; state isolated. |\n| e2e | shim `terminus`, full subprocess run for one site + fixed `--date` | `build/<site>.eml`, `.html`, `.txt` produced; exit 0. |\n| live | real `terminus self:info` (or read-only `env:info` on `its-wws-test1`) | Terminus auth + JSON parse work end-to-end. |\n| render | Playwright loads a committed `fixtures/html/*.html` | key elements present; **zero console errors**. |\n| email | scaffolded round-trip | `@pytest.mark.skip(\"email send disabled until SMTP/SendGrid\")` — imports/collects cleanly. |\n| regression | `terminus()` expired-session retry | with the fix, one retry then success; no crash, no infinite loop. |\n| regression | `check/umich` `else` branch | with the fix, prints via `sc.console.print`, no `TypeError`. |\n| interlock | `run_program([\"--all\"])`, `[\"-a\"]`, `[\"--for-real\"]` | each raises `ForbiddenFlagError`. |\n\nThe two bug **fixes** land with their regressions (the tests would fail on today's code and pass\nafter the fix).\n\n---\n\n## 10. (reserved)\n\n---\n\n## 11. GMail email round-trip tier — design (deferred, scaffolded, skipped)\nCannot run today (C4: send is disabled; SendGrid unimplemented). Scaffolded now so it activates\nthe moment email sending lands.\n\n- **Auth:** Gmail API + an OAuth refresh token (or a service account with domain-wide delegation)\n  stored as a secret (env var / AWS Secrets Manager, matching the program's own secret story).\n  No account password in the harness. Scopes: read + search (to detect bounce/rejection/\n  undeliverable notices) — send happens via the program under test, not the harness.\n- **Identity:** sender and recipient are the **same** GMail test account, so delivery *and* error\n  notices land in one inbox. A guard asserts the recipient is that test identity (never a\n  customer), mirroring §5.11.\n- **Flow (when active):** program sends → poll the inbox by a unique per-run subject/token for a\n  few minutes → assert receipt → scan for error notices (unknown sender / undeliverable /\n  rejected / spam) → optionally load the received HTML in Playwright to check GMail rendering\n  (GMail strips a subset of HTML/CSS/JS and may gate remote content / truncate long messages —\n  handle those states before asserting content).\n- **State today:** the test file exists and imports cleanly but is `@pytest.mark.skip`ped with a\n  reason pointing at the SMTP/SendGrid milestone.\n\n```\n [program under test] --send--> (GMail test acct) <--search-- [harness, Gmail API]\n                                       │                          │\n                                 error notices ──────────────► assert receipt + no errors\n                                       │\n                                 received HTML ─► Playwright ─► GMail-render assertions\n```\n\n---\n\n## 12. Documentation updates (performed during implementation)\n- **README.md:** add a **Testing** section — install (`uv pip install .[test]` +\n  `playwright install chromium`), `run-tests` modes/tiers, live vs `--fast`, `--record`,\n  `--update-goldens`, `--coverage`; **retire the two TODO bullets** (\"test harness\", \"test\n  suite\") or mark the harness done.\n- **CLAUDE.md:** add testing conventions that aren't obvious from the code — the importability\n  seam (module loads via `importlib`, `sc.options` set by caller), the two mock seams\n  (`run_terminus`, the `php` inliner), the `--all`/`--for-real` `run_program` interlock, the\n  fixture/golden refresh commands, and the standing \"tests accompany every change\" policy.\n- **tests/README.md** (new, dev-facing): layout, marks, how to write a new test in each tier,\n  how to record fixtures, determinism/normalization rules.\n- **docs/:** **no** testing docs added — `docs/` is end-user-only per the repo convention.\n- **pyproject.toml:** add `[project.optional-dependencies] test = [\"pytest\", \"syrupy\",\n  \"hypothesis\", \"pytest-cov\", \"pytest-playwright\"]`; `[tool.pytest.ini_options]` (markers,\n  `testpaths = [\"tests\"]`); `[tool.coverage.run]` with `source` pointing at the extension-less\n  script (coverage.py needs it named explicitly since it lacks a `.py` suffix).\n\n---\n\n## 13. Acceptance criteria (the \"done\" bar — exact commands + observable outcomes)\n1. `uv pip install .[test] && playwright install chromium` → exits 0.\n2. `./run-tests --fast` → green, **no network** (unit + shim e2e + render on committed HTML).\n3. `./run-tests` → green, including live read-only smoke against `its-wws-test1/2`; a grep of the\n   run + the interlock test **prove** `--all`/`--for-real` were never used.\n4. Exactly one passing smoke test per tier exists (§9 table); `email` collects but is skipped.\n5. The two bug fixes are in place; both regressions pass (and fail on the pre-fix code).\n6. The interlock test passes: `run_program` raises `ForbiddenFlagError` for `--all`, `-a`,\n   `--for-real`.\n7. `./run-tests --llm` emits terse, machine-parseable output (summary counts + `FAILED` nodeids,\n   no boilerplate).\n8. `./run-tests --coverage` reports coverage with **no threshold gate**.\n9. `./run-tests --update-goldens` regenerates snapshots; an immediate re-run is green.\n10. Seam-refactor byte-identity check passed for `its-wws-test1` at a fixed `--date` (volatile\n    bits normalized) and is recorded in the handoff notes.\n11. README/CLAUDE.md/tests-README/pyproject updates present (§12).\n\n---\n\n## 14. Deferred / explicitly NOT in scope (Prime Directive #7: written down)\n- The **full test suite** (only smoke-per-tier ships now).\n- **Re-enabling SMTP; implementing SendGrid; activating the GMail email tier** (C4).\n- The **large modularization refactor** and plugin/config migration (later stages). Only the\n  §5.1 importability seam — and, if kept tiny, the §5.10 `recommend_plan` extraction — may be\n  pulled forward, and only as necessary for testing.\n- **CI/CD** — next year; the design keeps everything CI-portable so it's a workflow file later.\n- **`fqdns.json` regeneration / 24-h staleness** (C5).\n- **Performance / parallel-check testing.**\n- **Coverage gaps accepted by C1–C4:** the `--all` aggregation + CSV/results-JSON path, real\n  SMTP delivery, and any customer-facing send path are untested by design.\n\n---\n\n## 15. Reviewer Concerns\n_(Populated only if the adversarial review leaves unresolved items after the iteration cap or a\nconvergence stop. Empty means the spec passed clean.)_\n"
}

Review ONLY the document on disk.\n\nRead `/workspace/development/2026-07-04-test-harness/SPEC.md` in full. It is a design specification for a **test harness** (not the full test suite) for a Python program called `pantheon-sitehealth-emails`. You may also read the actual code it references to check factual accuracy: the main script `/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails` (a ~3,700-line file with NO .py extension), `/workspace/script_context.py`, `/workspace/check/umich/__init__.py`, `/workspace/pyproject.toml`, and `/workspace/composer.json`. For each, output either **PASS** or a list of specific issues, each with a concrete suggested fix:\n1. **Completeness** — Are all requirements addressed? Missing edge cases or gaps the spec should have caught?\n2. **Consistency** — Do parts of the document agree with each other? Any contradictions (e.g. between decisions, the layout, acceptance criteria)?\n3. **Clarity** — Could an engineer implement the harness from this without asking questions? Any ambiguous language?\n4. **Scope** — Does the document creep beyond designing a *harness + smoke tests*? Any YAGNI violations, or conversely anything under-specified?\n5. **Feasibility** — Can this actually be built as described? Hidden complexity? Specifically scrutinize: (a) loading an extension-less file via importlib and whether SQLAlchemy model re-registration or matplotlib import causes problems; (b) whether coverage.py can measure an extension-less script; (c) whether the golden-snapshot normalization of CIDs/dates/PNGs is actually workable; (d) whether the claimed \"genuinely pure\" functions and the plan-recommendation extraction are as described; (e) whether the `run_program` interlock and live-first defaults are coherent.\n\nKey context to judge against (the spec's own stated scope):\n- Deliverable is the harness + ONE smoke test per tier, NOT a full suite.\n- Two hard constraints: never run the program with `--all` or `--for-real`.\n- Live tests (real Terminus, read-only) are the DEFAULT; offline/mocked tests only where clearly beneficial. The dev-container firewall is off.\n- Bugs found are to be fixed now with regressions.\n- Email round-trip testing is deferred/scaffolded because email send is disabled.\n\nAt the very end, output a single overall **quality score from 1 to 10** and a one-line verdict. Be genuinely critical — your job is to catch problems before implementation, not to rubber-stamp. If it's solid, say so, but find the real weaknesses.",

### ↳ Tool result

```
I've verified the load-bearing claims against source. The spec is unusually accurate — every line number I spot-checked was correct (bugs at `terminus()` :320-337 and `check/umich/__init__.py:11`; `run_terminus` :226 with 300s timeout and no `shell=True`; disabled SMTP block :3627-3631; `.eml` write :3624; CIDs :3505-3506; DB engine :818-836 + `create_all`/`sys.exit` under `--create-tables`; plan model inline in `main()` from ~:3095; `if __name__=="__main__": main()` already present at :3672-3673 with the problematic module-scope `parse_args()` at :219). Findings below.

---

## 1. Completeness

**Issues:**

- **Syrupy/golden machinery and Hypothesis are designed and added as dependencies, but no §9 smoke test exercises either.** §5.0/§5.9 build an entire golden-normalization design and §12 adds `syrupy` + `hypothesis` to `[test]` deps; §5.3 has a `__snapshots__/` dir; acceptance #9 requires `--update-goldens` to "regenerate snapshots" and re-run green. But the §9 smoke set contains no snapshot/property test — the render smoke uses Playwright element assertions, not syrupy, and the unit smoke is plain `fix_drush_output`/`escape_url` assertions, not Hypothesis. So the golden pipeline that §5.9 spends the most effort on is never proven by the "prove the harness works" deliverable, and acceptance #9 is vacuous (nothing to regenerate). *Fix:* add one golden smoke test (normalized `build/<site>.html` → syrupy) to §9's e2e or render row, and one Hypothesis property smoke for `fix_drush_output`; or drop syrupy/hypothesis from the initial deliverable and defer them to the full suite.

- **Subprocess coverage is unaddressed, which undercuts the coverage story.** §12 treats coverage of the extension-less file as solely a "name it explicitly" config problem, but the larger obstacle is that pytest-cov does not measure code run in the `run_program()` subprocess (e2e/live). The 3,700-line `main()` body is exercised *only* via subprocess, so `--coverage` will report near-zero coverage of it unless `COVERAGE_PROCESS_START` + `coverage.process_startup()` (or `coverage run` wrapping) is wired in. Acceptance #8 ("reports coverage") is technically satisfiable but misleading. *Fix:* either state that `--coverage` covers only in-process tiers (and say so in §5.0/§12), or specify the subprocess-coverage plumbing.

## 2. Consistency

**Issues:**

- **§6 "Nil input" row is factually wrong.** It claims `out=None` → "`json.loads` path raises `JSONDecodeError`, caught at :328." `json.loads(None)` raises `TypeError`, and the `except json.JSONDecodeError` at :328 does **not** catch it — `terminus()` would crash, not fall through to `result=""`. *Fix:* correct the row to say the None-injection surfaces an uncaught `TypeError` (a real gap in the program worth a pinning test), or drop the `None` case and keep only the `""` case (which genuinely hits :328).

- **§5.2 reset list contradicts §3.** §3 says `icon` and the configured `text_maker` "Must be reset between in-process tests," but the §5.2 snapshot/restore list omits both (and `sc.console`). They're effectively immutable so omitting them is arguably fine — but then §3 shouldn't say they "must be reset." *Fix:* reconcile the two lists (either add them to §5.2 or soften §3).

## 3. Clarity

**Issues:**

- **§3 "`build`+`parse_args()` run at module scope (:141-219)" is ambiguous/misleading.** There is no `build` side effect at module scope — the `build/` directory is created inside `main()` (:800). "build" here apparently means "building the arg parser," but a reader will conflate it with the `build/` artifact dir. *Fix:* reword to "the arg-parser construction + `parse_args()` run at module scope (:142-219)."

- **§5.9 "force the `Agg` backend" gives no mechanism.** `matplotlib.pyplot` is imported at the target module's top (:42), so `matplotlib.use("Agg")` after load is too late; the harness must set `MPLBACKEND=Agg` (or `matplotlib.use` before pyplot import) *before* the session-scoped `importlib` load. *Fix:* state that the module-load fixture sets `MPLBACKEND=Agg` in the environment before loading.

- **"One ~15-line refactor" understates the diff.** The seam refactor re-indents ~77 lines of `add_argument` calls (:147-218) into `build_arg_parser()`. It's mechanical and behavior-preserving (and the byte-identity gate covers it), but "15-line" is optimistic. Minor. *Fix:* call it "a single mechanical wrap of the existing arg-parser block."

## 4. Scope

**Mostly PASS** — deliverable stays at harness + one-per-tier, GMail tier is correctly deferred/scaffolded, `recommend_plan` extraction is explicitly optional. Two soft notes:

- **Hypothesis is premature for a smoke deliverable** (ties to Completeness finding above) — a property-testing framework with no shipping property test is YAGNI for this stage.
- **Live-as-default (§5.4) makes routine `./run-tests` non-hermetic.** Bare `./run-tests` needs live Terminus auth + network and can fail on unrelated API drift. This is a defensible, stated tradeoff (catches drift), but consider whether `--fast` should be the default and live opt-in for the inner loop. Judgment call, not a defect.

## 5. Feasibility

Core mechanics are sound: the single subprocess seam (`run_terminus`) makes monkeypatch/shim interception clean; module-level `run_terminus` name lookup means patching `module.run_terminus` correctly intercepts `terminus()/wp()/drush()`; the `__main__` guard already exists so only `parse_args()` needs relocating; session-scoped single load correctly avoids SQLAlchemy re-registration; `matplotlib` is headless-Agg by default. **Issues:**

- **(a/coverage) `[tool.coverage.run] source` pointing "at the extension-less script" is questionable syntax.** `source` expects package names/dirs; a single extension-less file is better handled via an `include`/glob, and modern coverage may still filter non-`.py` morfs in reporting. Combined with the subprocess gap above, the coverage claim is the shakiest concrete plan in the spec. *Fix:* specify `include = ["*/pantheon-sitehealth-emails"]` (or a symlinked `.py` for coverage) and validate it actually reports.

- **(d) The proposed `recommend_plan(traffic, plan_info, current_plan)` signature is materially understated.** The inline model (:3095-3211) also reads `db_session.get(PantheonOverageProtection, …)` per month, `overage_block_size`/`overage_block_cost`, the current-month `estimate`, and `site_plan_start`. A behavior-preserving pure extraction needs all of those as parameters, so it is not the "small" 3-arg function implied and may not "stay small." The spec's fallback (parametrized e2e) is the safer default; *Fix:* correct the signature sketch or lead with the fallback.

- **(c) Golden PNG normalization is workable — with a caveat.** I confirmed the chart/banner/sitelens gauges are attached as MIME parts referenced by `cid:` (no base64 blobs in the HTML), so HTML/txt snapshots are deterministic after a **CID-pattern regex** (not just the two named `make_msgid` sites at :3505-3506 — the sitelens attachment CIDs under `full.toml` are also random). *Fix:* phrase §5.9 as "regex-normalize all `make_msgid` CIDs," not just :3505-3506.

- **(j) Render tier over email HTML is weak.** The committed `build/*.html`/`-inline2.html` reference images via `cid:`, which won't resolve in standalone Chromium; failed image loads don't emit `console.error`, so "zero console errors" may be trivially true or fail on missing resources rather than testing rendering. *Fix:* stub/rewrite `cid:` refs to local files before loading, or assert on DOM structure only and drop the console-error claim for cid'd images.

- **(e) Interlock + live-first is coherent.** `run_program` token-checking `--all/-a/--for-real` and raising `ForbiddenFlagError` is sound; live full-program runs are safe because SMTP send is commented out (even without `--for-real` no mail leaves), so `build/` artifacts are the only effect. No defect.

**Minor:** `fix_drush_output` is listed under "**genuinely pure**" but it calls `sc.debug(...)` → `sc.options.verbose`; with the default `sc.options = {}` this raises `AttributeError`, so it's not pure and requires the sc-reset fixture to have set `sc.options`. Re-label as "directly unit-testable (given sc.options set)."

---

## Overall

**Quality score: 8/10.** A rigorous, honest, and factually accurate spec whose weakest points are a golden/Hypothesis pipeline shipped without any smoke test to prove it (and a correspondingly vacuous acceptance #9), an under-plumbed subprocess-coverage story, and an understated `recommend_plan` extraction — all fixable with small edits, none fatal to the design.
```

### ↳ Tool result

```
All 12 items verified against the actual source. Here is the second-round review.

## Verification of the 12 prior-round fixes

**1. Golden + property smoke tests (acceptance #4/#9 vacuity) — RESOLVED.**
§9 now has a `golden` row (SPEC.md:431) and a `property` row (:432), each explicitly self-justifying ("this is what proves the golden pipeline + acceptance #9"; "proves the Hypothesis wiring"). Acceptance #4 (:506-507) lists `golden` and `property` among required smoke rows; acceptance #9 (:516-517) exercises the golden snapshot regeneration. No longer vacuous.

**2. Subprocess coverage gap — RESOLVED.**
§5.0 (:177-181) states pytest-cov measures in-process (unit/integration) tiers by default and that `main()` run via `run_program()` in a subprocess is invisible unless `COVERAGE_PROCESS_START` + `coverage.process_startup()` is wired. §12 (:494-497) specifies that as optional; acceptance #8 (:513-515) matches. Consistent throughout.

**3. Nil-input row (TypeError vs JSONDecodeError) — RESOLVED.**
§6 (:376) now reads `out=None → json.loads(None)` raises **TypeError**, **not** caught by `except json.JSONDecodeError` at `:328`. Verified against code: line 327 `json.loads(output)`, line 328 `except json.JSONDecodeError` — `json.loads(None)` does raise TypeError. Correct, and it correctly pins current (crashing) behavior rather than "fixing."

**4. §5.2 vs §3 reset-list contradiction — RESOLVED.**
Both lists now match exactly (8 items: options, config, news, hooks, substitutions, plugin, check, plugin_context). §3 (:79-80) and §5.2 (:227-228) both exclude `console`, `icon`, `text_maker` and label them immutable/not-reset. Reconciled.

**5. "build+parse_args() run at module scope" ambiguity — RESOLVED.**
§3 (:69-73) reworded to "The arg-parser construction + `parse_args()` run at module scope (`:142-219`, ending `sc.options = args_parser.parse_args()`)" and explicitly disambiguates the `build/` dir as a separate `main()`-time effect at `:800`. Verified: line 219 is exactly `sc.options = args_parser.parse_args()`; line 800 creates `build/`.

**6. §5.9 Agg-backend mechanism — RESOLVED.**
§5.9 (:336-340) now sets `MPLBACKEND=Agg` in the environment **before** the importlib load, correctly noting `matplotlib.pyplot` is imported at `:42` so a later `matplotlib.use("Agg")` is too late. Verified pyplot import at line 42.

**7. "15-line refactor" understatement — RESOLVED.**
§4 Approach C (:154) now says "~77-line arg-parser block." Verified: 142→219 is 77 lines. No "15-line" string remains anywhere.

**8. coverage `source` on extension-less file — RESOLVED.**
§12 (:492-494) now uses `include = ["*/pantheon-sitehealth-emails"]` and explains why `source` is wrong for a single extension-less file, with a "validate it reports non-zero" hedge.

**9. recommend_plan signature / §5.10 default — RESOLVED.**
§5.10 (:344-356) leads with the parametrized-e2e default ("safer default and needs no refactor") and the extraction caveat now enumerates the real dependencies: `plan_info`, current plan, per-month `PantheonOverageProtection` via `db_session.get`, `overage_block_size`/`overage_block_cost`, `estimate`, `site_plan_start`. Verified against the inline model at :3095-3211 — every listed dependency is genuinely consumed there (db_session.get at :3114, overage_block_* at :3108-3112, estimate at :3106, site_plan_start at :3132). Extraction correctly deferred to the refactor stage.

**10. Golden CID normalization for ALL make_msgid CIDs — RESOLVED.**
§5.9 (:332-335) now normalizes **all** make_msgid CIDs, not just banner/chart at :3505-3506, explicitly calling out the per-attachment SiteLens gauge CIDs under `full.toml`. Verified: `check/umich/sitelens.py:207` creates `image_cid = make_msgid(...)` rendered as `cid:` at :220 — a real third source of random CIDs.

**11. Render tier cid: refs / weak "zero console errors" — RESOLVED.**
§5.3 (:252), §6 (:380), and §9 (:434) all now rewrite `cid:` refs to local PNGs and assert **DOM structure / key selectors** rather than console-error absence. The "zero console errors" phrasing is gone (grep-confirmed); replaced with "renders without load errors," which is now defensible since image refs resolve to local files.

**12. fix_drush_output "genuinely pure" mislabel — RESOLVED.**
§3 (:81-87) now states these helpers are "not literally *pure*" because `fix_drush_output` and the `check_*` helpers call `sc.debug()`/`sc.console.print()`, requiring `sc.options.verbose`. Verified: `fix_drush_output` calls `sc.debug(...)` at :408, and `sc.debug` reads `options.verbose`. The §5.10 and §9 property rows correctly carry the "(with `sc.options` set)" qualifier.

## New issues introduced by the edits

None are blocking; all are minor:

- **N1 (completeness, minor).** The single shipped e2e/golden smoke's **config is unspecified** — minimal.toml vs full.toml. This matters because the SiteLens-gauge CID normalization added in fix #10 is only exercised if the golden smoke runs under `full.toml` (umich enabled). If the smoke uses minimal.toml (all plugins disabled per §5.7), only banner/chart CIDs appear and the newly-broadened "all make_msgid CIDs" rule is never actually tested by anything that ships. Worth pinning which config the golden smoke uses.

- **N2 (feasibility, minor).** §5.2 says the reset fixture "snapshots and restores" `sc.hooks`, `sc.news`, `sc.substitutions` — but `hooks` is a dict-of-lists and `add_hook`/`add_notice`/`add_news_item` mutate those lists **in place** (script_context.py:41, :77, :90-92). A shallow snapshot of the container won't isolate nested mutation; the fixture must deep-copy. The spec doesn't specify copy depth. Easy to get wrong at implementation time.

- **N3 (consistency, cosmetic).** The §5.4 pyramid diagram (:278) still summarizes render as "Playwright over `build/*.html` from disk" without the cid→PNG rewrite that §5.3/§6/§9 now emphasize. Harmless loose summary, but slightly out of step with the reconciled render description.

- **N4 (cosmetic).** Acceptance #4's parenthetical tier list (:506-507) enumerates 7 of the 11 §9 rows; the regression/interlock rows are covered redundantly by #5/#6. Not wrong, just non-exhaustive phrasing.

## Overall assessment

- **Completeness:** high — tiers, fixtures, shims, interlock, deferrals, and acceptance commands all present; only N1's config-selection gap.
- **Consistency:** the four previously-contradictory areas (reset list, coverage claims, CID scope, render assertions) are now aligned across §3/§5/§6/§9/§12/§13.
- **Clarity:** strong; the ambiguity fixes (build vs build/, pure vs impure, 77-line) land cleanly.
- **Scope:** disciplined — harness-only, refactor and recommend_plan extraction explicitly deferred.
- **Feasibility:** sound; every load-bearing factual claim I spot-checked (lines 42, 219, 226/316-337, 328, 391/408, 800, 818-836, 3095-3211, 3505-3506, 3554/3559/3576, 3624-3631, 3672-3673, sitelens.py:207) matches source exactly.

**Quality score: 9/10.**

**Verdict:** All 12 prior-round issues are genuinely and verifiably resolved with no new contradictions; only minor, non-blocking gaps remain (unspecified smoke-test config and reset-fixture copy depth) — ready to implement.
```
