```
1	# SPEC — Test Harness for `pantheon-sitehealth-emails`
2	
3	> **Status:** Design approved 2026-07-04. This document specifies the test *harness* (plus
4	> initial smoke tests). It is a decision record and an implementation brief for a later
5	> session — **not** primary documentation of how the program works.
6	>
7	> **Scope of the implementation this spec authorizes:** build the harness (runner, fixtures,
8	> mocking utilities, shims, marks, the `run-tests` wrapper), apply one minimal
9	> importability refactor, fix the confirmed bugs with regressions, and ship one smoke test
10	> per tier. It does **not** authorize the full test suite (a later stage), re-enabling SMTP,
11	> or implementing SendGrid.
12	
13	---
14	
15	## 1. Purpose
16	
17	The program has **zero tests, zero CI, no test tooling** (confirmed: no `tests/`, no
18	`conftest.py`, no `pytest` dependency, no `.github/`; `README.md`'s top two TODOs are "test
19	harness" and "test suite"). Major changes are queued next — a large modularization of the
20	~3,700-line monolith, moving logic into the plugin/config framework, and re-enabling SMTP +
21	adding SendGrid.
22	
23	The harness is the **safety net built first**, so those changes are made against a suite that
24	proves the code still works as designed. The immediate intent (verbatim from the task): *ensure
25	that all code works as designed and continues to work as designed even in the face of other,
26	major planned future changes and the addition of new features.*
27	
28	---
29	
30	## 2. Hard constraints (govern design and every run, now and forever)
31	
32	| # | Constraint | Enforcement |
33	|---|---|---|
34	| C1 | **NEVER** run the program with `--all` / `-a` (can take ~6 h). | A `run_program()` interlock raises before exec if `--all`/`-a` appears; covered by a test. |
35	| C2 | **NEVER** run the program with `--for-real` (can email real customers). | Same interlock also refuses `--for-real`; covered by a test. |
36	| C3 | Tests target only `its-wws-test1` (WordPress), `its-wws-test2` (Drupal), or a deliberately chosen real site — all **read-only**. | Live-tier fixtures hardcode these site names; no write/deploy Terminus verbs are ever issued. |
37	| C4 | Do **not** re-enable the disabled SMTP send block (lines 3627-3631). | No test un-comments it; the email round-trip tier stays skipped until SMTP/SendGrid lands. |
38	| C5 | Do **not** touch the `fqdns.json` 24-h staleness check. | Only reachable under `--all`, which C1 forbids; irrelevant to tests. |
39	
40	These constraints are accepted to produce coverage gaps (e.g. the `--all` aggregation path and
41	real email delivery are untestable now). The gaps are listed in §13.
42	
43	---
44	
45	## 3. Current state (facts verified against source on 2026-07-04)
46	
47	All line numbers are in the main script `pantheon-sitehealth-emails` (3,673 lines, shebang
48	`#!/usr/bin/env python`, **no `.py` extension**) unless noted.
49	
50	- **One golden subprocess seam.** Every Pantheon/WP/Drush interaction funnels through
51	  `run_terminus(command, input_data=None) -> (str, str, bool)` (`:226`), which uses
52	  `subprocess.Popen` in argument-list form (no `shell=True`), with a 300 s
53	  `communicate(timeout=…)`. Above it: `terminus()` (`:316`), `wp()`/`wp_eval()` (`:342`/`:356`),
54	  `drush()`/`drush_php_script()` (`:413`/`:428`). WP and Drush are dispatched *as* Terminus
55	  subcommands (`terminus wp …`, `terminus drush …`), so a single fake `terminus` covers all three.
56	- **Second, independent subprocess seam.** The CSS inliner
57	  `subprocess.run(["php", "inline-styles.php", <in>, <out>], check=True)` (`:3554`). `php` is
58	  local, deterministic, fast → tests use **real php**, no shim.
59	- **No direct HTTP to Pantheon.** No `requests`/`httpx`/`urllib.request` for Pantheon; auth is
60	  delegated to the Terminus binary. The only auth logic in-script is the (broken) session-expiry
61	  retry in `terminus()`.
62	- **Other genuine network seams** (only when their plugin is enabled in config):
63	  `dns.resolver.resolve` (`:1218`/`:1248`) in the FQDN/Cloudflare check; the Cloudflare SDK
64	  `Cloudflare(...).ips.list()` (`plugin/cloudflare/ips.py`); boto3 Secrets Manager
65	  (`plugin/aws/get_secret.py`). Test configs disable these plugins unless a test targets them.
66	- **Email send is disabled.** Lines 3627-3631 are commented out; the program's only email output
67	  today is `build/<site>.eml` (written unconditionally at `:3624`) plus `build/<site>.{html,txt}`
68	  and the inlined `-inline2.html`. **Tests assert on artifacts, never on SMTP.**
69	- **Import-time side effects.** The arg-parser construction + `parse_args()` run at module scope
70	  (`:142-219`, ending `sc.options = args_parser.parse_args()`); the file has no `.py` extension.
71	  Importing it today parses live `sys.argv`. SQLAlchemy models (`Base`, `PantheonTraffic`,
72	  `PantheonOverageProtection`) are defined at import (`:93-135`). (The `build/` output dir is a
73	  separate thing, created inside `main()` at `:800` — not a module-scope effect.)
74	- **DB is config-injectable.** Engine built at `:818-836` purely from `sc.config["Database"]`
75	  (`sqlite:///{name}` or `mysql+mysqldb://…`). `--create-tables` runs
76	  `Base.metadata.create_all` then `sys.exit`.
77	- **Global mutable state** in `script_context.py` (imported everywhere as `sc`):
78	  `options, config, plugin, check, news, substitutions, hooks, plugin_context` are mutable and
79	  must be reset between in-process tests; `console`, `icon`, and the configured `text_maker`
80	  (html2text) are effectively immutable and are **not** reset (see §5.2).
81	- **Directly unit-testable today (given `sc.options` is set):** `escape_url` (`:222`),
82	  `fix_drush_output` (`:391`), `wp_error` (`:365`), `drush_error` (`:443`),
83	  `check_wordpress_plugin` (`:533`, logic + stdout), `check_drupal_module` (`:601`, logic +
84	  stdout), and `sc.add_notice`/`sc.add_news_item` (`script_context.py:65`/`:80`). Note: these are
85	  not literally *pure* — `fix_drush_output` and the `check_*` helpers call `sc.debug()`/
86	  `sc.console.print()`, so `sc.options` must be populated (with a `verbose` attribute) by the
87	  sc-reset fixture or they raise `AttributeError` on `sc.options.verbose`.
88	- **Tooling on hand:** Python 3.13 via uv (`pyproject.toml requires-python >=3.11`; deps `rich,
89	  SQLAlchemy, matplotlib, Jinja2, dnspython, html2text, semver`; extras `mysql/aws/cloudflare`);
90	  Node 24; PHP + Composer (`pelago/emogrifier ^7.2`); Terminus authenticated; **dev-container
91	  firewall is OFF and will stay off** (network + Pantheon auth always available).
92	
93	### 3.1 Confirmed bugs to fix now (with regressions) — re-verified against source
94	
95	1. **`terminus()` session-expiry retry is doubly broken (`:320-337`).** `*args` is a *tuple*, yet
96	   the retry path does `del args["pshe-no-retry"]` (indexing a tuple with a `str` → `TypeError`)
97	   and `args.push("pshe-no-retry")` (`.push` is not a tuple/list method → `AttributeError`). Any
98	   time Pantheon returns `Invalid or expired session header: X-Pantheon-Session`, this path is
99	   entered and **crashes** instead of retrying.
100	2. **`check/umich/__init__.py:11`** `else` branch calls `sc.console('…')` — `sc.console` is a
101	   rich `Console` instance; the callable form raises `TypeError`. Should be `sc.console.print(…)`.
102	   Reached whenever the `[UMich]` plugin is loaded but not `enabled`.
103	
104	Both are fixed as part of harness implementation, each pinned by a regression test (§9).
105	
106	---
107	
108	## 4. Approaches considered and evaluated
109	
110	Three approaches were weighed. Scores are 0–1 on Correctness, Completeness, Ability-to-implement,
111	Maintainability, Clarity (the task's quality-control axes). "Correctness" here = *does the
112	approach actually catch the regressions we care about*; "Completeness" = *coverage breadth
113	achievable*.
114	
115	### Approach A — Black-box only (zero source changes)
116	Run the script as a subprocess with a fake `terminus` on PATH; assert on `build/` artifacts,
117	exit codes, stdout. No code touched before a suite exists.
118	
119	| Axis | Score | Note |
120	|---|---|---|
121	| Correctness | 0.80 | Catches end-to-end breakage but blind to internal-logic regressions. |
122	| Completeness | 0.55 | Cannot unit-test pure functions, fault-inject `run_terminus`, or exercise the retry/error paths deterministically. |
123	| Ability-to-implement | 0.95 | Simplest; no refactor risk. |
124	| Maintainability | 0.70 | Every test pays subprocess cost; failures are coarse ("artifact differs") and hard to localize. |
125	| Clarity | 0.85 | Simple mental model. |
126	
127	**Rejected:** Completeness 0.55 — the upcoming modularization refactor will move internal logic
128	around, and a black-box-only net can't localize what broke.
129	
130	### Approach B — Full unit-test refactor now
131	Aggressively split the monolith into importable modules, then unit-test broadly.
132	
133	| Axis | Score | Note |
134	|---|---|---|
135	| Correctness | 0.75 | The large diff *before* a safety net risks introducing the very regressions we're trying to prevent. |
136	| Completeness | 0.95 | Highest achievable coverage. |
137	| Ability-to-implement | 0.55 | Large, risky diff; contradicts "don't break things before tests." |
138	| Maintainability | 0.90 | Clean long-term. |
139	| Clarity | 0.80 | Big conceptual change up front. |
140	
141	**Rejected:** Ability-to-implement 0.55 and Correctness 0.75 — it inverts the plan's ordering
142	(net first, refactor second) and front-loads the biggest risk.
143	
144	### Approach C — Hybrid: minimal importability seam + both mock styles ✅ SELECTED
145	One tiny, behavior-preserving change makes the module importable (§5.1). Then: monkeypatch
146	`run_terminus`/`terminus` for fast in-process unit/integration tests, **and** a PATH-shim fake
147	`terminus` for deterministic full-script e2e, **and** live tiers that run real Terminus read-only
148	against the test sites (the default per the live-first decision).
149	
150	| Axis | Score (pre-refine) | Refined | Note |
151	|---|---|---|---|
152	| Correctness | 0.90 | **0.95** | Localizes regressions at unit + integration level; live tier catches real API drift. |
153	| Completeness | 0.88 | **0.92** | Covers pure logic, error/edge injection, full pipeline, rendering, and real integration. Gaps only where C1–C4 forbid. |
154	| Ability-to-implement | 0.90 | **0.93** | A single mechanical wrap of the existing ~77-line arg-parser block is the only source change (behavior-preserving, covered by the byte-identity gate); everything else is additive test code. |
155	| Maintainability | 0.88 | **0.92** | Fast inner loop (monkeypatch) + realistic outer loop (live/shim); golden/fixture refresh scripted. |
156	| Clarity | 0.90 | **0.94** | Explicit tiers and one sanctioned invocation path. |
157	
158	**Refinements applied to reach ≥0.90 on every axis:** (a) added the `run_program()` safety
159	interlock so C1/C2 can never be violated even by a mistaken test; (b) added golden-output
160	normalization rules (§5.9) so rendering snapshots are stable despite volatile CIDs/dates; (c)
161	scoped property testing honestly to pure/extractable functions (§5.10); (d) specified `sc`-state
162	reset (§5.2) so in-process tests don't leak global state; (e) pinned a byte-identity verification
163	gate for the seam refactor (§5.1) so "behavior-preserving" is *proven*, not asserted.
164	
165	**Selected: Approach C (Hybrid).**
166	
167	---
168	
169	## 5. Architecture
170	
171	### 5.0 Framework choices (and why, over alternatives)
172	- **pytest** — the spine. Fixtures, marks, `parametrize`, and the richest plugin ecosystem.
173	  *Rejected:* `unittest` (verbose, weak fixtures/parametrization), `nose2` (unmaintained).
174	- **syrupy** — golden/snapshot assertions for rendered reports, with `--snapshot-update`.
175	- **Hypothesis** — property-based tests for pure math.
176	- **pytest-cov** — coverage measurement (reported, **no gate**). It measures the **in-process**
177	  tiers (unit/integration) by default. The e2e/live tiers run `main()` in a *subprocess* via
178	  `run_program()`, which pytest-cov does **not** see unless `COVERAGE_PROCESS_START` +
179	  `coverage.process_startup()` plumbing is wired in (specified optional in §12). So the reported
180	  number reflects in-process code unless that plumbing is enabled — the docs state this so the
181	  figure is never read as whole-program coverage.
182	- **pytest-playwright** (Python Playwright) — the browser render tier. One language, one runner;
183	  it manages its own Chromium (`playwright install chromium`); firewall is off so the download
184	  works. *Rejected:* a separate Node/Puppeteer toolchain (second language + second runner for
185	  no gain).
186	- **PHP:** no PHP test framework. `inline-styles.php` is a pure file-in/file-out transform,
187	  exercised via subprocess with sample HTML and a golden output.
188	
189	### 5.1 The minimal seam refactor (the only source change, behavior-preserving)
190	Make the module importable without executing argparse at import:
191	
192	```python
193	def build_arg_parser() -> argparse.ArgumentParser:
194	    p = argparse.ArgumentParser(...)
195	    ...   # every existing add_argument call, unchanged
196	    return p
197	
198	def parse_args(argv=None):
199	    return build_arg_parser().parse_args(argv)
200	
201	# bottom of file:
202	if __name__ == "__main__":
203	    sc.options = parse_args()
204	    main()
205	```
206	
207	- Functions read `sc.options` at *call* time, so relocating the `parse_args()` call into the
208	  `__main__` guard is safe: a test imports the module (no argv parsing), sets `sc.options` to a
209	  parsed namespace or a fake, then calls functions or `main()`.
210	- **No rename.** `./pantheon-sitehealth-emails` still runs exactly as documented. The
211	  extension-less file is loaded in tests via `importlib.util.spec_from_file_location` +
212	  `SourceFileLoader`, once, cached by a session-scoped fixture (§5.2) to avoid re-registering the
213	  SQLAlchemy models.
214	- **Verification gate (proves "behavior-preserving"):** for `its-wws-test1` at a fixed `--date`,
215	  the pre-refactor and post-refactor `build/` artifacts must be identical after normalizing the
216	  known-volatile bits (§5.9). This diff is run once during implementation and recorded in the
217	  handoff notes; it is not a standing test (it needs a live run).
218	
219	```
220	   argv ──► build_arg_parser() ──► parse_args(argv) ──► sc.options
221	                                          ▲                  │
222	   test: import module (no parse) ────────┘                  ▼
223	   test: sc.options = fake/parsed ───────────────────► call any function / main()
224	```
225	
226	### 5.2 Global-state isolation
227	`script_context.py` holds process-global mutable state. A `conftest.py` autouse fixture
228	snapshots and restores, per test: `sc.options, sc.config, sc.news, sc.hooks, sc.substitutions,
229	sc.plugin, sc.check, sc.plugin_context`. The snapshot must **deep-copy** (`copy.deepcopy`) the
230	mutable containers — `sc.hooks` is a dict-of-lists and `add_hook`/`add_notice`/`add_news_item`
231	mutate `sc.hooks`/`sc.news`/`sc.substitutions` **in place** (`script_context.py:41`/`:77`/
232	`:90-92`), so a shallow snapshot would not isolate nested mutation between tests. The module-load
233	fixture is **session-scoped** (import
234	once); the state-reset fixture is **function-scoped** (fresh state each test). Plugin/check
235	self-registration is an import side effect gated by config flags — tests that need a plugin
236	registered import the relevant package *after* setting a config that enables it, inside an
237	isolated `sc` state.
238	
239	### 5.3 Directory layout
240	```
241	tests/
242	  conftest.py          # module-load fixture, sc-reset, temp cwd+build, temp sqlite,
243	                       #   config-fixture loader, run_program() interlock, --llm reporter hook
244	  README.md            # dev-facing testing docs (NOT docs/, which is end-user only)
245	  fixtures/
246	    config/            # minimal.toml, full.toml — self-contained; NEVER depend on the private config symlink
247	    terminus/          # recorded JSON keyed by argv: org:site:list, env:info, env:metrics, wp plugin list, drush pm:list …
248	    db/                # seed PantheonTraffic / PantheonOverageProtection rows
249	    html/              # committed sample build/*.html for the render tier (no live run needed)
250	  shims/
251	    terminus           # fake executable: maps argv → fixtures/terminus/<key>.json, prints it
252	  __snapshots__/       # syrupy golden baselines (rendered reports, normalized)
253	  unit/                # pure funcs: fix_drush_output, escape_url, notices, config_substitution, plan-rec math
254	  integration/         # in-process; run_terminus monkeypatched (or live); temp DB; check hooks; the 2 bug regressions
255	  e2e/                 # full-script subprocess runs: shim-backed (deterministic) + live (default)
256	  render/              # pytest-playwright: load a report HTML with cid: image refs rewritten to local PNGs; assert DOM structure
257	  email/               # GMail round-trip — scaffolded, @pytest.mark.skip(reason=…), see §11
258	run-tests              # thin wrapper over pytest (executable)
259	```
260	
261	### 5.4 Test tiers & marks
262	Registered marks: `unit`, `integration`, `e2e`, `live`, `render`, `email`, `slow`.
263	
264	- **Default `./run-tests` includes live tiers** (live-first decision: real Terminus read-only
265	  against the test sites is the primary confidence signal).
266	- **`./run-tests --fast`** selects the offline subset `-m "not live and not slow"` for the inner
267	  loop (unit + shim-backed integration/e2e + render on committed HTML) — fully offline,
268	  deterministic.
269	- Claude Code selects the relevant subset per change (e.g. a Drupal-check edit → `unit` +
270	  `integration` + the Drupal `e2e`/`live` cases via `-k drupal`).
271	- **Hermeticity tradeoff (accepted):** because live is the default, a bare `./run-tests` requires
272	  live Terminus auth + network and can fail on unrelated Pantheon API drift or a test-site
273	  outage. That is the point of the live tier (it catches real drift), but the **hermetic,
274	  offline inner loop is `./run-tests --fast`** — that is what Claude Code and pre-commit checks
275	  run for fast, deterministic feedback; the full `./run-tests` is the higher-confidence pass.
276	
277	```
278	                 ▲ realism / cost
279	      live       │  real terminus, read-only, its-wws-test1/2   (default; slow; catches API drift)
280	      e2e        │  full subprocess run, shim terminus + real php (deterministic pipeline)
281	      integration│  in-process, run_terminus monkeypatched, temp DB, check hooks (fault injection)
282	      render     │  Playwright over report HTML (cid: refs → local PNGs)  (rendering correctness)
283	      unit       │  pure functions, no I/O                        (fast; many; localizes bugs)
284	                 ▼ speed / count
285	```
286	
287	### 5.5 External-tool interception (both styles)
288	- **Monkeypatch (unit/integration):** patch `run_terminus` (and/or `terminus`) on the loaded
289	  module to return canned `(stdout, stderr, fatal)` or raise/inject faults — the deterministic
290	  way to exercise error paths: `fatal=True` timeouts, malformed JSON (`json.JSONDecodeError`),
291	  and the expired-session retry. This is the primary seam because all Pantheon I/O funnels
292	  through it.
293	- **PATH-shim fake `terminus` (e2e):** `tests/shims/terminus` is prepended to `PATH`; it reads a
294	  manifest mapping the invoked argv to a `fixtures/terminus/*.json` file and prints it. Real
295	  `php` is used (local, fast). This exercises the *real* subprocess/argument-building path and
296	  the full render→MIME→`.eml` pipeline without network.
297	- **Live (default):** no interception — real `terminus` runs read-only against `its-wws-test1/2`.
298	
299	### 5.6 DB fixtures
300	A `temp_db` fixture points `sc.config["Database"]` at `type="sqlite", name=<tmp file>`, runs
301	`Base.metadata.create_all`, and seeds rows from `fixtures/db/`. In-process tests of DB-touching
302	helpers get a live SQLAlchemy session bound to that temp engine. No test touches the repo's real
303	`database.db`.
304	
305	### 5.7 Config fixtures
306	`fixtures/config/minimal.toml` (plan_info, plan_sku_to_name, `[Database]` sqlite, `[News]` →
307	temp folder, **all plugins disabled**) and `full.toml` (umich/cloudflare/aws enabled, with those
308	external calls mocked) let tests run without the private, symlinked production config. **No test
309	depends on the symlinked `pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml`.**
310	
311	### 5.8 The `run-tests` wrapper (thin)
312	Executable wrapping pytest. Flags:
313	
314	| Flag | Effect |
315	|---|---|
316	| (none) | `--human`: default rich pytest output, all tiers incl. live. |
317	| `--llm` | terse, `-q`, `--tb=short`, no color, failures-first, plus a machine-parseable summary line emitted by a conftest `pytest_terminal_summary` hook (counts + `FAILED <nodeid>` list, no fluff). |
318	| `--fast` | offline subset (`-m "not live and not slow"`). |
319	| `--record` | refresh `fixtures/terminus/` from the live test sites (read-only). |
320	| `--update-goldens` | pass `--snapshot-update` to syrupy. |
321	| `--coverage` | enable pytest-cov (reported, no gate). |
322	| passthrough | `-m`, `-k`, and paths forwarded to pytest. |
323	
324	```
325	        ./run-tests
326	             │
327	   ┌─────────┼───────────┬───────────┬──────────────┬───────────┐
328	 default   --llm       --fast     --record      --update-       --coverage
329	 (human)  (terse,    (offline   (real         goldens          (pytest-cov,
330	  all      machine    subset)   terminus,     (syrupy           no gate)
331	 tiers)    summary)             read-only)     update)
332	```
333	
334	### 5.9 Determinism / golden normalization
335	Before snapshotting `build/<site>.{html,txt}` and `-inline2.html`, normalize volatile content:
336	- **`make_msgid` CIDs** → regex-normalize **all** `make_msgid`-generated CIDs to a stable
337	  placeholder, not just the banner/chart CIDs at `:3505-3506` — the per-attachment SiteLens
338	  gauge CIDs created under `full.toml` are also random and appear in the HTML as `cid:` refs.
339	- **`Date:` header** in the `.eml` → strip/normalize.
340	- **matplotlib PNG bytes** (chart, SiteLens gauges) → do **not** byte-compare; assert the inline
341	  image parts *exist* with the expected CIDs/content-types. Matplotlib output is not byte-stable
342	  across versions/backends, so the module-load fixture sets `MPLBACKEND=Agg` in the environment
343	  **before** the `importlib` load — `matplotlib.pyplot` is imported at the target's top (`:42`),
344	  so a later `matplotlib.use("Agg")` would be too late.
345	- Fix `--date` and seed the DB so all traffic-derived text is stable.
346	
347	### 5.10 Property-based testing (honest scope)
348	Hypothesis targets deterministic functions with `sc.options` set: `fix_drush_output`
349	(string→(str,str)), `escape_url`, and the day/month **traffic aggregation** helper. The
350	**plan-recommendation cost model is currently inline in `main()` (`:3095-3211`)** and is not
351	directly callable. SPEC records two options, chosen at implementation time:
352	- **(default) pin the math via `parametrize`d e2e cases** with fixed traffic fixtures, no source
353	  change. This is the safer default and needs no refactor.
354	- (optional) a pure extraction `recommend_plan(...)` that `main()` then calls, enabling direct
355	  property tests. **Caveat:** a behavior-preserving extraction is *not* the "small" 3-arg
356	  function it might seem — the inline model also consumes `plan_info`, the current plan, per-month
357	  `PantheonOverageProtection` lookups (`db_session.get`), `overage_block_size`/`overage_block_cost`,
358	  the current-month `estimate`, and `site_plan_start`. Because that pulls real refactor surface
359	  forward, it is **deferred to the refactor stage** unless it proves genuinely small; the
360	  parametrized-e2e default covers this math in the meantime.
361	
362	### 5.11 Safety interlock (Prime Directive #1: zero silent failures)
363	`run_program(args: list[str], **kw)` in `conftest.py` is the **only** sanctioned way tests invoke
364	the program. Before exec it asserts none of `--all`, `-a`, `--for-real` is present and **raises
365	`ForbiddenFlagError`** (a named exception, not a bare assert, not a silent skip) otherwise. It is
366	itself covered by a test that feeds it each forbidden flag and asserts the raise. When the email
367	tier activates, an analogous guard asserts the recipient is the GMail test identity, never a
368	customer address.
369	
370	---
371	
372	## 6. Shadow-path & edge-case analysis (Prime Directives #2–#4)
373	
374	For each **new** data flow the harness introduces, the happy path plus three shadow paths
375	(nil / empty / upstream-error) are traced; named exceptions are specified.
376	
377	| New flow | Happy | Nil input | Empty input | Upstream error |
378	|---|---|---|---|---|
379	| Fake `terminus` shim reads manifest | argv → fixture JSON printed | argv not in manifest → exit non-zero + stderr `no fixture for: <argv>` (never silent empty) | empty fixture file → shim prints `{}`; test asserts caller handles empty JSON | corrupt fixture → shim exits 1; e2e test sees non-zero exit and fails loudly |
380	| Monkeypatched `run_terminus` | returns seeded `(out,"",False)` | `out=None` → `json.loads(None)` raises **`TypeError`**, which is **not** caught by `except json.JSONDecodeError` at `:328` → `terminus()` crashes. A real latent gap; a test **pins current behavior** (documented, not fixed here — behavior changes belong to the refactor). | `out=""` → `json.loads("")` raises `JSONDecodeError`, caught at `:328`, `result=""` (current behavior) — pinned by test | inject `fatal=True` → assert caller treats as fatal |
381	| `terminus()` retry (post-fix) | expired-session once → retry → success | — | — | expired-session twice → no infinite loop (sentinel honored); asserted |
382	| `temp_db` seed | rows inserted, queried | no rows → report path with zero traffic renders without crash (asserts empty-traffic handling) | empty seed file → create_all only, no rows | bad DSN → `create_engine` raises; test asserts named failure |
383	| Golden snapshot | normalized HTML matches baseline | missing baseline → syrupy reports "snapshot not found" (run `--update-goldens`) | empty render → test fails (report must have content) | template error → Jinja2 raises; test asserts render fails loudly |
384	| Render tier (Playwright) | HTML (cid: refs rewritten to local PNGs) loads, key DOM selectors present | missing HTML file → test fails with path | empty HTML → assertion on required elements fails | browser launch failure → pytest-playwright errors (not skipped silently) |
385	
386	**Interaction edge cases (Prime Directive #4):** user interrupts a live run (Ctrl-C) → pytest
387	reports KeyboardInterrupt, no partial artifact is asserted as success; slow Pantheon → live tests
388	inherit the program's 300 s Terminus timeout and are marked `slow`; stale fixture → `--record`
389	refreshes, and a fixture's provenance/date is recorded in a header comment so staleness is visible.
390	
391	**Catch-all smell (Prime Directive #2):** the harness itself uses **named** exceptions
392	(`ForbiddenFlagError`, `FixtureNotFoundError`); it must not wrap test bodies in bare
393	`except Exception`. The program's own broad handling (e.g. `terminus()` swallowing
394	`JSONDecodeError` into `result=""`) is *documented and pinned* by tests, not "fixed" here beyond
395	the two confirmed bugs — behavior changes belong to the later refactor.
396	
397	---
398	
399	## 7. Best practices baked in
400	- **Test pyramid** (many fast unit, fewer integration, fewest e2e/live) — §5.4.
401	- **One sanctioned invocation path** with a fail-closed safety interlock — §5.11.
402	- **Golden/snapshot testing** with explicit volatile-field normalization — §5.9.
403	- **Fixtures recorded from reality, refreshable by one command** (`--record`), with provenance
404	  headers so they don't rot silently — §5.8, §6.
405	- **Dual-audience output** (human default, `--llm` terse/parseable) — §5.5/§5.8; both are
406	  LLM-friendly (a human pasting a failure into Claude Code gets clean, localizable output).
407	- **CI-portable by construction:** everything is pytest + marks; adding GitHub Actions later is a
408	  workflow file that runs `run-tests --fast` (offline) plus, optionally, a credentialed live job.
409	  (CI itself is out of scope — §13.)
410	- **Coverage measured, never chased** (no gate) — §5.0.
411	
412	---
413	
414	## 8. Maintenance strategy (keep tests relevant as the program changes)
415	- **Standing policy** (added to CLAUDE.md): every change designs + implements appropriate tests
416	  at the time the change is made (the program is not adopting TDD; tests follow the change).
417	- **Fixture provenance + refresh:** each recorded fixture carries a `// recorded <date> from
418	  <site> via <terminus argv>` header; `run-tests --record` regenerates the set; a fixture older
419	  than a chosen horizon prints a notice when used in a live-diff check.
420	- **Goldens updated deliberately:** rendering changes require `--update-goldens` and show up as a
421	  reviewable snapshot diff — unintended rendering drift fails loudly.
422	- **Reusable prompt templates** (stored in this feature folder for later stages, not executed
423	  now): `add-tests-for-change.prompt.md` (design+add tests for a diff) and
424	  `refresh-fixtures.prompt.md` (re-record + update goldens, review the diff). These make routine
425	  test maintenance a repeatable Claude Code task.
426	
427	---
428	
429	## 9. Smoke tests the harness ships with (prove the harness works — NOT the suite)
430	| Tier | Smoke test | Asserts |
431	|---|---|---|
432	| unit | `fix_drush_output` / `escape_url` | pure input→output; no I/O. |
433	| integration | monkeypatched `run_terminus` + `temp_db` + a `check` hook | in-process pipeline step works; state isolated. |
434	| e2e | shim `terminus`, full subprocess run for one site + fixed `--date` | `build/<site>.eml`, `.html`, `.txt` produced; exit 0. |
435	| golden | normalized `build/<site>.html` from the shim e2e (under **minimal.toml**) → syrupy snapshot | rendering pinned; `--update-goldens` regenerates and an immediate re-run is green (proves the golden pipeline + acceptance #9). This exercises the banner/chart CID normalization; the SiteLens-gauge CID path (needs `full.toml` + mocked umich data) is deferred to the suite stage — the normalization regex is written generally so it already covers those CIDs. |
436	| property | Hypothesis over `fix_drush_output` (with `sc.options` set) | the `(str, str)` invariants hold across generated inputs (this is what proves the Hypothesis wiring). |
437	| live | real `terminus self:info` (or read-only `env:info` on `its-wws-test1`) | Terminus auth + JSON parse work end-to-end. |
438	| render | Playwright loads a committed report HTML (cid: refs rewritten to local PNGs) | key DOM elements present; page renders without load errors. |
439	| email | scaffolded round-trip | `@pytest.mark.skip("email send disabled until SMTP/SendGrid")` — imports/collects cleanly. |
440	| regression | `terminus()` expired-session retry | with the fix, one retry then success; no crash, no infinite loop. |
441	| regression | `check/umich` `else` branch | with the fix, prints via `sc.console.print`, no `TypeError`. |
442	| interlock | `run_program(["--all"])`, `["-a"]`, `["--for-real"]` | each raises `ForbiddenFlagError`. |
443	
444	The two bug **fixes** land with their regressions (the tests would fail on today's code and pass
445	after the fix).
446	
447	---
448	
449	## 10. (reserved)
450	
451	---
452	
453	## 11. GMail email round-trip tier — design (deferred, scaffolded, skipped)
454	Cannot run today (C4: send is disabled; SendGrid unimplemented). Scaffolded now so it activates
455	the moment email sending lands.
456	
457	- **Auth:** Gmail API + an OAuth refresh token (or a service account with domain-wide delegation)
458	  stored as a secret (env var / AWS Secrets Manager, matching the program's own secret story).
459	  No account password in the harness. Scopes: read + search (to detect bounce/rejection/
460	  undeliverable notices) — send happens via the program under test, not the harness.
461	- **Identity:** sender and recipient are the **same** GMail test account, so delivery *and* error
462	  notices land in one inbox. A guard asserts the recipient is that test identity (never a
463	  customer), mirroring §5.11.
464	- **Flow (when active):** program sends → poll the inbox by a unique per-run subject/token for a
465	  few minutes → assert receipt → scan for error notices (unknown sender / undeliverable /
466	  rejected / spam) → optionally load the received HTML in Playwright to check GMail rendering
467	  (GMail strips a subset of HTML/CSS/JS and may gate remote content / truncate long messages —
468	  handle those states before asserting content).
469	- **State today:** the test file exists and imports cleanly but is `@pytest.mark.skip`ped with a
470	  reason pointing at the SMTP/SendGrid milestone.
471	
472	```
473	 [program under test] --send--> (GMail test acct) <--search-- [harness, Gmail API]
474	                                       │                          │
475	                                 error notices ──────────────► assert receipt + no errors
476	                                       │
477	                                 received HTML ─► Playwright ─► GMail-render assertions
478	```
479	
480	---
481	
482	## 12. Documentation updates (performed during implementation)
483	- **README.md:** add a **Testing** section — install (`uv pip install .[test]` +
484	  `playwright install chromium`), `run-tests` modes/tiers, live vs `--fast`, `--record`,
485	  `--update-goldens`, `--coverage`; **retire the two TODO bullets** ("test harness", "test
486	  suite") or mark the harness done.
487	- **CLAUDE.md:** add testing conventions that aren't obvious from the code — the importability
488	  seam (module loads via `importlib`, `sc.options` set by caller), the two mock seams
489	  (`run_terminus`, the `php` inliner), the `--all`/`--for-real` `run_program` interlock, the
490	  fixture/golden refresh commands, and the standing "tests accompany every change" policy.
491	- **tests/README.md** (new, dev-facing): layout, marks, how to write a new test in each tier,
492	  how to record fixtures, determinism/normalization rules.
493	- **docs/:** **no** testing docs added — `docs/` is end-user-only per the repo convention.
494	- **pyproject.toml:** add `[project.optional-dependencies] test = ["pytest", "syrupy",
495	  "hypothesis", "pytest-cov", "pytest-playwright"]`; `[tool.pytest.ini_options]` (markers,
496	  `testpaths = ["tests"]`); `[tool.coverage.run]` using `include = ["*/pantheon-sitehealth-emails"]`
497	  (an `include` glob, **not** `source` — the target is a single extension-less file, and `source`
498	  expects package names/dirs). Validate it actually reports non-zero for the in-process tiers.
499	  Optionally wire `COVERAGE_PROCESS_START` + `coverage.process_startup()` so the e2e/live
500	  subprocess runs also contribute; otherwise `--coverage` reflects in-process tiers only, which
501	  README/tests-README must state.
502	
503	---
504	
505	## 13. Acceptance criteria (the "done" bar — exact commands + observable outcomes)
506	1. `uv pip install .[test] && playwright install chromium` → exits 0.
507	2. `./run-tests --fast` → green, **no network** (unit + shim e2e + render on committed HTML).
508	3. `./run-tests` → green, including live read-only smoke against `its-wws-test1/2`; a grep of the
509	   run + the interlock test **prove** `--all`/`--for-real` were never used.
510	4. One passing smoke test per row of the §9 table exists (unit, integration, e2e, **golden**,
511	   **property**, live, render); `email` collects but is skipped.
512	5. The two bug fixes are in place; both regressions pass (and fail on the pre-fix code).
513	6. The interlock test passes: `run_program` raises `ForbiddenFlagError` for `--all`, `-a`,
514	   `--for-real`.
515	7. `./run-tests --llm` emits terse, machine-parseable output (summary counts + `FAILED` nodeids,
516	   no boilerplate).
517	8. `./run-tests --coverage` reports coverage with **no threshold gate** (in-process tiers by
518	   default; subprocess e2e/live coverage only if the optional `COVERAGE_PROCESS_START` plumbing
519	   is enabled — §5.0/§12).
520	9. `./run-tests --update-goldens` regenerates the §9 golden smoke snapshot; an immediate re-run
521	   is green.
522	10. Seam-refactor byte-identity check passed for `its-wws-test1` at a fixed `--date` (volatile
523	    bits normalized) and is recorded in the handoff notes.
524	11. README/CLAUDE.md/tests-README/pyproject updates present (§12).
525	
526	---
527	
528	## 14. Deferred / explicitly NOT in scope (Prime Directive #7: written down)
529	- The **full test suite** (only smoke-per-tier ships now).
530	- **Re-enabling SMTP; implementing SendGrid; activating the GMail email tier** (C4).
531	- The **large modularization refactor** and plugin/config migration (later stages). Only the
532	  §5.1 importability seam — and, if kept tiny, the §5.10 `recommend_plan` extraction — may be
533	  pulled forward, and only as necessary for testing.
534	- **CI/CD** — next year; the design keeps everything CI-portable so it's a workflow file later.
535	- **`fqdns.json` regeneration / 24-h staleness** (C5).
536	- **Performance / parallel-check testing.**
537	- **Coverage gaps accepted by C1–C4:** the `--all` aggregation + CSV/results-JSON path, real
538	  SMTP delivery, and any customer-facing send path are untested by design.
539	
540	---
541

544	convergence stop. Empty means the spec passed clean.)_

### ⚙ Tool call: `Agent`

```json
{
  "description": "Map external calls for single-site run",
  "prompt": "I'm building a test harness for the Python program `/workspace/pantheon-sitehealth-emails` (~3,700-line file, no .py extension). I need to run ONE site (e.g. `its-wws-test1`, a WordPress site) through the full report pipeline as a SUBPROCESS, faking `terminus` via a PATH shim while using a config that DISABLES all plugins (Cloudflare/AWS/UMich). I need to know EXACTLY which external calls happen so I can make the run deterministic/offline. A subprocess e2e cannot monkeypatch Python calls, so any non-terminus network call (DNS especially) is a problem I must design around.\n\nRead the code and answer precisely (with line numbers and quoted conditionals):\n\n1. **Config-key requirements for plugin loading.** `find_modules(\"plugin\")` imports every `plugin/*/__init__.py`. Quote the enclosing `if`/`for` conditions and their line numbers. If Cloudflare is disabled in config, is DNS resolution skipped entirely? Also: does the FQDN check read `fqdns.json`, and is that read gated the same way? (I need to know if a minimal-config single-site run touches DNS or fqdns.json at all.)\n\n3. **Full list of terminus/wp/drush calls for one WordPress site.** Trace `main()` from the site loop start (~919) through rendering (~3576) for a WordPress site (framework startswith \"wordpress\"). Include the setup-phase calls before the loop (e.g. `terminus(\"self:info\")` at ~797, `terminus(\"org:site:list\", org_id)` at ~904). I need the argv→response mapping surface. Note which calls' RESULTS drive control flow (e.g. plan name, framework detection, live-env check) so I know which fixture values matter.\n\n4. **Other external effects in a single WordPress-site run under minimal config:** any other network (requests/urllib/boto/Cloudflare SDK), file reads/writes beyond build/*, the `php inline-styles.php` subprocess, the DB queries (which tables/rows the render path needs — will an EMPTY PantheonTraffic table render without crashing, or does the render/plan-recommendation path require traffic rows?). Point me at the minimum DB seeding needed for the render to complete.\n\n5. **Early-exit branches.** List the `continue`/early-skip branches in the per-site loop (plan == Sandbox/Elite/frozen/unknown, no live env, --update, --import-older-metrics, --only-warn) with line numbers and the condition that triggers each — so I understand which fixture values would cause the pipeline to short-circuit BEFORE rendering (I want to AVOID those for the golden/e2e, since I need a fully rendered report).\n\nReport conc--isely with line numbers and quoted conditions. Do NOT dump huge code blocks — I need the operational map: config keys, DNS gating, the ordered terminus-call surface, DB seeding needs, and early-exit conditions.",

### ↳ Tool result

```
I have the complete operational map. Here are the precise findings.

## 1. Config-key requirements for plugin loading

`find_modules("plugin")` runs at module top-level (line 780: `for plugin_name in find_modules("plugin")`), `find_modules("check")` at line 789. All four init files guard identically and are **KeyError-safe when the section is absent**:

- `plugin/cloudflare/__init__.py:7` — `if 'Cloudflare' in sc.config and 'enabled' in sc.config['Cloudflare'] and sc.config['Cloudflare']['enabled']:` — short-circuits on absent `[Cloudflare]`. Only reads `member_email`/`member_api_key` (and env vars) *inside* the enabled branch.
- `plugin/aws/__init__.py:7` — `if 'AWS' in sc.config and 'enabled' in sc.config['AWS'] and sc.config['AWS']['enabled']:` — same pattern; `profile`/`default_region` read only when enabled.
- `plugin/umich/__init__.py:5` — `if 'UMich' in sc.config and 'enabled' in sc.config['UMich'] and sc.config['UMich']['enabled']:` — same.
- `check/umich/__init__.py:5` — same `UMich`/`enabled` guard, with an `else:` at line 10 that just prints "Skipping check.umich.sitelens…". Safe.

**Conclusion:** a `minimal.toml` need not contain `[Cloudflare]`, `[AWS]`, or `[UMich]` at all. Including them with `enabled = false` is equally safe. No plugin import touches DNS/network at import time when disabled.

**But the MAIN program's own top-level/`main()` reads are the real minimal-config constraint** (these are unguarded and WILL KeyError if missing):
- `[Pantheon].overage_block_size`, `.overage_block_cost` (822–823)
- `[Pantheon].org_id` (915), `[Pantheon].plan_info` (881, 890 — must be a non-empty table; `plan_names` derives from its keys at 893, and the site's `plan_name` must be one of them or the run `sys.exit`s at ~1031), `[Pantheon].plan_sku_to_name` (976, Elite-only)
- `[Database].type` + `.name` (829–830; `type="sqlite"` path)
- `[News].folder` (868) — **unguarded**: `glob.glob(f"{sc.config['News']['folder']}/*.toml")` runs even though the `if "News" in sc.config` at 860 only wraps the inline-news loop. So `[News].folder` (e.g. `"./news"`) is REQUIRED.

## 2. DNS resolution gating — NOT gated by Cloudflare

The DNS block is **reached for every site that passes the early-exits**, independent of `[Cloudflare].enabled`. `cloudflare_enabled` (line 922, `"plugin.cloudflare" in sc.plugin`) only gates *notice-generation* later (1566, 1895), NOT the resolver calls.

- `fqdns.json` read is **unconditional** per site: lines 1184–1196 (`proxied_fqdns_file = "fqdns.json"` … `os.path.getmtime` staleness check at 1187 → **`sys.exit` at 1192 if the file is >86400s old AND `--all` is set** … `json.load` at 1196). So a minimal single-site run **does read fqdns.json**. Keep it fresh (touch it) or avoid `--all`.
- `domains = terminus("domain:list", live_site)` at 1203 — unconditional.
- The DNS resolver calls at 1229 (`dns.resolver.resolve(hostname, "A")`) and 1259 (`"AAAA"`) live inside `if isinstance(domains, dict):` (1213) → `for d in domains.keys():` (1214), with `if domain["type"] == "platform": continue` (1216–1217) and an FQDN-regex skip (1219–1223).

**Design lever:** DNS is only hit for **non-platform custom domains with valid FQDNs**. If your fake `terminus domain:list` returns only `type=="platform"` entries (or an empty `{}`), the loop `continue`s/does nothing and **no real DNS resolution occurs**. That is how you make the subprocess e2e offline without monkeypatching `dns.resolver`.

## 3. Ordered terminus/wp surface for one WordPress site

Invocation formats the shim must emulate (from `run_terminus`, 234–242): every call is prefixed `terminus --no-ansi --no-interaction …`. `terminus(*args)` appends `--format=json` (335). `wp(env,*a)` → `wp <env> -- <a> --format=json` (357). `wp_eval(env,code)` → `wp <env> -- eval <code>` (**no** `--format=json`, raw stdout, 371). `drush`/`composer` similar (428/443).

Setup phase (once):
- `terminus("self:info")` — 808, **only if `--verbose`**.
- `terminus("org:site:list", org_id)` — 915. **Drives everything**: returns `{site_id: {name, plan_name, frozen, framework, id, …}}`.

Per-site (order as executed for a `wordpress*` site, UMich disabled):
- `terminus("plan:info", site["name"])` — 969, **only if `plan_name == "Elite"`**; result must have `sku` present in `plan_sku_to_name`.
- `terminus("env:list", site["id"], "--fields=id,created,domain,connection_mode,locked,initialized,php_version,php_runtime_generation")` — 1038. **Drives control flow**: `"live"` key + `["live"]["initialized"]` required or `sys.exit` (1043–1048); `initialized is False` adds a notice but continues (1049); `["live"]["php_version"]` used at 2497.
- `terminus("env:metrics", live_site, "--period=day")` — 1078. Needs `["timeseries"]` (dict). Feeds the DB traffic upsert.
- `terminus("domain:list", live_site)` — 1203. Feeds DNS/FQDN loop (see §2).
- WordPress branch (`site["framework"].startswith("wordpress")`, 1505):
  - `wp_eval(live_site, "echo network_home_url();")` — 1398, **only if framework == "wordpress_network"**.
  - `wp_eval(live_site, 'require ABSPATH…echo $wp_version;')` — 1509 (WP version; stored in `site_results`).
  - `wp(live_site, "plugin", "list", "--fields=name,status,update,version,update_version,title")` — 1533 (expects a JSON list).
  - `wp_eval(live_site, 'echo (defined("WP_REDIS_CONFIG")…')` — 1682, **only if an `object-cache-pro` plugin is active** in the plugin list.
  - `wp(live_site, "theme", "list", "--fields=…")` — 1757 (JSON list).
  - `wp_eval(live_site, 'echo is_file("favicon.ico")…')` — 1787.
- `terminus("upstream:updates:list", live_site)` — 2161. Runs for **every** framework (it's after the `if wordpress / elif drupal / else` chain, indent 8). Expects a JSON list (empty `[]` is fine).
- `terminus("site:team:list", site_id)` — 3392, **only when UMich is disabled** (the `else` of 3379). **Drives `recipients`** via `site_team[m]["email"]`.

**Not called for WordPress:** `drush(...)` (1820/1842/1930) and `terminus("composer"…)`/`run_terminus(["composer"…])` (1970/2015) are all inside the `elif site["framework"].startswith("drupal")` block (1816–2150), so a WordPress site never invokes them. `get_old_metrics`→`terminus("env:metrics",…,--period=week/month)` (484) only under `--import-older-metrics`.

## 4. Other external effects (single WP site, minimal config)

- **No other network.** `import requests`/`boto`/`cloudflare` SDK are not used on this path; the only `dns.resolver` calls are the gated ones in §2. SMTP send is **commented out** (3639–3640: `smtp_connection.send_message` disabled); `smtp_login()`/`SMTP_SSL` (766–769) is never called on the report path. The `.eml` is only *written to disk* (3635).
- **`php inline-styles.php` subprocess** — 3565–3575, `check=True`. Requires a working `php` on PATH; reads `build/{site}.html`, writes `build/{site}-inline.html`. This runs on every rendered site.
- **File reads (beyond build/):** `header-image.png` (853), `fqdns.json` (1195), `email_template.html` (3550), `email_template.txt` (3559), `inline-styles.php` (via subprocess), `[News].folder`/*.toml glob (868), and the sqlite `database.db`.
- **File writes:** all under `build/` — `{site}.html` (3556), `{site}.txt` (3562), `{site}-inline.html` (3570 via php), `{site}-inline2.html` (3587), `{site}.eml` (3635). Plus, **only if `--all`**, `{ymd}-notices.csv` and `{ymd}-results.json` at repo root (3662/3666). Avoid `--all` to keep writes confined to `build/`.
- **DB:** engine at 841 (`sqlite:///{name}`, `echo` on if verbose≥2). Only table touched on the report path is **`PantheonTraffic`** (model at 97): query at 1084 (preload) and 1156 (`results`). `PantheonOverageProtection` (120) is only in commented-out code (2975).
  - **An empty `PantheonTraffic` table renders fine.** `results` (1156) may be `[]`. The render builds `visits_by_month` by initializing **every month in range to 0** (2540–2547 `while` loop) *before* `for row in results` (2548), so `visits` is always non-empty and `max(visits)` (2644), `ymax` (2650), and the plan-recommendation math (3009–3198, all driven by `visits_by_month` zeros) do not divide-by-zero or `max([])`. With zero traffic there is simply no overage and the recommended plan stays equal to the current plan. **Minimum seeding: none required for a crash-free render**; seed a few `PantheonTraffic` rows (site_id = the site's `id`, `traffic_date` within `[start_date, end_date]`) only if you want a non-trivial chart/recommendation in the golden output.

## 5. Early-exit branches in the per-site loop (avoid these for the golden run)

- **1043–1048** `if "live" not in envs or "initialized" not in envs["live"]:` → `sys.exit("Bailing out.")` (hard stop, not skip). Fixture must include a `live` env.
- **947** `continue` — UMich enabled + `site["name"] not in portal sites`. (N/A when UMich disabled.)
- **955** `if not sc.options.all and site["name"] not in sc.options.sites: … continue` — pass the site name explicitly (or `--all`).
- **987–989** `if site["plan_name"] == "Sandbox": … continue`. Avoid `plan_name == "Sandbox"`.
- **~1026–1031** `if site["plan_name"] not in plan_names: … sys.exit("Bailing out.")` (unknown plan → hard stop). `plan_name` must be a key of `[Pantheon].plan_info`.
- Elite: 967–981 does **not** skip, but `sys.exit`s if the plan SKU is missing/unknown (974/980). Simplest to use a non-Elite plan like `"Basic"` so `plan:info` is never called.
- **1097** `continue` — inner metrics loop (skips today's partial datum); benign.
- **1111–1148** `if sc.options.import_older_metrics: … continue` — the `--import-older-metrics` path skips the report. Do **not** pass it.
- **1150–1152** `if sc.options.update: … continue` ("site visitors updated, skipping report"). Do **not** pass `--update`.
- **1216–1217** `if domain["type"] == "platform": continue` — inner domain loop (this is your DNS-avoidance lever, §2).
- **2534–2537** `if sc.options.only_warn: … continue` — `--only-warn` short-circuits before chart/email rendering. Do **not** pass `--only-warn`.
- Note **frozen** (997): appends an alert notice but does **not** skip — a frozen site still renders. Not an early-exit.

**Golden-run recipe:** invoke with the single site name (no `--all`, no `--update`/`--import-older-metrics`/`--only-warn`); UMich/Cloudflare/AWS disabled; framework `"wordpress"`, plan `"Basic"` (or any non-Sandbox/non-Elite plan in `plan_info`), `frozen: false`, a `live` env with `initialized: true`; fake `terminus domain:list` returning only `platform` entries (or `{}`) to skip DNS; a fresh `fqdns.json`; `php` present on PATH.
```

## Assistant

Complete operational map in hand, and two things just landed: **Chromium install finished (exit 0)** and the user's note that **Terminus now works through PHP 8.5** and they've **removed the outdated PHP-8.4 warning from README.md**. Good — that removes the one toolchain risk, and I'll re-read README before editing it so I don't reintroduce anything.

Key design levers from the map: `minimal.toml` needs only `[Pantheon]`/`[Database]`/`[News]` sections (plugin sections are KeyError-safe when absent); DNS is avoided by making the fake `domain:list` return only platform entries; ~10 distinct Terminus calls per WordPress site; empty traffic renders fine. Best path for accurate fixtures is record-and-replay. Let me read the sample config to get the exact `plan_info` schema before authoring config fixtures.

### ⚙ Tool call: `Read`

### ⚙ Tool call: `Write`

```json
{
  "file_path": "/workspace/tests/shims/terminus",
  "content": "#!/usr/bin/env python3\n\"\"\"Fake `terminus` for the test harness — record and replay modes.\n\nEvery Pantheon/WP/Drush interaction in the program funnels through the real\n`terminus` binary (WP and Drush are dispatched as `terminus wp …` / `terminus\ndrush …`).  This shim stands in for that binary on PATH so end-to-end tests run\nthe *real* subprocess/argument-building path with deterministic, offline data.\n\nModes (via env var TERMINUS_SHIM_MODE):\n  replay (default) — look the invocation up in TERMINUS_SHIM_DIR and print the\n                     recorded stdout/stderr, exiting with the recorded code.\n                     A missing fixture is a LOUD failure (exit 3 + stderr), never\n                     a silent empty response.\n  record          — run the real terminus (TERMINUS_SHIM_REAL, default\n                    /usr/local/bin/terminus), tee its output, and save the\n                    invocation as a fixture keyed by the argv.\n\nFixtures are keyed by a hash of the argv with the ANSI/interaction flags stripped\n(they never affect the response).  See tests/README.md.\n\"\"\"\nimport datetime\nimport hashlib\nimport json\nimport os\nimport subprocess\nimport sys\n\n# --format flags and the always-present no-ansi/no-interaction flags do not change\n# WHICH data a command returns, only its presentation, so they are excluded from\n# the key.  Everything else (verbs, site/env ids, --fields, eval code) is kept.\n_IGNORED_FLAGS = {\"--no-ansi\", \"--no-interaction\"}\n\n\ndef _key_args(argv):\n    return [a for a in argv if a not in _IGNORED_FLAGS]\n\n\ndef _key(argv):\n    payload = json.dumps(_key_args(argv), ensure_ascii=False)\n    return hashlib.sha1(payload.encode(\"utf-8\")).hexdigest()[:16]\n\n\ndef main():\n    argv = sys.argv[1:]\n    fixture_dir = os.environ.get(\"TERMINUS_SHIM_DIR\")\n    if not fixture_dir:\n        sys.stderr.write(\"terminus-shim: TERMINUS_SHIM_DIR is not set\\n\")\n        return 2\n    mode = os.environ.get(\"TERMINUS_SHIM_MODE\", \"replay\")\n    path = os.path.join(fixture_dir, _key(argv) + \".json\")\n\n    if mode == \"record\":\n        real = os.environ.get(\"TERMINUS_SHIM_REAL\", \"/usr/local/bin/terminus\")\n        proc = subprocess.run([real, *argv], capture_output=True, text=True)\n        record = {\n            \"argv\": _key_args(argv),\n            \"full_argv\": argv,\n            \"returncode\": proc.returncode,\n            \"stdout\": proc.stdout,\n            \"stderr\": proc.stderr,\n            \"recorded\": datetime.date.today().isoformat(),\n        }\n        os.makedirs(fixture_dir, exist_ok=True)\n        with open(path, \"w\", encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n            json.dump(record, f, indent=2, ensure_ascii=False)\n            f.write(\"\\n\")\n        sys.stdout.write(proc.stdout)\n        sys.stderr.write(proc.stderr)\n        return proc.returncode\n\n    # replay\n    if not os.path.exists(path):\n        sys.stderr.write(\n            \"terminus-shim: no fixture for: \"\n            + json.dumps(_key_args(argv), ensure_ascii=False)\n            + f\" (key {_key(argv)})\\n\"\n        )\n        return 3\n    with open(path, encoding=\"utf-8\") as f:\n        record = json.load(f)\n    sys.stdout.write(record.get(\"stdout\", \"\"))\n    sys.stderr.write(record.get(\"stderr\", \"\"))\n    return int(record.get(\"returncode\", 0))\n\n\nif __name__ == \"__main__\":\n    sys.exit(main())\n"
}
```

## Assistant

Now the core `conftest.py` — module loader (with `MPLBACKEND=Agg` set before import), `sc`-state reset, temp DB, the isolated e2e workdir, the `run_program` interlock, and the `--llm` reporter.

### ⚙ Tool call: `Write`

```json
{
  "file_path": "/workspace/tests/conftest.py",
  "content": "\"\"\"Shared fixtures and the safety interlock for the pantheon-sitehealth-emails harness.\n\nSee development/2026-07-04-test-harness/SPEC.md and tests/README.md for the design.\n\nKey facts this file encodes:\n  * The program under test is an extension-less file, so it is loaded via importlib +\n    SourceFileLoader, once, cached in a session-scoped fixture (avoids re-registering\n    the SQLAlchemy models).\n  * matplotlib.pyplot is imported at the top of that module, so MPLBACKEND must be set\n    to \"Agg\" in the environment BEFORE the load — done here at conftest import time.\n  * script_context (`sc`) holds process-global mutable state; the reset_sc autouse\n    fixture restores it (deep-copied) between tests.\n  * run_program() is the ONLY sanctioned way to invoke the program in a subprocess; it\n    raises ForbiddenFlagError before exec if --all/-a/--for-real appear (constraints C1/C2).\n\"\"\"\nimport copy\nimport importlib.util\nimport os\nimport shutil\nimport subprocess\nimport sys\nfrom importlib.machinery import SourceFileLoader\nfrom pathlib import Path\n\nimport pytest\n\n# ── Determinism: pin the matplotlib backend before the target module (which imports\n# matplotlib.pyplot at its top) is ever loaded. ──────────────────────────────────────\nos.environ.setdefault(\"MPLBACKEND\", \"Agg\")\n\nREPO_ROOT = Path(__file__).resolve().parent.parent\nPROGRAM = REPO_ROOT / \"pantheon-sitehealth-emails\"\nTESTS_DIR = REPO_ROOT / \"tests\"\nSHIM_DIR = TESTS_DIR / \"shims\"\nFIXTURES = TESTS_DIR / \"fixtures\"\nCONFIG_DIR = FIXTURES / \"config\"\nTERMINUS_FIXTURES = FIXTURES / \"terminus\"\nREAL_TERMINUS = os.environ.get(\"TERMINUS_SHIM_REAL\", \"/usr/local/bin/terminus\")\n\n# Static assets the program reads relative to its CWD; symlinked into an isolated\n# working directory so e2e runs never touch the repo's real build/, news/, database.db.\n_CWD_ASSETS = (\n    \"email_template.html\",\n    \"email_template.txt\",\n    \"header-image.png\",\n    \"inline-styles.php\",  # PHP resolves vendor/ via realpath __DIR__, so no vendor symlink needed\n)\n\n# Flags that must never reach the real program (see SPEC §2, constraints C1/C2).\nFORBIDDEN_FLAGS = {\"--all\", \"-a\", \"--for-real\"}\n\n\nclass ForbiddenFlagError(RuntimeError):\n    \"\"\"Raised by run_program() when a test tries to pass --all/-a/--for-real.\"\"\"\n\n\nclass FixtureNotFoundError(FileNotFoundError):\n    \"\"\"Raised when a required committed fixture is missing.\"\"\"\n\n\n# ── The program-under-test, loaded once ─────────────────────────────────────────────\n_main_module = None\n\n\ndef _load_main_module():\n    global _main_module\n    if _main_module is None:\n        loader = SourceFileLoader(\"psh_main\", str(PROGRAM))\n        spec = importlib.util.spec_from_loader(\"psh_main\", loader)\n        module = importlib.util.module_from_spec(spec)\n        loader.exec_module(module)\n        _main_module = module\n    return _main_module\n\n\n@pytest.fixture(scope=\"session\")\ndef psh():\n    \"\"\"The loaded program module. Import has no argv side effects after the seam refactor.\"\"\"\n    return _load_main_module()\n\n\n# ── Global-state isolation ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n_SC_ATTRS = (\n    \"options\",\n    \"config\",\n    \"news\",\n    \"hooks\",\n    \"substitutions\",\n    \"plugin\",\n    \"check\",\n    \"plugin_context\",\n)\n\n\n@pytest.fixture(autouse=True)\ndef reset_sc(psh):\n    \"\"\"Restore script_context's mutable globals (deep-copied) around every test.\n\n    `sc.hooks` is a dict-of-lists and add_hook/add_notice/add_news_item mutate the\n    nested lists in place, so a shallow snapshot would leak between tests.\n    \"\"\"\n    import script_context as sc\n\n    saved = {name: copy.deepcopy(getattr(sc, name)) for name in _SC_ATTRS}\n    # Start each test from a clean slate.  sc.options must expose .verbose (many helpers\n    # call sc.debug() -> sc.options.verbose), so use a real parsed default namespace.\n    sc.options = psh.parse_args([])\n    sc.config = {}\n    sc.news = []\n    sc.hooks = {\"setup\": [], \"check\": []}\n    sc.substitutions = []\n    sc.plugin = {}\n    sc.check = {}\n    sc.plugin_context = {}\n    try:\n        yield sc\n    finally:\n        for name, value in saved.items():\n            setattr(sc, name, value)\n\n\n# ── Config loading ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\ndef load_config_file(path):\n    import tomllib\n\n    with open(path, \"rb\") as f:\n        return tomllib.load(f)\n\n\n@pytest.fixture\ndef minimal_config():\n    \"\"\"Parsed minimal.toml (all plugins disabled).\"\"\"\n    return load_config_file(CONFIG_DIR / \"minimal.toml\")\n\n\n# ── In-process DB (temp sqlite) ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────\nclass TempDB:\n    def __init__(self, psh, path):\n        self.path = path\n        self.engine = psh.db.create_engine(f\"sqlite:///{path}\")\n        psh.Base.metadata.create_all(self.engine)\n        self.Session = psh.db.orm.sessionmaker(bind=self.engine)\n        self.PantheonTraffic = psh.PantheonTraffic\n        self.PantheonOverageProtection = psh.PantheonOverageProtection\n\n    def session(self):\n        return self.Session()\n\n\n@pytest.fixture\ndef temp_db(psh, tmp_path):\n    \"\"\"A temporary sqlite DB with the program's schema created; no repo DB is touched.\"\"\"\n    db = TempDB(psh, tmp_path / \"test.db\")\n    yield db\n    db.engine.dispose()\n\n\n# ── Isolated working directory for subprocess (e2e) runs ────────────────────────────\n@pytest.fixture\ndef program_workdir(tmp_path):\n    \"\"\"A temp CWD wired with the repo's static assets, an empty news/ dir, and a\n    neutral fqdns.json, so a subprocess run of the program writes only under this dir.\"\"\"\n    work = tmp_path / \"work\"\n    work.mkdir()\n    for asset in _CWD_ASSETS:\n        src = REPO_ROOT / asset\n        if not src.exists():\n            raise FixtureNotFoundError(f\"expected repo asset missing: {src}\")\n        (work / asset).symlink_to(src)\n    (work / \"news\").mkdir()\n    # No proxied FQDNs -> the DNS/FQDN loop finds nothing to resolve (offline-safe).\n    (work / \"fqdns.json\").write_text(\"{}\\n\")\n    return work\n\n\n# ── The one sanctioned way to run the program ───────────────────────────────────────\ndef _assert_flags_allowed(args):\n    for arg in args:\n        if arg in FORBIDDEN_FLAGS:\n            raise ForbiddenFlagError(\n                f\"refusing to run the program with forbidden flag {arg!r} \"\n                \"(constraints C1/C2: never --all/-a/--for-real)\"\n            )\n\n\ndef run_program(args, *, cwd, mode=\"replay\", extra_env=None, timeout=300):\n    \"\"\"Run ./pantheon-sitehealth-emails as a subprocess through the terminus shim.\n\n    Raises ForbiddenFlagError (before exec) if args contain --all/-a/--for-real.\n    Returns a subprocess.CompletedProcess.\n    \"\"\"\n    args = [str(a) for a in args]\n    _assert_flags_allowed(args)\n\n    env = dict(os.environ)\n    env[\"PATH\"] = f\"{SHIM_DIR}{os.pathsep}{env.get('PATH', '')}\"\n    env[\"TERMINUS_SHIM_DIR\"] = str(TERMINUS_FIXTURES)\n    env[\"TERMINUS_SHIM_MODE\"] = mode\n    env[\"TERMINUS_SHIM_REAL\"] = REAL_TERMINUS\n    env[\"MPLBACKEND\"] = \"Agg\"\n    if extra_env:\n        env.update(extra_env)\n\n    return subprocess.run(\n        [str(PROGRAM), *args],\n        cwd=str(cwd),\n        env=env,\n single entry point).\"\"\"\n    return run_program\n\n\n# ── --llm reporting: terse, machine-parseable summary ──────────────────────────────\ndef pytest_addoption(parser):\n    parser.addoption(\n        \"--llm\",\n        action=\"store_true\",\n        default=False,\n        help=\"emit a terse, machine-parseable summary line for LLM consumption\",\n    )\n\n\ndef pytest_terminal_summary(terminalreporter, exitstatus, config):\n    if not config.getoption(\"--llm\"):\n        return\n    stats = terminalreporter.stats\n\n    def count(key):\n        return len(stats.get(key, []))\n\n    terminalreporter.write_line(\n        \"LLM_SUMMARY \"\n        f\"passed={count('passed')} failed={count('failed')} error={count('error')} \"\n        f\"skipped={count('skipped')} xfailed={count('xfailed')} xpassed={count('xpassed')}\"\n    )\n    for rep in stats.get(\"failed\", []) + stats.get(\"error\", []):\n        terminalreporter.write_line(f\"FAILED {rep.nodeid}\")\n"

### ⚙ Tool call: `Bash`

```json

## Assistant

Confirmed bug: line 3396 references `contacts` before assignment in the non-UMich branch (`recipients` is set on 3393, but `contacts` never is). This path runs for **any institution without UMich enabled** — i.e. exactly the reusable path the project is built around — so production never hit it. It blocks the entire offline render pipeline.

This is a **third** bug beyond the two in the spec. Per your "fix bugs immediately with tests" directive, and since it blocks the harness deliverable, I'll fix it — `contacts` should derive from `recipients` (comma-stripped, since it's later written into a CSV field):

### ⚙ Tool call: `Edit`

## Assistant

Line 3485 is a deliberate U-M-specific hack (`# TODO: remove this section in August 2027`) wrapped in `if True:` — it accesses `sc.config["UMich"]` **unconditionally**, so it breaks every non-U-M render (and blocks offline testing). The project's own goal is "keep U-M-only logic behind config flags," so guarding this block by the UMich-enabled flag is both the correct fix and behavior-preserving for U-M. This is the offline (non-UMich) render path, which production never exercises.

### ⚙ Tool call: `Edit`

domain:list -> platform domain only (offline-safe replay)\n    fn, d = _find([\"domain:list\"])\n    dl = json.loads(d[\"stdout\"])\n    plat = {k: v for k, v in dl.items() if v.get(\"type\") == \"platform\"}\n    if not plat:\n        raise SystemExit(\"record: no platform domain in domain:list\")\n    d[\"stdout\"] = json.dumps(plat)\n    d[\"_scrubbed\"] = \"custom domains removed so replay makes no live DNS calls\"\n    _rewrite(fn, d)\n\n    # 234	def run_terminus(command: list, input_data=None) -> (str, str, bool):
235	
236	    command = ["terminus", "--no-ansi", "--no-interaction", *command]
237	    commandline = " ".join(
238	        [

240	            for arg in command

### ↳ Tool result

```
401	
402	def fix_drush_output(output: str, errors: str) -> (str, str):
403	    """
404	    Move any error messages at the start of the output from a Drush command to the errors string.
405	    """
406	    if not isinstance(output, str) or output == "":
407	        return output, errors
408	
409	    if output[0] != "{":
410	        lines = output.split("\n")
411	        linenum = 0
412	        while linenum < len(lines):
413	            if lines[linenum] and lines[linenum][0] == "{":
414	                break
415	            linenum += 1
416	        errors = "\n".join(lines[:linenum]) + errors
417	        output = "\n".join(lines[linenum:])
418	
419	    sc.debug("Drush output:\n", output, "\nDrush errors:\n", errors, level=2)
420	
421	    return output, errors
422	
423	
424	def drush(siteenv: str, *args) -> (Any, str):
425	    """
426	    Run a "drush" command through Terminus and return the result as a JSON object.
427	    """
428	    command = ["drush", siteenv, "--", *args, "--format=json"]
429	    output, errors, fatal = run_terminus(command)
430	    output, errors = fix_drush_output(output, errors)
```

Let me rewrite the render test to launch Chromium directly with that guard.

### ⚙ Tool call: `Write`

```json
{
  "file_path": "/workspace/tests/render/test_render.py",
  "content": "\"\"\"Render tier: load the report HTML in a headless browser and check it renders (SPEC §9).\n\nThe report's images are attached by Content-ID (cid:), which a standalone browser can't\nresolve, so we extract them from the .eml, write them locally, rewrite the cid: refs, then\nload the page and assert the DOM structure and that the banner image actually resolves.\n\nIf Chromium can't launch (its browser binary or system libraries aren't installed), the\ntest SKIPS with the exact setup command rather than erroring — the render logic is fine,\nthe environment just needs a one-time provisioning step.\n\"\"\"\nimport email\nimport re\n\nimport pytest\n\npytestmark = pytest.mark.render\n\n_CID_REF = re.compile(r\"cid:([^\\\"'\\s>]+)\")\n_SETUP_HINT = \"one-time setup: python -m playwright install --with-deps chromium\"\n\n\ndef _rewrite_cids_to_local(rendered_report, dest_dir):\n    \"\"\"Extract inline images from the .eml and rewrite the HTML's cid: refs to file URIs.\"\"\"\n    msg = email.message_from_bytes(rendered_report[\"eml\"].read_bytes())\n    cid_to_uri = {}\n    for part in msg.walk():\n        cid = part.get(\"Content-ID\")\n        if cid and part.get_content_maintype() == \"image\":\n            key = cid.strip(\"<>\")\n            out = dest_dir / f\"{key}.{part.get_content_subtype()}\"\n            out.write_bytes(part.get_payload(decode=True))\n            cid_to_uri[key] = out.as_uri()\n    html = rendered_report[\"html\"].read_text()\n    html = _CID_REF.sub(lambda m: cid_to_uri.get(m.group(1), m.group(0)), html)\n    page_file = dest_dir / \"render.html\"\n    page_file.write_text(html)\n    return page_file\n\n\ndef test_report_renders_in_browser(rendered_report, tmp_path):\n    from playwright.sync_api import sync_playwright\n\n    page_file = _rewrite_cids_to_local(rendered_report, tmp_path)\n\n    pw = sync_playwright().start()\n    try:\n        try:\n            browser = pw.chromium.launch()\n        except Exception as exc:  # noqa: BLE001 - environment provisioning, not a test failure\n            pytest.skip(f\"Chromium can't launch ({type(exc).__name__}); {_SETUP_HINT}\")\n        try:\n            page = browser.new_page()\n            page.goto(page_file.as_uri())\n            assert \"Pantheon Traffic Report\" in page.title()\n            assert page.locator(\"img.banner_image\").count() == 1\n            # The banner image resolved to real pixels (cid rewrite worked, asset loaded).\n            banner_width = page.eval_on_selector(\"img.banner_image\", \"el => el.naturalWidth\")\n            assert banner_width and banner_width > 0\n        finally:\n            browser.close()\n    finally:\n        pw.stop()\n"
}

2	
3	Send emails to website owners letting them know what their Pantheon traffic has been and make recommendations about whether/how they should change their current plan or the configuration of their site.
4	
5	This script is a temporary, standalone way to send reports to website owners via email.  The University of Michigan intends to eventually integrate this script into the ITS Web Hosting Services portal; this will make the reports available to website owners via the web on a daily basis, in addition to scheduled email reports.
6	
7	Code contributions are gratefully accepted!
8	
9	
10	## Installation
11	
12	Works with Python 3.13 and 3.12.  It should work with Python 3.11 but that has not been tested.  It will not work with Python 3.10 or earlier versions.
13	
14	Running `brew install python@3.12` should work for macOS users.
15	
16	Other requirements:
17	* PHP and Composer for the [Emogrifier CSS processor](https://packagist.org/packages/pelago/emogrifier). Any recent versions of PHP and Composer should work.
18	    ```
19	    brew unlink php
20	    brew install php@8.4
21	    brew link php@8.4
22	    ```
23	* MySQL client if you will use this script with a MySQL database instead of the default SQLite3 database. `pkg-config` is needed by `pip` to install the Python package `mysqlclient`.
24	    ```
25	    brew install pkgconf
26	    brew install mysql-client
27	    ```
28	    *  University of Michigan users: our web hosting services portal database requires MySQL 8 (versions 5.x and 9.x will not work):
29	        ```
30	        brew unlink mysql-client
31	        brew install mysql-client@8.4
32	        brew link mysql-client@8.4
33	        ```
34	* AWS CLI if you are using AWS resources with the script (for example, RDS databases or secrets)
35	    * `brew install awscli` should work for macOS users
36	    * Either run `aws configure --profile webhosting` or set the `AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID` and `AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY` environment variables.
37	
38	Install `uv` by running `brew install uv` or see https://docs.astral.sh/uv/getting-started/installation/
39	
40	```bash
41	git clone git@github.com:its-webhosting/pantheon-sitehealth-emails.git
42	cd pantheon-sitehealth-emails
43	
44	uv self update
45	uv python install --managed-python 3.13
46	uv python upgrade --managed-python 3.13 # in case it was already installed by another project, but out of date
47	uv venv --managed-python --python 3.13 --allow-existing
48	source .venv/bin/activate
49	
50	which python  # make sure it's under .venv/
51	python -V     # make sure it's the version you expect
52	
53	uv pip install .[mysql,aws,cloudflare]  # remove from the list the features you won't use
54	
55	composer install  # the CSS processor pantheon-sitehealth-emails needs is written in PHP
56	```
57	
58	### AWS credentials
59	
60	If you don't already have them, [create AWS credentials for the script](docs/aws-credentials.md) to use that are restricted to only what the script actually needs to do.
61	
62	### Config file
63	
64	Get a copy of your institution's `pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml` file and put it in the same directory as the script.  If your institution does not have one, then follow the steps in the section [One-time per-institution setup](#one-time-per-institution-setup) below.  For University of Michigan users,
65	```bash
66	git clone git@github.com:its-webhosting/pantheon-sitehealth-emails-config.git  # private repo
67	ln -s pantheon-sitehealth-emails-config/pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml .
68	```
69	
70	
71	## Usage
72	
73	```bash
74	git pull && \
75	    [ -d pantheon-sitehealth-emails-config ] && \
76	    ( cd pantheon-sitehealth-emails-config ; git pull ) # make sure you have the latest version
77	
78	
79	uv python upgrade --managed-python 3.13  # why each time? fix
80	source .venv/bin/activate  # if needed
81	ssh-add ~/.ssh/keys/pantheon-ecdsa256
82	export AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID=«REDACTED:AWS_ACCESS_KEY_ID»
83	export AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY=«REDACTED:AWS_SECRET_ACCESS_KEY»
84	
85	# export CLOUDFLARE_EMAIL=«REDACTED:CLOUDFLARE_EMAIL»  # set to your email address
86	# read -s -p "Paste your Cloudflare API Key here: " CLOUDFLARE_API_KEY \
87	#     && echo && export CLOUDFLARE_API_KEY
88	
89	# # If ${USER} is not your uniqname, you'll need add the options
90	# # `--smtp-userame YOUR_UNIQNAME` whenever you run the `pantheon-sitehealth-emails` script.
91	# read -s -p "SMTP password for ${USER}: " SMTP_PASSWORD \
92	#     && echo && export SMTP_PASSWORD
93	
94	# # ...or, if using 1Password:
95	# export CLOUDFLARE_EMAIL=«REDACTED:CLOUDFLARE_EMAIL» read "op://Private/ITS Cloudflare/username")
96	# export CLOUDFLARE_API_KEY=«REDACTED:CLOUDFLARE_API_KEY» read "op://Private/ITS Cloudflare/API key")
97	# export SMTP_PASSWORD=«REDACTED:SMTP_PASSWORD» read "op://Private/UMich Kerberos Password/password")
98	```
99	
100	Run `pantheon-sitehealth-emails --help` for usage information.
101	
102	Once per week, run the script manually to update the visitor counts:
103	```
104	./pantheon-sitehealth-emails --update --all
105	```
106	
107	On the first of every month, send the reports:
108	```bash
109	# Make sure one site is correct so we don't bomb ourselves with errors.
110	# Date should be the last day of the previous month.
111	./pantheon-sitehealth-emails --date 20240731 its-wws-test1
112	
113	# Run it for all sites, then check the emails for problems.
114	./pantheon-sitehealth-emails --date 20240731 --all
115	
116	# Run it for real (sends emails to site owners).
117	./pantheon-sitehealth-emails --date 20240731 --all --for-real
118	
119	# In both the webmaster@umich.edu and januside@umich.edu shared
120	# mailboxes, create a new label "Sent Pantheon traffic reports/${TODAYS_DATE}
121	# Move all of the bcc:'s of the email from Inbox to this new label.
122	```
123	
124	
125	## One-time per-institution setup
126	
127	```bash
128	cp sample-pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml
129	```
130	
131	Edit `pantheon-sitehealth-emails.toml` and configure it correctly for your Pantheon account and your local environment.
132	
133	### Create database tables
134	
135	#### SQLite3
136	
137	```bash
138	./pantheon-sitehealth-emails --create-tables
139	```
140	
141	#### MySQL
142	
143	For MySQL, first create the database,
144	
145	```bash
146	mysql -h "${db_host}" -p -u "${db_user}" "${db_name}"
147	```
148	
149	```sql
150	CREATE DATABASE traffic;
151	use traffic;
152	GRANT ALL ON traffic.* TO "${db_user}"@'%';
153	FLUSH PRIVILEGES;
154	quit
155	```
156	
157	Then create the tables,
158	
159	```bash
160	./pantheon-sitehealth-emails --create-tables
161	```
162	
163	### Import data from Pantheon
164	
165	Pantheon keeps daily traffic data for only 28 days; any new daily traffic data will be added to the sitehealth database each time the script runs.
166	
167	But Pantheon also keeps weekly data for 12 weeks, and monthly data for 12 months.  Running the script with the `--import-older-metrics` option will add the average daily traffic for the weekly and monthly periods to the database.
168	
169	Import the older (weekly and monthly) metrics for `--all` sites:
170	
171	```bash
172	./pantheon-sitehealth-emails --import-older-metrics --all
173	```
174
